00002 DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DUMACH ()
00003 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DUMACH
00004 !***PURPOSE  Compute the unit roundoff of the machine.
00005 !***CATEGORY  R1
00006 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (RUMACH-S, DUMACH-D)
00007 !***KEYWORDS  MACHINE CONSTANTS
00008 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00009 !***DESCRIPTION
00010 ! *Usage:
00011 !        DOUBLE PRECISION  A, DUMACH
00012 !        A = DUMACH()
00013 !
00014 ! *Function Return Values:
00015 !     A : the unit roundoff of the machine.
00016 !
00017 ! *Description:
00018 !     The unit roundoff is defined as the smallest positive machine
00019 !     number u such that  1.0 + u .ne. 1.0.  This is computed by DUMACH
00020 !     in a machine-independent manner.
00021 !
00022 !***REFERENCES  (NONE)
00023 !***ROUTINES CALLED  DUMSUM
00024 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYYYMMDD)
00025 !   19930216  DATE WRITTEN
00026 !   19930818  Added SLATEC-format prologue.  (FNF)
00027 !   20030707  Added DUMSUM to force normal storage of COMP.  (ACH)
00028 !***END PROLOGUE  DUMACH
00029 !
00030 DOUBLE PRECISION U, COMP
00031 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DUMACH
00032 U = 1.0D0
00033 10   U = U*0.5D0
00034 CALL DUMSUM(1.0D0, U, COMP)
00035 IF (COMP .NE. 1.0D0) GOTO 10
00036 DUMACH = U*2.0D0
00037 RETURN
00038 !----------------------- End of Function DUMACH ------------------------
00039 END
00040 SUBROUTINE DUMSUM(A,B,C)
00041 !     Routine to force normal storing of A + B, for DUMACH.
00042 DOUBLE PRECISION A, B, C
00043 C = A + B
00044 RETURN
00045 END

00047 SUBROUTINE DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
00048 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DCFODE
00049 !***SUBSIDIARY
00050 !***PURPOSE  Set ODE integrator coefficients.
00051 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SCFODE-S, DCFODE-D)
00052 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00053 !***DESCRIPTION
00054 !
00055 !  DCFODE is called by the integrator routine to set coefficients
00056 !  needed there.  The coefficients for the current method, as
00057 !  given by the value of METH, are set for all orders and saved.
00058 !  The maximum order assumed here is 12 if METH = 1 and 5 if METH = 2.
00059 !  (A smaller value of the maximum order is also allowed.)
00060 !  DCFODE is called once at the beginning of the problem,
00061 !  and is not called again unless and until METH is changed.
00062 !
00063 !  The ELCO array contains the basic method coefficients.
00064 !  The coefficients el(i), 1 .le. i .le. nq+1, for the method of
00065 !  order nq are stored in ELCO(i,nq).  They are given by a genetrating
00066 !  polynomial, i.e.,
00067 !      l(x) = el(1) + el(2)*x + ... + el(nq+1)*x**nq.
00068 !  For the implicit Adams methods, l(x) is given by
00069 !      dl/dx = (x+1)*(x+2)*...*(x+nq-1)/factorial(nq-1),    l(-1) = 0.
00070 !  For the BDF methods, l(x) is given by
00071 !      l(x) = (x+1)*(x+2)* ... *(x+nq)/K,
00072 !  where         K = factorial(nq)*(1 + 1/2 + ... + 1/nq).
00073 !
00074 !  The TESCO array contains test constants used for the
00075 !  local error test and the selection of step size and/or order.
00076 !  At order nq, TESCO(k,nq) is used for the selection of step
00077 !  size at order nq - 1 if k = 1, at order nq if k = 2, and at order
00078 !  nq + 1 if k = 3.
00079 !
00080 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
00081 !***ROUTINES CALLED  (NONE)
00082 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
00083 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
00084 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
00085 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
00086 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
00087 !***END PROLOGUE  DCFODE
00088 !**End
00089 INTEGER METH
00090 INTEGER I, IB, NQ, NQM1, NQP1
00091 DOUBLE PRECISION ELCO, TESCO
00092 DOUBLE PRECISION AGAMQ, FNQ, FNQM1, PC, PINT, RAGQ,RQFAC, RQ1FAC, TSIGN, XPIN
00093 DIMENSION ELCO(13,12), TESCO(3,12)
00094 DIMENSION PC(12)
00095 !
00096 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DCFODE
00097 GOTO (100, 200), METH
00098 !
00099 100  ELCO(1,1) = 1.0D0
00100 ELCO(2,1) = 1.0D0
00101 TESCO(1,1) = 0.0D0
00102 TESCO(2,1) = 2.0D0
00103 TESCO(1,2) = 1.0D0
00104 TESCO(3,12) = 0.0D0
00105 PC(1) = 1.0D0
00106 RQFAC = 1.0D0
00107 DO 140 NQ = 2,12
00108 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00109 ! The PC array will contain the coefficients of the polynomial
00110 !     p(x) = (x+1)*(x+2)*...*(x+nq-1).
00111 ! Initially, p(x) = 1.
00112 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00113 RQ1FAC = RQFAC
00114 RQFAC = RQFAC/NQ
00115 NQM1 = NQ - 1
00116 FNQM1 = NQM1
00117 NQP1 = NQ + 1
00118 ! Form coefficients of p(x)*(x+nq-1). ----------------------------------
00119 PC(NQ) = 0.0D0
00120 DO 110 IB = 1,NQM1
00121 I = NQP1 - IB
00122 110      PC(I) = PC(I-1) + FNQM1*PC(I)
00123 PC(1) = FNQM1*PC(1)
00124 ! Compute integral, -1 to 0, of p(x) and x*p(x). -----------------------
00125 PINT = PC(1)
00126 XPIN = PC(1)/2.0D0
00127 TSIGN = 1.0D0
00128 DO 120 I = 2,NQ
00129 TSIGN = -TSIGN
00130 PINT = PINT + TSIGN*PC(I)/I
00131 120      XPIN = XPIN + TSIGN*PC(I)/(I+1)
00132 ! Store coefficients in ELCO and TESCO. --------------------------------
00133 ELCO(1,NQ) = PINT*RQ1FAC
00134 ELCO(2,NQ) = 1.0D0
00135 DO 130 I = 2,NQ
00136 130      ELCO(I+1,NQ) = RQ1FAC*PC(I)/I
00137 AGAMQ = RQFAC*XPIN
00138 RAGQ = 1.0D0/AGAMQ
00139 TESCO(2,NQ) = RAGQ
00140 IF (NQ .LT. 12) TESCO(1,NQP1) = RAGQ*RQFAC/NQP1
00141 TESCO(3,NQM1) = RAGQ
00142 140    CONTINUE
00143 RETURN
00144 !
00145 200  PC(1) = 1.0D0
00146 RQ1FAC = 1.0D0
00147 DO 230 NQ = 1,5
00148 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00149 ! The PC array will contain the coefficients of the polynomial
00150 !     p(x) = (x+1)*(x+2)*...*(x+nq).
00151 ! Initially, p(x) = 1.
00152 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00153 FNQ = NQ
00154 NQP1 = NQ + 1
00155 ! Form coefficients of p(x)*(x+nq). ------------------------------------
00156 PC(NQP1) = 0.0D0
00157 DO 210 IB = 1,NQ
00158 I = NQ + 2 - IB
00159 210      PC(I) = PC(I-1) + FNQ*PC(I)
00160 PC(1) = FNQ*PC(1)
00161 ! Store coefficients in ELCO and TESCO. --------------------------------
00162 DO 220 I = 1,NQP1
00163 220      ELCO(I,NQ) = PC(I)/PC(2)
00164 ELCO(2,NQ) = 1.0D0
00165 TESCO(1,NQ) = RQ1FAC
00166 TESCO(2,NQ) = NQP1/ELCO(1,NQ)
00167 TESCO(3,NQ) = (NQ+2)/ELCO(1,NQ)
00168 RQ1FAC = RQ1FAC/FNQ
00169 230    CONTINUE
00170 RETURN
00171 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DCFODE ----------------------
00172 END
00173 
00174 SUBROUTINE DINTDY (T, K, YH, NYH, DKY, IFLAG)
00175 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DINTDY
00176 !***SUBSIDIARY
00177 !***PURPOSE  Interpolate solution derivatives.
00178 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SINTDY-S, DINTDY-D)
00179 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00180 !***DESCRIPTION
00181 !
00182 !  DINTDY computes interpolated values of the K-th derivative of the
00183 !  dependent variable vector y, and stores it in DKY.  This routine
00184 !  is called within the package with K = 0 and T = TOUT, but may
00185 !  also be called by the user for any K up to the current order.
00186 !  (See detailed instructions in the usage documentation.)
00187 !
00188 !  The computed values in DKY are gotten by interpolation using the
00189 !  Nordsieck history array YH.  This array corresponds uniquely to a
00190 !  vector-valued polynomial of degree NQCUR or less, and DKY is set
00191 !  to the K-th derivative of this polynomial at T.
00192 !  The formula for DKY is:
00193 !               q
00194 !   DKY(i)  =  sum  c(j,K) * (T - tn)**(j-K) * h**(-j) * YH(i,j+1)
00195 !              j=K
00196 !  where  c(j,K) = j*(j-1)*...*(j-K+1), q = NQCUR, tn = TCUR, h = HCUR.
00197 !  The quantities  nq = NQCUR, l = nq+1, N = NEQ, tn, and h are
00198 !  communicated by COMMON.  The above sum is done in reverse order.
00199 !  IFLAG is returned negative if either K or T is out of bounds.
00200 !
00201 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
00202 !***ROUTINES CALLED  XERRWD
00203 !***COMMON BLOCKS    DLS001
00204 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
00205 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
00206 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
00207 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
00208 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
00209 !   010418  Reduced size of Common block /DLS001/. (ACH)
00210 !   031105  Restored 'own' variables to Common block /DLS001/, to
00211 !           enable interrupt/restart feature. (ACH)
00212 !   050427  Corrected roundoff decrement in TP. (ACH)
00213 !***END PROLOGUE  DINTDY
00214 !**End
00215 INTEGER K, NYH, IFLAG
00216 DOUBLE PRECISION T, YH, DKY
00217 DIMENSION YH(NYH,*), DKY(*)
00218 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF
00219 INTEGER LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00220 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS,CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
00221 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6),&
00222 ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER,&
00223 MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00224 INTEGER I, IC, J, JB, JB2, JJ, JJ1, JP1
00225 DOUBLE PRECISION C, R, S, TP
00226 CHARACTER*80 MSG
00227 !
00228 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DINTDY
00229 IFLAG = 0
00230 IF (K .LT. 0 .OR. K .GT. NQ) GOTO 80
00231 TP = TN - HU -  100.0D0*UROUND*SIGN(ABS(TN) + ABS(HU), HU)
00232 IF ((T-TP)*(T-TN) .GT. 0.0D0) GOTO 90
00233 !
00234 S = (T - TN)/H
00235 IC = 1
00236 IF (K .EQ. 0) GOTO 15
00237 JJ1 = L - K
00238 DO 10 JJ = JJ1,NQ
00239 10     IC = IC*JJ
00240 15   C = IC
00241 DO 20 I = 1,N
00242 20     DKY(I) = C*YH(I,L)
00243 IF (K .EQ. NQ) GOTO 55
00244 JB2 = NQ - K
00245 DO 50 JB = 1,JB2
00246 J = NQ - JB
00247 JP1 = J + 1
00248 IC = 1
00249 IF (K .EQ. 0) GOTO 35
00250 JJ1 = JP1 - K
00251 DO 30 JJ = JJ1,J
00252 30       IC = IC*JJ
00253 35     C = IC
00254 DO 40 I = 1,N
00255 40       DKY(I) = C*YH(I,JP1) + S*DKY(I)
00256 50     CONTINUE
00257 IF (K .EQ. 0) RETURN
00258 55   R = H**(-K)
00259 DO 60 I = 1,N
00260 60     DKY(I) = R*DKY(I)
00261 RETURN
00262 !
00263 80   MSG = 'DINTDY-  K (=I1) illegal      '
00264 CALL XERRWD (MSG, 30, 51, 0, 1, K, 0, 0, 0.0D0, 0.0D0)
00265 IFLAG = -1
00266 RETURN
00267 90   MSG = 'DINTDY-  T (=R1) illegal      '
00268 CALL XERRWD (MSG, 30, 52, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1, T, 0.0D0)
00269 MSG='      T not in interval TCUR - HU (= R1) to TCUR (=R2)      '
00270 CALL XERRWD (MSG, 60, 52, 0, 0, 0, 0, 2, TP, TN)
00271 IFLAG = -2
00272 RETURN
00273 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DINTDY ----------------------
00274 END
00275 
00276 SUBROUTINE DPREPJ (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
00277 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DPREPJ
00278 !***SUBSIDIARY
00279 !***PURPOSE  Compute and process Newton iteration matrix.
00280 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SPREPJ-S, DPREPJ-D)
00281 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00282 !***DESCRIPTION
00283 !
00284 !  DPREPJ is called by DSTODE to compute and process the matrix
00285 !  P = I - h*el(1)*J , where J is an approximation to the Jacobian.
00286 !  Here J is computed by the user-supplied routine JAC if
00287 !  MITER = 1 or 4, or by finite differencing if MITER = 2, 3, or 5.
00288 !  If MITER = 3, a diagonal approximation to J is used.
00289 !  J is stored in WM and replaced by P.  If MITER .ne. 3, P is then
00290 !  subjected to LU decomposition in preparation for later solution
00291 !  of linear systems with P as coefficient matrix.  This is done
00292 !  by DGEFA if MITER = 1 or 2, and by DGBFA if MITER = 4 or 5.
00293 !
00294 !  In addition to variables described in DSTODE and DLSODE prologues,
00295 !  communication with DPREPJ uses the following:
00296 !  Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
00297 !  FTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODE).
00298 !  SAVF  = array containing f evaluated at predicted y.
00299 !  WM    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains the
00300 !          inverse diagonal matrix if MITER = 3 and the LU decomposition
00301 !          of P if MITER is 1, 2 , 4, or 5.
00302 !          Storage of matrix elements starts at WM(3).
00303 !          WM also contains the following matrix-related data:
00304 !          WM(1) = SQRT(UROUND), used in numerical Jacobian increments.
00305 !          WM(2) = H*EL0, saved for later use if MITER = 3.
00306 !  IWM   = integer work space containing pivot information, starting at
00307 !          IWM(21), if MITER is 1, 2, 4, or 5.  IWM also contains band
00308 !          parameters ML = IWM(1) and MU = IWM(2) if MITER is 4 or 5.
00309 !  EL0   = EL(1) (input).
00310 !  IERPJ = output error flag,  = 0 if no trouble, .gt. 0 if
00311 !          P matrix found to be singular.
00312 !  JCUR  = output flag = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian matrix
00313 !          (or approximation) is now current.
00314 !  This routine also uses the COMMON variables EL0, H, TN, UROUND,
00315 !  MITER, N, NFE, and NJE.
00316 !
00317 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
00318 !***ROUTINES CALLED  DGBFA, DGEFA, DVNORM
00319 !***COMMON BLOCKS    DLS001
00320 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
00321 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
00322 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
00323 !   890504  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
00324 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
00325 !   010418  Reduced size of Common block /DLS001/. (ACH)
00326 !   031105  Restored 'own' variables to Common block /DLS001/, to
00327 !           enable interrupt/restart feature. (ACH)
00328 !***END PROLOGUE  DPREPJ
00329 !**End
00330 EXTERNAL F, JAC
00331 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
00332 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM
00333 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), EWT(*), FTEM(*), SAVF(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
00334 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR
00335 INTEGER LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00336 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
00337 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6),&
00338 ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER,&
00339 MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00340 INTEGER I, I1, I2, IER, II, J, J1, JJ, LENP, MBA, MBAND, MEB1, MEBAND, ML, ML3, MU, NP1
00341 DOUBLE PRECISION CON, DI, FAC, HL0, R, R0, SRUR, YI, YJ, YJJ, DVNORM
00342 !
00343 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DPREPJ
00344 NJE = NJE + 1
00345 IERPJ = 0
00346 JCUR = 1
00347 HL0 = H*EL0
00348 GOTO (100, 200, 300, 400, 500), MITER
00349 ! If MITER = 1, call JAC and multiply by scalar. -----------------------
00350 100  LENP = N*N
00351 DO 110 I = 1,LENP
00352 110    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
00353 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, 0, 0, WM(3), N)
00354 CON = -HL0
00355 DO 120 I = 1,LENP
00356 120    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
00357 GOTO 240
00358 ! If MITER = 2, make N calls to F to approximate J. --------------------
00359 200  FAC = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)
00360 R0 = 1000.0D0*ABS(H)*UROUND*N*FAC
00361 IF (R0 .EQ. 0.0D0) R0 = 1.0D0
00362 SRUR = WM(1)
00363 J1 = 2
00364 DO 230 J = 1,N
00365 YJ = Y(J)
00366 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YJ),R0/EWT(J))
00367 Y(J) = Y(J) + R
00368 FAC = -HL0/R
00369 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
00370 DO 220 I = 1,N
00371 220      WM(I+J1) = (FTEM(I) - SAVF(I))*FAC
00372 Y(J) = YJ
00373 J1 = J1 + N
00374 230    CONTINUE
00375 NFE = NFE + N
00376 ! Add identity matrix. -------------------------------------------------
00377 240  J = 3
00378 NP1 = N + 1
00379 DO 250 I = 1,N
00380 WM(J) = WM(J) + 1.0D0
00381 250    J = J + NP1
00382 ! Do LU decomposition on P. --------------------------------------------
00383 CALL DGEFA (WM(3), N, N, IWM(21), IER)
00384 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
00385 RETURN
00386 ! If MITER = 3, construct a diagonal approximation to J and P. ---------
00387 300  WM(2) = HL0
00388 R = EL0*0.1D0
00389 DO 310 I = 1,N
00390 310    Y(I) = Y(I) + R*(H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2))
00391 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, WM(3))
00392 NFE = NFE + 1
00393 DO 320 I = 1,N
00394 R0 = H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2)
00395 DI = 0.1D0*R0 - H*(WM(I+2) - SAVF(I))
00396 WM(I+2) = 1.0D0
00397 IF (ABS(R0) .LT. UROUND/EWT(I)) GOTO 320
00398 IF (ABS(DI) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 330
00399 WM(I+2) = 0.1D0*R0/DI
00400 320    CONTINUE
00401 RETURN
00402 330  IERPJ = 1
00403 RETURN
00404 ! If MITER = 4, call JAC and multiply by scalar. -----------------------
00405 400  ML = IWM(1)
00406 MU = IWM(2)
00407 ML3 = ML + 3
00408 MBAND = ML + MU + 1
00409 MEBAND = MBAND + ML
00410 LENP = MEBAND*N
00411 DO 410 I = 1,LENP
00412 410    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
00413 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, ML, MU, WM(ML3), MEBAND)
00414 CON = -HL0
00415 DO 420 I = 1,LENP
00416 420    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
00417 GOTO 570
00418 ! If MITER = 5, make MBAND calls to F to approximate J. ----------------
00419 500  ML = IWM(1)
00420 MU = IWM(2)
00421 MBAND = ML + MU + 1
00422 MBA = MIN(MBAND,N)
00423 MEBAND = MBAND + ML
00424 MEB1 = MEBAND - 1
00425 SRUR = WM(1)
00426 FAC = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)
00427 R0 = 1000.0D0*ABS(H)*UROUND*N*FAC
00428 IF (R0 .EQ. 0.0D0) R0 = 1.0D0
00429 DO 560 J = 1,MBA
00430 DO 530 I = J,N,MBAND
00431 YI = Y(I)
00432 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YI),R0/EWT(I))
00433 530      Y(I) = Y(I) + R
00434 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
00435 DO 550 JJ = J,N,MBAND
00436 Y(JJ) = YH(JJ,1)
00437 YJJ = Y(JJ)
00438 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YJJ),R0/EWT(JJ))
00439 FAC = -HL0/R
00440 I1 = MAX(JJ-MU,1)
00441 I2 = MIN(JJ+ML,N)
00442 II = JJ*MEB1 - ML + 2
00443 DO 540 I = I1,I2
00444 540        WM(II+I) = (FTEM(I) - SAVF(I))*FAC
00445 550      CONTINUE
00446 560    CONTINUE
00447 NFE = NFE + MBA
00448 ! Add identity matrix. -------------------------------------------------
00449 570  II = MBAND + 2
00450 DO 580 I = 1,N
00451 WM(II) = WM(II) + 1.0D0
00452 580    II = II + MEBAND
00453 ! Do LU decomposition of P. --------------------------------------------
00454 CALL DGBFA (WM(3), MEBAND, N, ML, MU, IWM(21), IER)
00455 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
00456 RETURN
00457 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DPREPJ ----------------------
00458 END
00459 
00460 SUBROUTINE DSOLSY (WM, IWM, X, TEM)
00461 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DSOLSY
00462 !***SUBSIDIARY
00463 !***PURPOSE  ODEPACK linear system solver.
00464 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SSOLSY-S, DSOLSY-D)
00465 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00466 !***DESCRIPTION
00467 !
00468 !  This routine manages the solution of the linear system arising from
00469 !  a chord iteration.  It is called if MITER .ne. 0.
00470 !  If MITER is 1 or 2, it calls DGESL to accomplish this.
00471 !  If MITER = 3 it updates the coefficient h*EL0 in the diagonal
00472 !  matrix, and then computes the solution.
00473 !  If MITER is 4 or 5, it calls DGBSL.
00474 !  Communication with DSOLSY uses the following variables:
00475 !  WM    = real work space containing the inverse diagonal matrix if
00476 !          MITER = 3 and the LU decomposition of the matrix otherwise.
00477 !          Storage of matrix elements starts at WM(3).
00478 !          WM also contains the following matrix-related data:
00479 !          WM(1) = SQRT(UROUND) (not used here),
00480 !          WM(2) = HL0, the previous value of h*EL0, used if MITER = 3.
00481 !  IWM   = integer work space containing pivot information, starting at
00482 !          IWM(21), if MITER is 1, 2, 4, or 5.  IWM also contains band
00483 !          parameters ML = IWM(1) and MU = IWM(2) if MITER is 4 or 5.
00484 !  X     = the right-hand side vector on input, and the solution vector
00485 !          on output, of length N.
00486 !  TEM   = vector of work space of length N, not used in this version.
00487 !  IERSL = output flag (in COMMON).  IERSL = 0 if no trouble occurred.
00488 !          IERSL = 1 if a singular matrix arose with MITER = 3.
00489 !  This routine also uses the COMMON variables EL0, H, MITER, and N.
00490 !
00491 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
00492 !***ROUTINES CALLED  DGBSL, DGESL
00493 !***COMMON BLOCKS    DLS001
00494 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
00495 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
00496 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
00497 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
00498 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
00499 !   010418  Reduced size of Common block /DLS001/. (ACH)
00500 !   031105  Restored 'own' variables to Common block /DLS001/, to
00501 !           enable interrupt/restart feature. (ACH)
00502 !***END PROLOGUE  DSOLSY
00503 !**End
00504 INTEGER IWM
00505 DOUBLE PRECISION WM, X, TEM
00506 DIMENSION WM(*), IWM(*), X(*), TEM(*)
00507 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
00508 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00509 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
00510 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
00511 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00512 INTEGER I, MEBAND, ML, MU
00513 DOUBLE PRECISION DI, HL0, PHL0, R
00514 !
00515 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DSOLSY
00516 IERSL = 0
00517 GOTO (100, 100, 300, 400, 400), MITER
00518 100  CALL DGESL (WM(3), N, N, IWM(21), X, 0)
00519 RETURN
00520 !
00521 300  PHL0 = WM(2)
00522 HL0 = H*EL0
00523 WM(2) = HL0
00524 IF (HL0 .EQ. PHL0) GOTO 330
00525 R = HL0/PHL0
00526 DO 320 I = 1,N
00527 DI = 1.0D0 - R*(1.0D0 - 1.0D0/WM(I+2))
00528 IF (ABS(DI) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 390
00529 320    WM(I+2) = 1.0D0/DI
00530 330  DO 340 I = 1,N
00531 340    X(I) = WM(I+2)*X(I)
00532 RETURN
00533 390  IERSL = 1
00534 RETURN
00535 !
00536 400  ML = IWM(1)
00537 MU = IWM(2)
00538 MEBAND = 2*ML + MU + 1
00539 CALL DGBSL (WM(3), MEBAND, N, ML, MU, IWM(21), X, 0)
00540 RETURN
00541 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DSOLSY ----------------------
00542 END
00543 
00544 SUBROUTINE DSRCOM (RSAV, ISAV, JOB)
00545 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DSRCOM
00546 !***SUBSIDIARY
00547 !***PURPOSE  Save/restore ODEPACK COMMON blocks.
00548 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SSRCOM-S, DSRCOM-D)
00549 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00550 !***DESCRIPTION
00551 !
00552 !  This routine saves or restores (depending on JOB) the contents of
00553 !  the COMMON block DLS001, which is used internally
00554 !  by one or more ODEPACK solvers.
00555 !
00556 !  RSAV = real array of length 218 or more.
00557 !  ISAV = integer array of length 37 or more.
00558 !  JOB  = flag indicating to save or restore the COMMON blocks:
00559 !         JOB  = 1 if COMMON is to be saved (written to RSAV/ISAV)
00560 !         JOB  = 2 if COMMON is to be restored (read from RSAV/ISAV)
00561 !         A call with JOB = 2 presumes a prior call with JOB = 1.
00562 !
00563 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
00564 !***ROUTINES CALLED  (NONE)
00565 !***COMMON BLOCKS    DLS001
00566 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
00567 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
00568 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
00569 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
00570 !   921116  Deleted treatment of block /EH0001/.  (ACH)
00571 !   930801  Reduced Common block length by 2.  (ACH)
00572 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
00573 !   010418  Reduced Common block length by 209+12. (ACH)
00574 !   031105  Restored 'own' variables to Common block /DLS001/, to
00575 !           enable interrupt/restart feature. (ACH)
00576 !   031112  Added SAVE statement for data-loaded constants.
00577 !***END PROLOGUE  DSRCOM
00578 !**End
00579 INTEGER ISAV, JOB
00580 INTEGER ILS
00581 INTEGER I, LENILS, LENRLS
00582 DOUBLE PRECISION RSAV,   RLS
00583 DIMENSION RSAV(*), ISAV(*)
00584 SAVE LENRLS, LENILS
00585 COMMON /DLS001/ RLS(218), ILS(37)
00586 DATA LENRLS/218/, LENILS/37/
00587 !
00588 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DSRCOM
00589 IF (JOB .EQ. 2) GOTO 100
00590 !
00591 DO 10 I = 1,LENRLS
00592 10     RSAV(I) = RLS(I)
00593 DO 20 I = 1,LENILS
00594 20     ISAV(I) = ILS(I)
00595 RETURN
00596 !
00597 100  CONTINUE
00598 DO 110 I = 1,LENRLS
00599 110     RLS(I) = RSAV(I)
00600 DO 120 I = 1,LENILS
00601 120     ILS(I) = ISAV(I)
00602 RETURN
00603 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DSRCOM ----------------------
00604 END
00605 
00606 SUBROUTINE DSTODE (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, ACOR, WM, IWM, F, JAC, PJAC, SLVS)
00607 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DSTODE
00608 !***SUBSIDIARY
00609 !***PURPOSE  Performs one step of an ODEPACK integration.
00610 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SSTODE-S, DSTODE-D)
00611 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
00612 !***DESCRIPTION
00613 !
00614 !  DSTODE performs one step of the integration of an initial value
00615 !  problem for a system of ordinary differential equations.
00616 !  Note:  DSTODE is independent of the value of the iteration method
00617 !  indicator MITER, when this is .ne. 0, and hence is independent
00618 !  of the type of chord method used, or the Jacobian structure.
00619 !  Communication with DSTODE is done with the following variables:
00620 !
00621 !  NEQ    = integer array containing problem size in NEQ(1), and
00622 !           passed as the NEQ argument in all calls to F and JAC.
00623 !  Y      = an array of length .ge. N used as the Y argument in
00624 !           all calls to F and JAC.
00625 !  YH     = an NYH by LMAX array containing the dependent variables
00626 !           and their approximate scaled derivatives, where
00627 !           LMAX = MAXORD + 1.  YH(i,j+1) contains the approximate
00628 !           j-th derivative of y(i), scaled by h**j/factorial(j)
00629 !           (j = 0,1,...,NQ).  on entry for the first step, the first
00630 !           two columns of YH must be set from the initial values.
00631 !  NYH    = a constant integer .ge. N, the first dimension of YH.
00632 !  YH1    = a one-dimensional array occupying the same space as YH.
00633 !  EWT    = an array of length N containing multiplicative weights
00634 !           for local error measurements.  Local errors in Y(i) are
00635 !           compared to 1.0/EWT(i) in various error tests.
00636 !  SAVF   = an array of working storage, of length N.
00637 !           Also used for input of YH(*,MAXORD+2) when JSTART = -1
00638 !           and MAXORD .lt. the current order NQ.
00639 !  ACOR   = a work array of length N, used for the accumulated
00640 !           corrections.  On a successful return, ACOR(i) contains
00641 !           the estimated one-step local error in Y(i).
00642 !  WM,IWM = real and integer work arrays associated with matrix
00643 !           operations in chord iteration (MITER .ne. 0).
00644 !  PJAC   = name of routine to evaluate and preprocess Jacobian matrix
00645 !           and P = I - h*el0*JAC, if a chord method is being used.
00646 !  SLVS   = name of routine to solve linear system in chord iteration.
00647 !  CCMAX  = maximum relative change in h*el0 before PJAC is called.
00648 !  H      = the step size to be attempted on the next step.
00649 !           H is altered by the error control algorithm during the
00650 !           problem.  H can be either positive or negative, but its
00651 !           sign must remain constant throughout the problem.
00652 !  HMIN   = the minimum absolute value of the step size h to be used.
00653 !  HMXI   = inverse of the maximum absolute value of h to be used.
00654 !           HMXI = 0.0 is allowed and corresponds to an infinite hmax.
00655 !           HMIN and HMXI may be changed at any time, but will not
00656 !           take effect until the next change of h is considered.
00657 !  TN     = the independent variable. TN is updated on each step taken.
00658 !  JSTART = an integer used for input only, with the following
00659 !           values and meanings:
00660 !                0  perform the first step.
00661 !            .gt.0  take a new step continuing from the last.
00662 !               -1  take the next step with a new value of H, MAXORD,
00663 !                     N, METH, MITER, and/or matrix parameters.
00664 !               -2  take the next step with a new value of H,
00665 !                     but with other inputs unchanged.
00666 !           On return, JSTART is set to 1 to facilitate continuation.
00667 !  KFLAG  = a completion code with the following meanings:
00668 !                0  the step was succesful.
00669 !               -1  the requested error could not be achieved.
00670 !               -2  corrector convergence could not be achieved.
00671 !               -3  fatal error in PJAC or SLVS.
00672 !           A return with KFLAG = -1 or -2 means either
00673 !           abs(H) = HMIN or 10 consecutive failures occurred.
00674 !           On a return with KFLAG negative, the values of TN and
00675 !           the YH array are as of the beginning of the last
00676 !           step, and H is the last step size attempted.
00677 !  MAXORD = the maximum order of integration method to be allowed.
00678 !  MAXCOR = the maximum number of corrector iterations allowed.
00679 !  MSBP   = maximum number of steps between PJAC calls (MITER .gt. 0).
00680 !  MXNCF  = maximum number of convergence failures allowed.
00681 !  METH/MITER = the method flags.  See description in driver.
00682 !  N      = the number of first-order differential equations.
00683 !  The values of CCMAX, H, HMIN, HMXI, TN, JSTART, KFLAG, MAXORD,
00684 !  MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, METH, MITER, and N are communicated via COMMON.
00685 !
00686 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
00687 !***ROUTINES CALLED  DCFODE, DVNORM
00688 !***COMMON BLOCKS    DLS001
00689 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
00690 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
00691 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
00692 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
00693 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
00694 !   010418  Reduced size of Common block /DLS001/. (ACH)
00695 !   031105  Restored 'own' variables to Common block /DLS001/, to
00696 !           enable interrupt/restart feature. (ACH)
00697 !***END PROLOGUE  DSTODE
00698 !**End
00699 EXTERNAL F, JAC, PJAC, SLVS
00700 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
00701 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, ACOR, WM
00702 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), YH1(*), EWT(*), SAVF(*),ACOR(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
00703 INTEGER IOWND, IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L
00704 INTEGER LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00705 INTEGER I, I1, IREDO, IRET, J, JB, M, NCF, NEWQ
00706 DOUBLE PRECISION CONIT, CRATE, EL, ELCO, HOLD, RMAX, TESCO, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
00707 DOUBLE PRECISION DCON, DDN, DEL, DELP, DSM, DUP, EXDN, EXSM, EXUP, R, RH, RHDN, RHSM, RHUP, TOLD, DVNORM
00708 
00709 COMMON /DLS001/ CONIT, CRATE, EL(13), ELCO(13,12), HOLD, RMAX, TESCO(3,12), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, &
00710 IOWND(6), IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, &
00711 LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
00712 
00713 !
00714 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DSTODE
00715 KFLAG = 0
00716 TOLD = TN
00717 NCF = 0
00718 IERPJ = 0
00719 IERSL = 0
00720 JCUR = 0
00721 ICF = 0
00722 DELP = 0.0D0
00723 IF (JSTART .GT. 0) GOTO 200
00724 IF (JSTART .EQ. -1) GOTO 100
00725 IF (JSTART .EQ. -2) GOTO 160
00726 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00727 ! On the first call, the order is set to 1, and other variables are
00728 ! initialized.  RMAX is the maximum ratio by which H can be increased
00729 ! in a single step.  It is initially 1.E4 to compensate for the small
00730 ! initial H, but then is normally equal to 10.  If a failure
00731 ! occurs (in corrector convergence or error test), RMAX is set to 2
00732 ! for the next increase.
00733 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00734 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
00735 NQ = 1
00736 L = 2
00737 IALTH = 2
00738 RMAX = 10000.0D0
00739 RC = 0.0D0
00740 EL0 = 1.0D0
00741 CRATE = 0.7D0
00742 HOLD = H
00743 MEO = METH
00744 NSLP = 0
00745 IPUP = MITER
00746 IRET = 3
00747 GOTO 140
00748 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00749 ! The following block handles preliminaries needed when JSTART = -1.
00750 ! IPUP is set to MITER to force a matrix update.
00751 ! If an order increase is about to be considered (IALTH = 1),
00752 ! IALTH is reset to 2 to postpone consideration one more step.
00753 ! If the caller has changed METH, DCFODE is called to reset
00754 ! the coefficients of the method.
00755 ! If the caller has changed MAXORD to a value less than the current
00756 ! order NQ, NQ is reduced to MAXORD, and a new H chosen accordingly.
00757 ! If H is to be changed, YH must be rescaled.
00758 ! If H or METH is being changed, IALTH is reset to L = NQ + 1
00759 ! to prevent further changes in H for that many steps.
00760 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00761 100  IPUP = MITER
00762 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
00763 IF (IALTH .EQ. 1) IALTH = 2
00764 IF (METH .EQ. MEO) GOTO 110
00765 CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
00766 MEO = METH
00767 IF (NQ .GT. MAXORD) GOTO 120
00768 IALTH = L
00769 IRET = 1
00770 GOTO 150
00771 110  IF (NQ .LE. MAXORD) GOTO 160
00772 120  NQ = MAXORD
00773 L = LMAX
00774 DO 125 I = 1,L
00775 125    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
00776 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
00777 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
00778 EL0 = EL(1)
00779 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
00780 DDN = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(1,L)
00781 EXDN = 1.0D0/L
00782 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
00783 RH = MIN(RHDN,1.0D0)
00784 IREDO = 3
00785 IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 170
00786 RH = MIN(RH,ABS(H/HOLD))
00787 H = HOLD
00788 GOTO 175
00789 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00790 ! DCFODE is called to get all the integration coefficients for the
00791 ! current METH.  Then the EL vector and related constants are reset
00792 ! whenever the order NQ is changed, or at the start of the problem.
00793 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00794 140  CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
00795 150  DO 155 I = 1,L
00796 155    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
00797 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
00798 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
00799 EL0 = EL(1)
00800 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
00801 GOTO (160, 170, 200), IRET
00802 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00803 ! If H is being changed, the H ratio RH is checked against
00804 ! RMAX, HMIN, and HMXI, and the YH array rescaled.  IALTH is set to
00805 ! L = NQ + 1 to prevent a change of H for that many steps, unless
00806 ! forced by a convergence or error test failure.
00807 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00808 160  IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 200
00809 RH = H/HOLD
00810 H = HOLD
00811 IREDO = 3
00812 GOTO 175
00813 170  RH = MAX(RH,HMIN/ABS(H))
00814 175  RH = MIN(RH,RMAX)
00815 RH = RH/MAX(1.0D0,ABS(H)*HMXI*RH)
00816 R = 1.0D0
00817 DO 180 J = 2,L
00818 R = R*RH
00819 DO 180 I = 1,N
00820 180      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J)*R
00821 H = H*RH
00822 RC = RC*RH
00823 IALTH = L
00824 IF (IREDO .EQ. 0) GOTO 690
00825 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00826 ! This section computes the predicted values by effectively
00827 ! multiplying the YH array by the Pascal Triangle matrix.
00828 ! RC is the ratio of new to old values of the coefficient  H*EL(1).
00829 ! When RC differs from 1 by more than CCMAX, IPUP is set to MITER
00830 ! to force PJAC to be called, if a Jacobian is involved.
00831 ! In any case, PJAC is called at least every MSBP steps.
00832 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00833 200  IF (ABS(RC-1.0D0) .GT. CCMAX) IPUP = MITER
00834 IF (NST .GE. NSLP+MSBP) IPUP = MITER
00835 TN = TN + H
00836 I1 = NQNYH + 1
00837 DO 215 JB = 1,NQ
00838 I1 = I1 - NYH
00839 !dir$ ivdep
00840 DO 210 I = I1,NQNYH
00841 210      YH1(I) = YH1(I) + YH1(I+NYH)
00842 215    CONTINUE
00843 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00844 ! Up to MAXCOR corrector iterations are taken.  A convergence test is
00845 ! made on the R.M.S. norm of each correction, weighted by the error
00846 ! weight vector EWT.  The sum of the corrections is accumulated in the
00847 ! vector ACOR(i).  The YH array is not altered in the corrector loop.
00848 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00849 220  M = 0
00850 DO 230 I = 1,N
00851 230    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
00852 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
00853 NFE = NFE + 1
00854 IF (IPUP .LE. 0) GOTO 250
00855 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00856 ! If indicated, the matrix P = I - h*el(1)*J is reevaluated and
00857 ! preprocessed before starting the corrector iteration.  IPUP is set
00858 ! to 0 as an indicator that this has been done.
00859 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00860 CALL PJAC (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, ACOR, SAVF, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
00861 IPUP = 0
00862 RC = 1.0D0
00863 NSLP = NST
00864 CRATE = 0.7D0
00865 IF (IERPJ .NE. 0) GOTO 430
00866 250  DO 260 I = 1,N
00867 260    ACOR(I) = 0.0D0
00868 270  IF (MITER .NE. 0) GOTO 350
00869 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00870 ! In the case of functional iteration, update Y directly from
00871 ! the result of the last function evaluation.
00872 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00873 DO 290 I = 1,N
00874 SAVF(I) = H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2)
00875 290    Y(I) = SAVF(I) - ACOR(I)
00876 DEL = DVNORM (N, Y, EWT)
00877 DO 300 I = 1,N
00878 Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*SAVF(I)
00879 300    ACOR(I) = SAVF(I)
00880 GOTO 400
00881 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00882 ! In the case of the chord method, compute the corrector error,
00883 ! and solve the linear system with that as right-hand side and
00884 ! P as coefficient matrix.
00885 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00886 350  DO 360 I = 1,N
00887 360    Y(I) = H*SAVF(I) - (YH(I,2) + ACOR(I))
00888 CALL SLVS (WM, IWM, Y, SAVF)
00889 IF (IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 430
00890 IF (IERSL .GT. 0) GOTO 410
00891 DEL = DVNORM (N, Y, EWT)
00892 DO 380 I = 1,N
00893 ACOR(I) = ACOR(I) + Y(I)
00894 380    Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*ACOR(I)
00895 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00896 ! Test for convergence.  If M.gt.0, an estimate of the convergence
00897 ! rate constant is stored in CRATE, and this is used in the test.
00898 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00899 400  IF (M .NE. 0) CRATE = MAX(0.2D0*CRATE,DEL/DELP)
00900 DCON = DEL*MIN(1.0D0,1.5D0*CRATE)/(TESCO(2,NQ)*CONIT)
00901 IF (DCON .LE. 1.0D0) GOTO 450
00902 M = M + 1
00903 IF (M .EQ. MAXCOR) GOTO 410
00904 IF (M .GE. 2 .AND. DEL .GT. 2.0D0*DELP) GOTO 410
00905 DELP = DEL
00906 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
00907 NFE = NFE + 1
00908 GOTO 270
00909 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00910 ! The corrector iteration failed to converge.
00911 ! If MITER .ne. 0 and the Jacobian is out of date, PJAC is called for
00912 ! the next try.  Otherwise the YH array is retracted to its values
00913 ! before prediction, and H is reduced, if possible.  If H cannot be
00914 ! reduced or MXNCF failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -2.
00915 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00916 410  IF (MITER .EQ. 0 .OR. JCUR .EQ. 1) GOTO 430
00917 ICF = 1
00918 IPUP = MITER
00919 GOTO 220
00920 430  ICF = 2
00921 NCF = NCF + 1
00922 RMAX = 2.0D0
00923 TN = TOLD
00924 I1 = NQNYH + 1
00925 DO 445 JB = 1,NQ
00926 I1 = I1 - NYH
00927 !dir$ ivdep
00928 DO 440 I = I1,NQNYH
00929 440      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
00930 445    CONTINUE
00931 IF (IERPJ .LT. 0 .OR. IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 680
00932 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 670
00933 IF (NCF .EQ. MXNCF) GOTO 670
00934 RH = 0.25D0
00935 IPUP = MITER
00936 IREDO = 1
00937 GOTO 170
00938 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00939 ! The corrector has converged.  JCUR is set to 0
00940 ! to signal that the Jacobian involved may need updating later.
00941 ! The local error test is made and control passes to statement 500
00942 ! if it fails.
00943 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00944 450  JCUR = 0
00945 IF (M .EQ. 0) DSM = DEL/TESCO(2,NQ)
00946 IF (M .GT. 0) DSM = DVNORM (N, ACOR, EWT)/TESCO(2,NQ)
00947 IF (DSM .GT. 1.0D0) GOTO 500
00948 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00949 ! After a successful step, update the YH array.
00950 ! Consider changing H if IALTH = 1.  Otherwise decrease IALTH by 1.
00951 ! If IALTH is then 1 and NQ .lt. MAXORD, then ACOR is saved for
00952 ! use in a possible order increase on the next step.
00953 ! If a change in H is considered, an increase or decrease in order
00954 ! by one is considered also.  A change in H is made only if it is by a
00955 ! factor of at least 1.1.  If not, IALTH is set to 3 to prevent
00956 ! testing for that many steps.
00957 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00958 KFLAG = 0
00959 IREDO = 0
00960 NST = NST + 1
00961 HU = H
00962 NQU = NQ
00963 DO 470 J = 1,L
00964 DO 470 I = 1,N
00965 470      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J) + EL(J)*ACOR(I)
00966 IALTH = IALTH - 1
00967 IF (IALTH .EQ. 0) GOTO 520
00968 IF (IALTH .GT. 1) GOTO 700
00969 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 700
00970 DO 490 I = 1,N
00971 490    YH(I,LMAX) = ACOR(I)
00972 GOTO 700
00973 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00974 ! The error test failed.  KFLAG keeps track of multiple failures.
00975 ! Restore TN and the YH array to their previous values, and prepare
00976 ! to try the step again.  Compute the optimum step size for this or
00977 ! one lower order.  After 2 or more failures, H is forced to decrease
00978 ! by a factor of 0.2 or less.
00979 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00980 500  KFLAG = KFLAG - 1
00981 TN = TOLD
00982 I1 = NQNYH + 1
00983 DO 515 JB = 1,NQ
00984 I1 = I1 - NYH
00985 !dir$ ivdep
00986 DO 510 I = I1,NQNYH
00987 510      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
00988 515    CONTINUE
00989 RMAX = 2.0D0
00990 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 660
00991 IF (KFLAG .LE. -3) GOTO 640
00992 IREDO = 2
00993 RHUP = 0.0D0
00994 GOTO 540
00995 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
00996 ! Regardless of the success or failure of the step, factors
00997 ! RHDN, RHSM, and RHUP are computed, by which H could be multiplied
00998 ! at order NQ - 1, order NQ, or order NQ + 1, respectively.
00999 ! In the case of failure, RHUP = 0.0 to avoid an order increase.
01000 ! The largest of these is determined and the new order chosen
01001 ! accordingly.  If the order is to be increased, we compute one
01002 ! additional scaled derivative.
01003 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01004 520  RHUP = 0.0D0
01005 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 540
01006 DO 530 I = 1,N
01007 530    SAVF(I) = ACOR(I) - YH(I,LMAX)
01008 DUP = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(3,NQ)
01009 EXUP = 1.0D0/(L+1)
01010 RHUP = 1.0D0/(1.4D0*DUP**EXUP + 0.0000014D0)
01011 540  EXSM = 1.0D0/L
01012 RHSM = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
01013 RHDN = 0.0D0
01014 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 560
01015 DDN = DVNORM (N, YH(1,L), EWT)/TESCO(1,NQ)
01016 EXDN = 1.0D0/NQ
01017 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
01018 560  IF (RHSM .GE. RHUP) GOTO 570
01019 IF (RHUP .GT. RHDN) GOTO 590
01020 GOTO 580
01021 570  IF (RHSM .LT. RHDN) GOTO 580
01022 NEWQ = NQ
01023 RH = RHSM
01024 GOTO 620
01025 580  NEWQ = NQ - 1
01026 RH = RHDN
01027 IF (KFLAG .LT. 0 .AND. RH .GT. 1.0D0) RH = 1.0D0
01028 GOTO 620
01029 590  NEWQ = L
01030 RH = RHUP
01031 IF (RH .LT. 1.1D0) GOTO 610
01032 R = EL(L)/L
01033 DO 600 I = 1,N
01034 600    YH(I,NEWQ+1) = ACOR(I)*R
01035 GOTO 630
01036 610  IALTH = 3
01037 GOTO 700
01038 620  IF ((KFLAG .EQ. 0) .AND. (RH .LT. 1.1D0)) GOTO 610
01039 IF (KFLAG .LE. -2) RH = MIN(RH,0.2D0)
01040 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01041 ! If there is a change of order, reset NQ, l, and the coefficients.
01042 ! In any case H is reset according to RH and the YH array is rescaled.
01043 ! Then exit from 690 if the step was OK, or redo the step otherwise.
01044 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01045 IF (NEWQ .EQ. NQ) GOTO 170
01046 630  NQ = NEWQ
01047 L = NQ + 1
01048 IRET = 2
01049 GOTO 150
01050 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01051 ! Control reaches this section if 3 or more failures have occured.
01052 ! If 10 failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -1.
01053 ! It is assumed that the derivatives that have accumulated in the
01054 ! YH array have errors of the wrong order.  Hence the first
01055 ! derivative is recomputed, and the order is set to 1.  Then
01056 ! H is reduced by a factor of 10, and the step is retried,
01057 ! until it succeeds or H reaches HMIN.
01058 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01059 640  IF (KFLAG .EQ. -10) GOTO 660
01060 RH = 0.1D0
01061 RH = MAX(HMIN/ABS(H),RH)
01062 H = H*RH
01063 DO 645 I = 1,N
01064 645    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
01065 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
01066 NFE = NFE + 1
01067 DO 650 I = 1,N
01068 650    YH(I,2) = H*SAVF(I)
01069 IPUP = MITER
01070 IALTH = 5
01071 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 200
01072 NQ = 1
01073 L = 2
01074 IRET = 3
01075 GOTO 150
01076 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01077 ! All returns are made through this section.  H is saved in HOLD
01078 ! to allow the caller to change H on the next step.
01079 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01080 660  KFLAG = -1
01081 GOTO 720
01082 670  KFLAG = -2
01083 GOTO 720
01084 680  KFLAG = -3
01085 GOTO 720
01086 690  RMAX = 10.0D0
01087 700  R = 1.0D0/TESCO(2,NQU)
01088 DO 710 I = 1,N
01089 710    ACOR(I) = ACOR(I)*R
01090 720  HOLD = H
01091 JSTART = 1
01092 RETURN
01093 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DSTODE ----------------------
01094 END
01095 
01096 SUBROUTINE DEWSET (N, ITOL, RTOL, ATOL, YCUR, EWT)
01097 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DEWSET
01098 !***SUBSIDIARY
01099 !***PURPOSE  Set error weight vector.
01100 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SEWSET-S, DEWSET-D)
01101 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
01102 !***DESCRIPTION
01103 !
01104 !  This subroutine sets the error weight vector EWT according to
01105 !      EWT(i) = RTOL(i)*ABS(YCUR(i)) + ATOL(i),  i = 1,...,N,
01106 !  with the subscript on RTOL and/or ATOL possibly replaced by 1 above,
01107 !  depending on the value of ITOL.
01108 !
01109 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
01110 !***ROUTINES CALLED  (NONE)
01111 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
01112 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
01113 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
01114 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
01115 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
01116 !***END PROLOGUE  DEWSET
01117 !**End
01118 INTEGER N, ITOL
01119 INTEGER I
01120 DOUBLE PRECISION RTOL, ATOL, YCUR, EWT
01121 DIMENSION RTOL(*), ATOL(*), YCUR(N), EWT(N)
01122 !
01123 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DEWSET
01124 GOTO (10, 20, 30, 40), ITOL
01125 10   CONTINUE
01126 DO 15 I = 1,N
01127 15     EWT(I) = RTOL(1)*ABS(YCUR(I)) + ATOL(1)
01128 RETURN
01129 20   CONTINUE
01130 DO 25 I = 1,N
01131 25     EWT(I) = RTOL(1)*ABS(YCUR(I)) + ATOL(I)
01132 RETURN
01133 30   CONTINUE
01134 DO 35 I = 1,N
01135 35     EWT(I) = RTOL(I)*ABS(YCUR(I)) + ATOL(1)
01136 RETURN
01137 40   CONTINUE
01138 DO 45 I = 1,N
01139 45     EWT(I) = RTOL(I)*ABS(YCUR(I)) + ATOL(I)
01140 RETURN
01141 !----------------------- END OF SUBROUTINE DEWSET ----------------------
01142 END
01143 
01144 DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DVNORM (N, V, W)
01145 !***BEGIN PROLOGUE  DVNORM
01146 !***SUBSIDIARY
01147 !***PURPOSE  Weighted root-mean-square vector norm.
01148 !***TYPE      DOUBLE PRECISION (SVNORM-S, DVNORM-D)
01149 !***AUTHOR  Hindmarsh, Alan C., (LLNL)
01150 !***DESCRIPTION
01151 !
01152 !  This function routine computes the weighted root-mean-square norm
01153 !  of the vector of length N contained in the array V, with weights
01154 !  contained in the array W of length N:
01155 !    DVNORM = SQRT( (1/N) * SUM( V(i)*W(i) )**2 )
01156 !
01157 !***SEE ALSO  DLSODE
01158 !***ROUTINES CALLED  (NONE)
01159 !***REVISION HISTORY  (YYMMDD)
01160 !   791129  DATE WRITTEN
01161 !   890501  Modified prologue to SLATEC/LDOC format.  (FNF)
01162 !   890503  Minor cosmetic changes.  (FNF)
01163 !   930809  Renamed to allow single/double precision versions. (ACH)
01164 !***END PROLOGUE  DVNORM
01165 !**End
01166 INTEGER N,   I
01167 DOUBLE PRECISION V, W,   SUM
01168 DIMENSION V(N), W(N)
01169 !
01170 !***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  DVNORM
01171 SUM = 0.0D0
01172 DO 10 I = 1,N
01173 10     SUM = SUM + (V(I)*W(I))**2
01174 DVNORM = SQRT(SUM/N)
01175 RETURN
01176 !----------------------- END OF FUNCTION DVNORM ------------------------
01177 END
01178 
01179 SUBROUTINE DIPREP (NEQ, Y, RWORK, IA, JA, IPFLAG, F, JAC)
01180 EXTERNAL F, JAC
01181 INTEGER NEQ, IA, JA, IPFLAG
01182 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, RWORK
01183 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), RWORK(*), IA(*), JA(*)
01184 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
01185 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01186 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
01187 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01188 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS,CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
01189 DOUBLE PRECISION RLSS
01190 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
01191 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01192 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, &
01193 IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01194 INTEGER I, IMAX, LEWTN, LYHD, LYHN
01195 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01196 ! This routine serves as an interface between the driver and
01197 ! Subroutine DPREP.  It is called only if MITER is 1 or 2.
01198 ! Tasks performed here are:
01199 !  * call DPREP,
01200 !  * reset the required WM segment length LENWK,
01201 !  * move YH back to its final location (following WM in RWORK),
01202 !  * reset pointers for YH, SAVF, EWT, and ACOR, and
01203 !  * move EWT to its new position if ISTATE = 1.
01204 ! IPFLAG is an output error indication flag.  IPFLAG = 0 if there was
01205 ! no trouble, and IPFLAG is the value of the DPREP error flag IPPER
01206 ! if there was trouble in Subroutine DPREP.
01207 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01208 IPFLAG = 0
01209 ! Call DPREP to do matrix preprocessing operations. --------------------
01210 CALL DPREP (NEQ, Y, RWORK(LYH), RWORK(LSAVF), RWORK(LEWT), RWORK(LACOR), IA, JA, RWORK(LWM), RWORK(LWM), IPFLAG, F, JAC)
01211 LENWK = MAX(LREQ,LWMIN)
01212 IF (IPFLAG .LT. 0) RETURN
01213 ! If DPREP was successful, move YH to end of required space for WM. ----
01214 LYHN = LWM + LENWK
01215 IF (LYHN .GT. LYH) RETURN
01216 LYHD = LYH - LYHN
01217 IF (LYHD .EQ. 0) GOTO 20
01218 IMAX = LYHN - 1 + LENYHM
01219 DO 10 I = LYHN,IMAX
01220 10     RWORK(I) = RWORK(I+LYHD)
01221 LYH = LYHN
01222 ! Reset pointers for SAVF, EWT, and ACOR. ------------------------------
01223 20   LSAVF = LYH + LENYH
01224 LEWTN = LSAVF + N
01225 LACOR = LEWTN + N
01226 IF (ISTATC .EQ. 3) GOTO 40
01227 ! If ISTATE = 1, move EWT (left) to its new position. ------------------
01228 IF (LEWTN .GT. LEWT) RETURN
01229 DO 30 I = 1,N
01230 30     RWORK(I+LEWTN-1) = RWORK(I+LEWT-1)
01231 40   LEWT = LEWTN
01232 RETURN
01233 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DIPREP ----------------------
01234 END
01235 
01236 SUBROUTINE DPREP (NEQ, Y, YH, SAVF, EWT, FTEM, IA, JA, WK, IWK, IPPER, F, JAC)
01237 EXTERNAL F,JAC
01238 INTEGER NEQ, IA, JA, IWK, IPPER
01239 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, SAVF, EWT, FTEM, WK
01240 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(*), SAVF(*), EWT(*), FTEM(*), IA(*), JA(*), WK(*), IWK(*)
01241 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
01242 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01243 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
01244 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01245 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
01246 DOUBLE PRECISION CON0, CONMIN, CCMXJ, PSMALL, RBIG, SETH
01247 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
01248 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01249 COMMON /DLSS01/ CON0, CONMIN, CCMXJ, PSMALL, RBIG, SETH, IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN,&
01250 IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, &
01251 NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01252 INTEGER I, IBR, IER, IPIL, IPIU, IPTT1, IPTT2, J, JFOUND, K, KNEW, KMAX, KMIN, LDIF, LENIGP, LIWK, MAXG, NP1, NZSUT
01253 DOUBLE PRECISION DQ, DYJ, ERWT, FAC, YJ
01254 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01255 ! This routine performs preprocessing related to the sparse linear
01256 ! systems that must be solved if MITER = 1 or 2.
01257 ! The operations that are performed here are:
01258 !  * compute sparseness structure of Jacobian according to MOSS,
01259 !  * compute grouping of column indices (MITER = 2),
01260 !  * compute a new ordering of rows and columns of the matrix,
01261 !  * reorder JA corresponding to the new ordering,
01262 !  * perform a symbolic LU factorization of the matrix, and
01263 !  * set pointers for segments of the IWK/WK array.
01264 ! In addition to variables described previously, DPREP uses the
01265 ! following for communication:
01266 ! YH     = the history array.  Only the first column, containing the
01267 !          current Y vector, is used.  Used only if MOSS .ne. 0.
01268 ! SAVF   = a work array of length NEQ, used only if MOSS .ne. 0.
01269 ! EWT    = array of length NEQ containing (inverted) error weights.
01270 !          Used only if MOSS = 2 or if ISTATE = MOSS = 1.
01271 ! FTEM   = a work array of length NEQ, identical to ACOR in the driver,
01272 !          used only if MOSS = 2.
01273 ! WK     = a real work array of length LENWK, identical to WM in
01274 !          the driver.
01275 ! IWK    = integer work array, assumed to occupy the same space as WK.
01276 ! LENWK  = the length of the work arrays WK and IWK.
01277 ! ISTATC = a copy of the driver input argument ISTATE (= 1 on the
01278 !          first call, = 3 on a continuation call).
01279 ! IYS    = flag value from ODRV or CDRV.
01280 ! IPPER  = output error flag with the following values and meanings:
01281 !          0  no error.
01282 !         -1  insufficient storage for internal structure pointers.
01283 !         -2  insufficient storage for JGROUP.
01284 !         -3  insufficient storage for ODRV.
01285 !         -4  other error flag from ODRV (should never occur).
01286 !         -5  insufficient storage for CDRV.
01287 !         -6  other error flag from CDRV.
01288 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01289 IBIAN = LRAT*2
01290 IPIAN = IBIAN + 1
01291 NP1 = N + 1
01292 IPJAN = IPIAN + NP1
01293 IBJAN = IPJAN - 1
01294 LIWK = LENWK*LRAT
01295 IF (IPJAN+N-1 .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01296 IF (MOSS .EQ. 0) GOTO 30
01297 !
01298 IF (ISTATC .EQ. 3) GOTO 20
01299 ! ISTATE = 1 and MOSS .ne. 0.  Perturb Y for structure determination. --
01300 DO 10 I = 1,N
01301 ERWT = 1.0D0/EWT(I)
01302 FAC = 1.0D0 + 1.0D0/(I + 1.0D0)
01303 Y(I) = Y(I) + FAC*SIGN(ERWT,Y(I))
01304 10     CONTINUE
01305 GOTO (70, 100), MOSS
01306 !
01307 20   CONTINUE
01308 ! ISTATE = 3 and MOSS .ne. 0.  Load Y from YH(*,1). --------------------
01309 DO 25 I = 1,N
01310 25     Y(I) = YH(I)
01311 GOTO (70, 100), MOSS
01312 !
01313 ! MOSS = 0.  Process user's IA,JA.  Add diagonal entries if necessary. -
01314 30   KNEW = IPJAN
01315 KMIN = IA(1)
01316 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
01317 DO 60 J = 1,N
01318 JFOUND = 0
01319 KMAX = IA(J+1) - 1
01320 IF (KMIN .GT. KMAX) GOTO 45
01321 DO 40 K = KMIN,KMAX
01322 I = JA(K)
01323 IF (I .EQ. J) JFOUND = 1
01324 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01325 IWK(KNEW) = I
01326 KNEW = KNEW + 1
01327 40       CONTINUE
01328 IF (JFOUND .EQ. 1) GOTO 50
01329 45     IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01330 IWK(KNEW) = J
01331 KNEW = KNEW + 1
01332 50     IWK(IPIAN+J) = KNEW + 1 - IPJAN
01333 KMIN = KMAX + 1
01334 60     CONTINUE
01335 GOTO 140
01336 !
01337 ! MOSS = 1.  Compute structure from user-supplied Jacobian routine JAC.
01338 70   CONTINUE
01339 ! A dummy call to F allows user to create temporaries for use in JAC. --
01340 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
01341 K = IPJAN
01342 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
01343 DO 90 J = 1,N
01344 IF (K .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01345 IWK(K) = J
01346 K = K + 1
01347 DO 75 I = 1,N
01348 75       SAVF(I) = 0.0D0
01349 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), SAVF)
01350 DO 80 I = 1,N
01351 IF (ABS(SAVF(I)) .LE. SETH) GOTO 80
01352 IF (I .EQ. J) GOTO 80
01353 IF (K .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01354 IWK(K) = I
01355 K = K + 1
01356 80       CONTINUE
01357 IWK(IPIAN+J) = K + 1 - IPJAN
01358 90     CONTINUE
01359 GOTO 140
01360 !
01361 ! MOSS = 2.  Compute structure from results of N + 1 calls to F. -------
01362 100  K = IPJAN
01363 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
01364 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
01365 DO 120 J = 1,N
01366 IF (K .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01367 IWK(K) = J
01368 K = K + 1
01369 YJ = Y(J)
01370 ERWT = 1.0D0/EWT(J)
01371 DYJ = SIGN(ERWT,YJ)
01372 Y(J) = YJ + DYJ
01373 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
01374 Y(J) = YJ
01375 DO 110 I = 1,N
01376 DQ = (FTEM(I) - SAVF(I))/DYJ
01377 IF (ABS(DQ) .LE. SETH) GOTO 110
01378 IF (I .EQ. J) GOTO 110
01379 IF (K .GT. LIWK) GOTO 210
01380 IWK(K) = I
01381 K = K + 1
01382 110      CONTINUE
01383 IWK(IPIAN+J) = K + 1 - IPJAN
01384 120    CONTINUE
01385 !
01386 140  CONTINUE
01387 IF (MOSS .EQ. 0 .OR. ISTATC .NE. 1) GOTO 150
01388 ! If ISTATE = 1 and MOSS .ne. 0, restore Y from YH. --------------------
01389 DO 145 I = 1,N
01390 145    Y(I) = YH(I)
01391 150  NNZ = IWK(IPIAN+N) - 1
01392 LENIGP = 0
01393 IPIGP = IPJAN + NNZ
01394 IF (MITER .NE. 2) GOTO 160
01395 !
01396 ! Compute grouping of column indices (MITER = 2). ----------------------
01397 MAXG = NP1
01398 IPJGP = IPJAN + NNZ
01399 IBJGP = IPJGP - 1
01400 IPIGP = IPJGP + N
01401 IPTT1 = IPIGP + NP1
01402 IPTT2 = IPTT1 + N
01403 LREQ = IPTT2 + N - 1
01404 IF (LREQ .GT. LIWK) GOTO 220
01405 CALL JGROUP (N, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), MAXG, NGP, IWK(IPIGP), IWK(IPJGP), IWK(IPTT1), IWK(IPTT2), IER)
01406 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 220
01407 LENIGP = NGP + 1
01408 !
01409 ! Compute new ordering of rows/columns of Jacobian. --------------------
01410 160  IPR = IPIGP + LENIGP
01411 IPC = IPR
01412 IPIC = IPC + N
01413 IPISP = IPIC + N
01414 IPRSP = (IPISP - 2)/LRAT + 2
01415 IESP = LENWK + 1 - IPRSP
01416 IF (IESP .LT. 0) GOTO 230
01417 IBR = IPR - 1
01418 DO 170 I = 1,N
01419 170    IWK(IBR+I) = I
01420 NSP = LIWK + 1 - IPISP
01421 CALL ODRV (N, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), WK, IWK(IPR), IWK(IPIC), NSP, IWK(IPISP), 1, IYS)
01422 IF (IYS .EQ. 11*N+1) GOTO 240
01423 IF (IYS .NE. 0) GOTO 230
01424 !
01425 ! Reorder JAN and do symbolic LU factorization of matrix. --------------
01426 IPA = LENWK + 1 - NNZ
01427 NSP = IPA - IPRSP
01428 LREQ = MAX(12*N/LRAT, 6*N/LRAT+2*N+NNZ) + 3
01429 LREQ = LREQ + IPRSP - 1 + NNZ
01430 IF (LREQ .GT. LENWK) GOTO 250
01431 IBA = IPA - 1
01432 DO 180 I = 1,NNZ
01433 180    WK(IBA+I) = 0.0D0
01434 IPISP = LRAT*(IPRSP - 1) + 1
01435 CALL CDRV (N,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN), WK(IPA),WK(IPA),WK(IPA),NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,5,IYS)
01436 LREQ = LENWK - IESP
01437 IF (IYS .EQ. 10*N+1) GOTO 250
01438 IF (IYS .NE. 0) GOTO 260
01439 IPIL = IPISP
01440 IPIU = IPIL + 2*N + 1
01441 NZU = IWK(IPIL+N) - IWK(IPIL)
01442 NZL = IWK(IPIU+N) - IWK(IPIU)
01443 IF (LRAT .GT. 1) GOTO 190
01444 CALL ADJLR (N, IWK(IPISP), LDIF)
01445 LREQ = LREQ + LDIF
01446 190  CONTINUE
01447 IF (LRAT .EQ. 2 .AND. NNZ .EQ. N) LREQ = LREQ + 1
01448 NSP = NSP + LREQ - LENWK
01449 IPA = LREQ + 1 - NNZ
01450 IBA = IPA - 1
01451 IPPER = 0
01452 RETURN
01453 !
01454 210  IPPER = -1
01455 LREQ = 2 + (2*N + 1)/LRAT
01456 LREQ = MAX(LENWK+1,LREQ)
01457 RETURN
01458 !
01459 220  IPPER = -2
01460 LREQ = (LREQ - 1)/LRAT + 1
01461 RETURN
01462 !
01463 230  IPPER = -3
01464 CALL CNTNZU (N, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), NZSUT)
01465 LREQ = LENWK - IESP + (3*N + 4*NZSUT - 1)/LRAT + 1
01466 RETURN
01467 !
01468 240  IPPER = -4
01469 RETURN
01470 !
01471 250  IPPER = -5
01472 RETURN
01473 !
01474 260  IPPER = -6
01475 LREQ = LENWK
01476 RETURN
01477 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPREP -----------------------
01478 END
01479 
01480 SUBROUTINE JGROUP (N,IA,JA,MAXG,NGRP,IGP,JGP,INCL,JDONE,IER)
01481 INTEGER N, IA, JA, MAXG, NGRP, IGP, JGP, INCL, JDONE, IER
01482 DIMENSION IA(*), JA(*), IGP(*), JGP(*), INCL(*), JDONE(*)
01483 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01484 ! This subroutine constructs groupings of the column indices of
01485 ! the Jacobian matrix, used in the numerical evaluation of the
01486 ! Jacobian by finite differences.
01487 !
01488 ! Input:
01489 ! N      = the order of the matrix.
01490 ! IA,JA  = sparse structure descriptors of the matrix by rows.
01491 ! MAXG   = length of available storage in the IGP array.
01492 !
01493 ! Output:
01494 ! NGRP   = number of groups.
01495 ! JGP    = array of length N containing the column indices by groups.
01496 ! IGP    = pointer array of length NGRP + 1 to the locations in JGP
01497 !          of the beginning of each group.
01498 ! IER    = error indicator.  IER = 0 if no error occurred, or 1 if
01499 !          MAXG was insufficient.
01500 !
01501 ! INCL and JDONE are working arrays of length N.
01502 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01503 INTEGER I, J, K, KMIN, KMAX, NCOL, NG
01504 !
01505 IER = 0
01506 DO 10 J = 1,N
01507 10     JDONE(J) = 0
01508 NCOL = 1
01509 DO 60 NG = 1,MAXG
01510 IGP(NG) = NCOL
01511 DO 20 I = 1,N
01512 20       INCL(I) = 0
01513 DO 50 J = 1,N
01514 ! Reject column J if it is already in a group.--------------------------
01515 IF (JDONE(J) .EQ. 1) GOTO 50
01516 KMIN = IA(J)
01517 KMAX = IA(J+1) - 1
01518 DO 30 K = KMIN,KMAX
01519 ! Reject column J if it overlaps any column already in this group.------
01520 I = JA(K)
01521 IF (INCL(I) .EQ. 1) GOTO 50
01522 30         CONTINUE
01523 ! Accept column J into group NG.----------------------------------------
01524 JGP(NCOL) = J
01525 NCOL = NCOL + 1
01526 JDONE(J) = 1
01527 DO 40 K = KMIN,KMAX
01528 I = JA(K)
01529 40         INCL(I) = 1
01530 50       CONTINUE
01531 ! Stop if this group is empty (grouping is complete).-------------------
01532 IF (NCOL .EQ. IGP(NG)) GOTO 70
01533 60     CONTINUE
01534 ! Error return if not all columns were chosen (MAXG too small).---------
01535 IF (NCOL .LE. N) GOTO 80
01536 NG = MAXG
01537 70   NGRP = NG - 1
01538 RETURN
01539 80   IER = 1
01540 RETURN
01541 !----------------------- End of Subroutine JGROUP ----------------------
01542 END
01543 
01544 SUBROUTINE ADJLR (N, ISP, LDIF)
01545 INTEGER N, ISP, LDIF
01546 DIMENSION ISP(*)
01547 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01548 ! This routine computes an adjustment, LDIF, to the required
01549 ! integer storage space in IWK (sparse matrix work space).
01550 ! It is called only if the word length ratio is LRAT = 1.
01551 ! This is to account for the possibility that the symbolic LU phase
01552 ! may require more storage than the numerical LU and solution phases.
01553 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01554 INTEGER IP, JLMAX, JUMAX, LNFC, LSFC, NZLU
01555 !
01556 IP = 2*N + 1
01557 ! Get JLMAX = IJL(N) and JUMAX = IJU(N) (sizes of JL and JU). ----------
01558 JLMAX = ISP(IP)
01559 JUMAX = ISP(IP+IP)
01560 ! NZLU = (size of L) + (size of U) = (IL(N+1)-IL(1)) + (IU(N+1)-IU(1)).
01561 NZLU = ISP(N+1) - ISP(1) + ISP(IP+N+1) - ISP(IP+1)
01562 LSFC = 12*N + 3 + 2*MAX(JLMAX,JUMAX)
01563 LNFC = 9*N + 2 + JLMAX + JUMAX + NZLU
01564 LDIF = MAX(0, LSFC - LNFC)
01565 RETURN
01566 !----------------------- End of Subroutine ADJLR -----------------------
01567 END
01568 
01569 SUBROUTINE CNTNZU (N, IA, JA, NZSUT)
01570 INTEGER N, IA, JA, NZSUT
01571 DIMENSION IA(*), JA(*)
01572 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01573 ! This routine counts the number of nonzero elements in the strict
01574 ! upper triangle of the matrix M + M(transpose), where the sparsity
01575 ! structure of M is given by pointer arrays IA and JA.
01576 ! This is needed to compute the storage requirements for the
01577 ! sparse matrix reordering operation in ODRV.
01578 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01579 INTEGER II, JJ, J, JMIN, JMAX, K, KMIN, KMAX, NUM
01580 !
01581 NUM = 0
01582 DO 50 II = 1,N
01583 JMIN = IA(II)
01584 JMAX = IA(II+1) - 1
01585 IF (JMIN .GT. JMAX) GOTO 50
01586 DO 40 J = JMIN,JMAX
01587 IF (JA(J) - II) 10, 40, 30
01588 10       JJ =JA(J)
01589 KMIN = IA(JJ)
01590 KMAX = IA(JJ+1) - 1
01591 IF (KMIN .GT. KMAX) GOTO 30
01592 DO 20 K = KMIN,KMAX
01593 IF (JA(K) .EQ. II) GOTO 40
01594 20         CONTINUE
01595 30       NUM = NUM + 1
01596 40       CONTINUE
01597 50     CONTINUE
01598 NZSUT = NUM
01599 RETURN
01600 !----------------------- End of Subroutine CNTNZU ----------------------
01601 END
01602 
01603 SUBROUTINE DPRJS (NEQ,Y,YH,NYH,EWT,FTEM,SAVF,WK,IWK,F,JAC)
01604 EXTERNAL F,JAC
01605 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWK
01606 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WK
01607 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), EWT(*), FTEM(*), SAVF(*), WK(*), IWK(*)
01608 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, 
01609 MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01610 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
01611 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01612 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
01613 DOUBLE PRECISION CON0, CONMIN, CCMXJ, PSMALL, RBIG, SETH
01614 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
01615 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01616 COMMON /DLSS01/ CON0, CONMIN, CCMXJ, PSMALL, RBIG, SETH, IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN,&
01617 IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, &
01618 NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01619 INTEGER I, IMUL, J, JJ, JOK, JMAX, JMIN, K, KMAX, KMIN, NG
01620 DOUBLE PRECISION CON, DI, FAC, HL0, PIJ, R, R0, RCON, RCONT, SRUR, DVNORM
01621 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01622 ! DPRJS is called to compute and process the matrix
01623 ! P = I - H*EL(1)*J , where J is an approximation to the Jacobian.
01624 ! J is computed by columns, either by the user-supplied routine JAC
01625 ! if MITER = 1, or by finite differencing if MITER = 2.
01626 ! if MITER = 3, a diagonal approximation to J is used.
01627 ! if MITER = 1 or 2, and if the existing value of the Jacobian
01628 ! (as contained in P) is considered acceptable, then a new value of
01629 ! P is reconstructed from the old value.  In any case, when MITER
01630 ! is 1 or 2, the P matrix is subjected to LU decomposition in CDRV.
01631 ! P and its LU decomposition are stored (separately) in WK.
01632 !
01633 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
01634 ! with DPRJS uses the following:
01635 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
01636 ! FTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODE).
01637 ! SAVF  = array containing f evaluated at predicted y.
01638 ! WK    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains the
01639 !         inverse diagonal matrix if MITER = 3, and P and its sparse
01640 !         LU decomposition if MITER is 1 or 2.
01641 !         Storage of matrix elements starts at WK(3).
01642 !         WK also contains the following matrix-related data:
01643 !         WK(1) = SQRT(UROUND), used in numerical Jacobian increments.
01644 !         WK(2) = H*EL0, saved for later use if MITER = 3.
01645 ! IWK   = integer work space for matrix-related data, assumed to
01646 !         be equivalenced to WK.  In addition, WK(IPRSP) and IWK(IPISP)
01647 !         are assumed to have identical locations.
01648 ! EL0   = EL(1) (input).
01649 ! IERPJ = output error flag (in Common).
01650 !       = 0 if no error.
01651 !       = 1  if zero pivot found in CDRV.
01652 !       = 2  if a singular matrix arose with MITER = 3.
01653 !       = -1 if insufficient storage for CDRV (should not occur here).
01654 !       = -2 if other error found in CDRV (should not occur here).
01655 ! JCUR  = output flag showing status of (approximate) Jacobian matrix:
01656 !          = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian is now current, or
01657 !          = 0 to indicate that a saved value was used.
01658 ! This routine also uses other variables in Common.
01659 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01660 HL0 = H*EL0
01661 CON = -HL0
01662 IF (MITER .EQ. 3) GOTO 300
01663 ! See whether J should be reevaluated (JOK = 0) or not (JOK = 1). ------
01664 JOK = 1
01665 IF (NST .EQ. 0 .OR. NST .GE. NSLJ+MSBJ) JOK = 0
01666 IF (ICF .EQ. 1 .AND. ABS(RC - 1.0D0) .LT. CCMXJ) JOK = 0
01667 IF (ICF .EQ. 2) JOK = 0
01668 IF (JOK .EQ. 1) GOTO 250
01669 !
01670 ! MITER = 1 or 2, and the Jacobian is to be reevaluated. ---------------
01671 20   JCUR = 1
01672 NJE = NJE + 1
01673 NSLJ = NST
01674 IPLOST = 0
01675 CONMIN = ABS(CON)
01676 GOTO (100, 200), MITER
01677 !
01678 ! If MITER = 1, call JAC, multiply by scalar, and add identity. --------
01679 100  CONTINUE
01680 KMIN = IWK(IPIAN)
01681 DO 130 J = 1, N
01682 KMAX = IWK(IPIAN+J) - 1
01683 DO 110 I = 1,N
01684 110      FTEM(I) = 0.0D0
01685 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), FTEM)
01686 DO 120 K = KMIN, KMAX
01687 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
01688 WK(IBA+K) = FTEM(I)*CON
01689 IF (I .EQ. J) WK(IBA+K) = WK(IBA+K) + 1.0D0
01690 120      CONTINUE
01691 KMIN = KMAX + 1
01692 130    CONTINUE
01693 GOTO 290
01694 !
01695 ! If MITER = 2, make NGP calls to F to approximate J and P. ------------
01696 200  CONTINUE
01697 FAC = DVNORM(N, SAVF, EWT)
01698 R0 = 1000.0D0 * ABS(H) * UROUND * N * FAC
01699 IF (R0 .EQ. 0.0D0) R0 = 1.0D0
01700 SRUR = WK(1)
01701 JMIN = IWK(IPIGP)
01702 DO 240 NG = 1,NGP
01703 JMAX = IWK(IPIGP+NG) - 1
01704 DO 210 J = JMIN,JMAX
01705 JJ = IWK(IBJGP+J)
01706 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(Y(JJ)),R0/EWT(JJ))
01707 210      Y(JJ) = Y(JJ) + R
01708 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
01709 DO 230 J = JMIN,JMAX
01710 JJ = IWK(IBJGP+J)
01711 Y(JJ) = YH(JJ,1)
01712 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(Y(JJ)),R0/EWT(JJ))
01713 FAC = -HL0/R
01714 KMIN =IWK(IBIAN+JJ)
01715 KMAX =IWK(IBIAN+JJ+1) - 1
01716 DO 220 K = KMIN,KMAX
01717 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
01718 WK(IBA+K) = (FTEM(I) - SAVF(I))*FAC
01719 IF (I .EQ. JJ) WK(IBA+K) = WK(IBA+K) + 1.0D0
01720 220        CONTINUE
01721 230      CONTINUE
01722 JMIN = JMAX + 1
01723 240    CONTINUE
01724 NFE = NFE + NGP
01725 GOTO 290
01726 !
01727 ! If JOK = 1, reconstruct new P from old P. ----------------------------
01728 250  JCUR = 0
01729 RCON = CON/CON0
01730 RCONT = ABS(CON)/CONMIN
01731 IF (RCONT .GT. RBIG .AND. IPLOST .EQ. 1) GOTO 20
01732 KMIN = IWK(IPIAN)
01733 DO 275 J = 1,N
01734 KMAX = IWK(IPIAN+J) - 1
01735 DO 270 K = KMIN,KMAX
01736 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
01737 PIJ = WK(IBA+K)
01738 IF (I .NE. J) GOTO 260
01739 PIJ = PIJ - 1.0D0
01740 IF (ABS(PIJ) .GE. PSMALL) GOTO 260
01741 IPLOST = 1
01742 CONMIN = MIN(ABS(CON0),CONMIN)
01743 260      PIJ = PIJ*RCON
01744 IF (I .EQ. J) PIJ = PIJ + 1.0D0
01745 WK(IBA+K) = PIJ
01746 270      CONTINUE
01747 KMIN = KMAX + 1
01748 275    CONTINUE
01749 !
01750 ! Do numerical factorization of P matrix. ------------------------------
01751 290  NLU = NLU + 1
01752 CON0 = CON
01753 IERPJ = 0
01754 DO 295 I = 1,N
01755 295    FTEM(I) = 0.0D0
01756 CALL CDRV (N,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN), WK(IPA),FTEM,FTEM,NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,2,IYS)
01757 IF (IYS .EQ. 0) RETURN
01758 IMUL = (IYS - 1)/N
01759 IERPJ = -2
01760 IF (IMUL .EQ. 8) IERPJ = 1
01761 IF (IMUL .EQ. 10) IERPJ = -1
01762 RETURN
01763 !
01764 ! If MITER = 3, construct a diagonal approximation to J and P. ---------
01765 300  CONTINUE
01766 JCUR = 1
01767 NJE = NJE + 1
01768 WK(2) = HL0
01769 IERPJ = 0
01770 R = EL0*0.1D0
01771 DO 310 I = 1,N
01772 310    Y(I) = Y(I) + R*(H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2))
01773 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, WK(3))
01774 NFE = NFE + 1
01775 DO 320 I = 1,N
01776 R0 = H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2)
01777 DI = 0.1D0*R0 - H*(WK(I+2) - SAVF(I))
01778 WK(I+2) = 1.0D0
01779 IF (ABS(R0) .LT. UROUND/EWT(I)) GOTO 320
01780 IF (ABS(DI) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 330
01781 WK(I+2) = 0.1D0*R0/DI
01782 320    CONTINUE
01783 RETURN
01784 330  IERPJ = 2
01785 RETURN
01786 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPRJS -----------------------
01787 END
01788 
01789 SUBROUTINE DSOLSS (WK, IWK, X, TEM)
01790 INTEGER IWK
01791 DOUBLE PRECISION WK, X, TEM
01792 DIMENSION WK(*), IWK(*), X(*), TEM(*)
01793 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
01794 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01795 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
01796 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01797 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS,CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
01798 DOUBLE PRECISION RLSS
01799 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
01800 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
01801 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, &
01802 IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
01803 INTEGER I
01804 DOUBLE PRECISION DI, HL0, PHL0, R
01805 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01806 ! This routine manages the solution of the linear system arising from
01807 ! a chord iteration.  It is called if MITER .ne. 0.
01808 ! If MITER is 1 or 2, it calls CDRV to accomplish this.
01809 ! If MITER = 3 it updates the coefficient H*EL0 in the diagonal
01810 ! matrix, and then computes the solution.
01811 ! communication with DSOLSS uses the following variables:
01812 ! WK    = real work space containing the inverse diagonal matrix if
01813 !         MITER = 3 and the LU decomposition of the matrix otherwise.
01814 !         Storage of matrix elements starts at WK(3).
01815 !         WK also contains the following matrix-related data:
01816 !         WK(1) = SQRT(UROUND) (not used here),
01817 !         WK(2) = HL0, the previous value of H*EL0, used if MITER = 3.
01818 ! IWK   = integer work space for matrix-related data, assumed to
01819 !         be equivalenced to WK.  In addition, WK(IPRSP) and IWK(IPISP)
01820 !         are assumed to have identical locations.
01821 ! X     = the right-hand side vector on input, and the solution vector
01822 !         on output, of length N.
01823 ! TEM   = vector of work space of length N, not used in this version.
01824 ! IERSL = output flag (in Common).
01825 !         IERSL = 0  if no trouble occurred.
01826 !         IERSL = -1 if CDRV returned an error flag (MITER = 1 or 2).
01827 !                    This should never occur and is considered fatal.
01828 !         IERSL = 1  if a singular matrix arose with MITER = 3.
01829 ! This routine also uses other variables in Common.
01830 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01831 IERSL = 0
01832 GOTO (100, 100, 300), MITER
01833 100  CALL CDRV (N,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN),WK(IPA),X,X,NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,4,IERSL)
01834 IF (IERSL .NE. 0) IERSL = -1
01835 RETURN
01836 !
01837 300  PHL0 = WK(2)
01838 HL0 = H*EL0
01839 WK(2) = HL0
01840 IF (HL0 .EQ. PHL0) GOTO 330
01841 R = HL0/PHL0
01842 DO 320 I = 1,N
01843 DI = 1.0D0 - R*(1.0D0 - 1.0D0/WK(I+2))
01844 IF (ABS(DI) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 390
01845 320    WK(I+2) = 1.0D0/DI
01846 330  DO 340 I = 1,N
01847 340    X(I) = WK(I+2)*X(I)
01848 RETURN
01849 390  IERSL = 1
01850 RETURN
01851 !
01852 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSOLSS ----------------------
01853 END
01854 
01855 SUBROUTINE DSRCMS (RSAV, ISAV, JOB)
01856 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01857 ! This routine saves or restores (depending on JOB) the contents of
01858 ! the Common blocks DLS001, DLSS01, which are used
01859 ! internally by one or more ODEPACK solvers.
01860 !
01861 ! RSAV = real array of length 224 or more.
01862 ! ISAV = integer array of length 71 or more.
01863 ! JOB  = flag indicating to save or restore the Common blocks:
01864 !        JOB  = 1 if Common is to be saved (written to RSAV/ISAV)
01865 !        JOB  = 2 if Common is to be restored (read from RSAV/ISAV)
01866 !        A call with JOB = 2 presumes a prior call with JOB = 1.
01867 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
01868 INTEGER ISAV, JOB
01869 INTEGER ILS, ILSS
01870 INTEGER I, LENILS, LENISS, LENRLS, LENRSS
01871 DOUBLE PRECISION RSAV,   RLS, RLSS
01872 DIMENSION RSAV(*), ISAV(*)
01873 SAVE LENRLS, LENILS, LENRSS, LENISS
01874 COMMON /DLS001/ RLS(218), ILS(37)
01875 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), ILSS(34)
01876 DATA LENRLS/218/, LENILS/37/, LENRSS/6/, LENISS/34/
01877 !
01878 IF (JOB .EQ. 2) GOTO 100
01879 DO 10 I = 1,LENRLS
01880 10     RSAV(I) = RLS(I)
01881 DO 15 I = 1,LENRSS
01882 15     RSAV(LENRLS+I) = RLSS(I)
01883 !
01884 DO 20 I = 1,LENILS
01885 20     ISAV(I) = ILS(I)
01886 DO 25 I = 1,LENISS
01887 25     ISAV(LENILS+I) = ILSS(I)
01888 !
01889 RETURN
01890 !
01891 100  CONTINUE
01892 DO 110 I = 1,LENRLS
01893 110     RLS(I) = RSAV(I)
01894 DO 115 I = 1,LENRSS
01895 115     RLSS(I) = RSAV(LENRLS+I)
01896 !
01897 DO 120 I = 1,LENILS
01898 120     ILS(I) = ISAV(I)
01899 DO 125 I = 1,LENISS
01900 125     ILSS(I) = ISAV(LENILS+I)
01901 !
01902 RETURN
01903 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSRCMS ----------------------
01904 END
01905 
01906 subroutine odrv(n, ia,ja,a, p,ip, nsp,isp, path, flag)
01907 !                                                                 5/2/83
01908 !***********************************************************************
