03862 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03863 160  IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 200
03864 RH = H/HOLD
03865 H = HOLD
03866 IREDO = 3
03867 GOTO 175
03868 170  RH = MAX(RH,HMIN/ABS(H))
03869 175  RH = MIN(RH,RMAX)
03870 RH = RH/MAX(1.0D0,ABS(H)*HMXI*RH)
03871 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03872 ! If METH = 1, also restrict the new step size by the stability region.
03873 ! If this reduces H, set IRFLAG to 1 so that if there are roundoff
03874 ! problems later, we can assume that is the cause of the trouble.
03875 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03876 IF (METH .EQ. 2) GOTO 178
03877 IRFLAG = 0
03878 PDH = MAX(ABS(H)*PDLAST,0.000001D0)
03879 IF (RH*PDH*1.00001D0 .LT. SM1(NQ)) GOTO 178
03880 RH = SM1(NQ)/PDH
03881 IRFLAG = 1
03882 178  CONTINUE
03883 R = 1.0D0
03884 DO 180 J = 2,L
03885 R = R*RH
03886 DO 180 I = 1,N
03887 180      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J)*R
03888 H = H*RH
03889 RC = RC*RH
03890 IALTH = L
03891 IF (IREDO .EQ. 0) GOTO 690
03892 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03893 ! This section computes the predicted values by effectively
03894 ! multiplying the YH array by the Pascal triangle matrix.
03895 ! RC is the ratio of new to old values of the coefficient  H*EL(1).
03896 ! When RC differs from 1 by more than CCMAX, IPUP is set to MITER
03897 ! to force PJAC to be called, if a Jacobian is involved.
03898 ! In any case, PJAC is called at least every MSBP steps.
03899 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03900 200  IF (ABS(RC-1.0D0) .GT. CCMAX) IPUP = MITER
03901 IF (NST .GE. NSLP+MSBP) IPUP = MITER
03902 TN = TN + H
03903 I1 = NQNYH + 1
03904 DO 215 JB = 1,NQ
03905 I1 = I1 - NYH
03906 !DIR$ IVDEP
03907 DO 210 I = I1,NQNYH
03908 210      YH1(I) = YH1(I) + YH1(I+NYH)
03909 215    CONTINUE
03910 PNORM = DMNORM (N, YH1, EWT)
03911 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03912 ! Up to MAXCOR corrector iterations are taken.  A convergence test is
03913 ! made on the RMS-norm of each correction, weighted by the error
03914 ! weight vector EWT.  The sum of the corrections is accumulated in the
03915 ! vector ACOR(i).  The YH array is not altered in the corrector loop.
03916 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03917 220  M = 0
03918 RATE = 0.0D0
03919 DEL = 0.0D0
03920 DO 230 I = 1,N
03921 230    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
03922 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
03923 NFE = NFE + 1
03924 IF (IPUP .LE. 0) GOTO 250
03925 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03926 ! If indicated, the matrix P = I - H*EL(1)*J is reevaluated and
03927 ! preprocessed before starting the corrector iteration.  IPUP is set
03928 ! to 0 as an indicator that this has been done.
03929 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03930 CALL PJAC (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, ACOR, SAVF, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
03931 IPUP = 0
03932 RC = 1.0D0
03933 NSLP = NST
03934 CRATE = 0.7D0
03935 IF (IERPJ .NE. 0) GOTO 430
03936 250  DO 260 I = 1,N
03937 260    ACOR(I) = 0.0D0
03938 270  IF (MITER .NE. 0) GOTO 350
03939 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03940 ! In the case of functional iteration, update Y directly from
03941 ! the result of the last function evaluation.
03942 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03943 DO 290 I = 1,N
03944 SAVF(I) = H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2)
03945 290    Y(I) = SAVF(I) - ACOR(I)
03946 DEL = DMNORM (N, Y, EWT)
03947 DO 300 I = 1,N
03948 Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*SAVF(I)
03949 300    ACOR(I) = SAVF(I)
03950 GOTO 400
03951 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03952 ! In the case of the chord method, compute the corrector error,
03953 ! and solve the linear system with that as right-hand side and
03954 ! P as coefficient matrix.
03955 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03956 350  DO 360 I = 1,N
03957 360    Y(I) = H*SAVF(I) - (YH(I,2) + ACOR(I))
03958 CALL SLVS (WM, IWM, Y, SAVF)
03959 IF (IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 430
03960 IF (IERSL .GT. 0) GOTO 410
03961 DEL = DMNORM (N, Y, EWT)
03962 DO 380 I = 1,N
03963 ACOR(I) = ACOR(I) + Y(I)
03964 380    Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*ACOR(I)
03965 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03966 ! Test for convergence.  If M .gt. 0, an estimate of the convergence
03967 ! rate constant is stored in CRATE, and this is used in the test.
03968 !
03969 ! We first check for a change of iterates that is the size of
03970 ! roundoff error.  If this occurs, the iteration has converged, and a
03971 ! new rate estimate is not formed.
03972 ! In all other cases, force at least two iterations to estimate a
03973 ! local Lipschitz constant estimate for Adams methods.
03974 ! On convergence, form PDEST = local maximum Lipschitz constant
03975 ! estimate.  PDLAST is the most recent nonzero estimate.
03976 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03977 400  CONTINUE
03978 IF (DEL .LE. 100.0D0*PNORM*UROUND) GOTO 450
03979 IF (M .EQ. 0 .AND. METH .EQ. 1) GOTO 405
03980 IF (M .EQ. 0) GOTO 402
03981 RM = 1024.0D0
03982 IF (DEL .LE. 1024.0D0*DELP) RM = DEL/DELP
03983 RATE = MAX(RATE,RM)
03984 CRATE = MAX(0.2D0*CRATE,RM)
03985 402  DCON = DEL*MIN(1.0D0,1.5D0*CRATE)/(TESCO(2,NQ)*CONIT)
03986 IF (DCON .GT. 1.0D0) GOTO 405
03987 PDEST = MAX(PDEST,RATE/ABS(H*EL(1)))
03988 IF (PDEST .NE. 0.0D0) PDLAST = PDEST
03989 GOTO 450
03990 405  CONTINUE
03991 M = M + 1
03992 IF (M .EQ. MAXCOR) GOTO 410
03993 IF (M .GE. 2 .AND. DEL .GT. 2.0D0*DELP) GOTO 410
03994 DELP = DEL
03995 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
03996 NFE = NFE + 1
03997 GOTO 270
03998 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
03999 ! The corrector iteration failed to converge.
04000 ! If MITER .ne. 0 and the Jacobian is out of date, PJAC is called for
04001 ! the next try.  Otherwise the YH array is retracted to its values
04002 ! before prediction, and H is reduced, if possible.  If H cannot be
04003 ! reduced or MXNCF failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -2.
04004 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04005 410  IF (MITER .EQ. 0 .OR. JCUR .EQ. 1) GOTO 430
04006 ICF = 1
04007 IPUP = MITER
04008 GOTO 220
04009 430  ICF = 2
04010 NCF = NCF + 1
04011 RMAX = 2.0D0
04012 TN = TOLD
04013 I1 = NQNYH + 1
04014 DO 445 JB = 1,NQ
04015 I1 = I1 - NYH
04016 !DIR$ IVDEP
04017 DO 440 I = I1,NQNYH
04018 440      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
04019 445    CONTINUE
04020 IF (IERPJ .LT. 0 .OR. IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 680
04021 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 670
04022 IF (NCF .EQ. MXNCF) GOTO 670
04023 RH = 0.25D0
04024 IPUP = MITER
04025 IREDO = 1
04026 GOTO 170
04027 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04028 ! The corrector has converged.  JCUR is set to 0
04029 ! to signal that the Jacobian involved may need updating later.
04030 ! The local error test is made and control passes to statement 500
04031 ! if it fails.
04032 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04033 450  JCUR = 0
04034 IF (M .EQ. 0) DSM = DEL/TESCO(2,NQ)
04035 IF (M .GT. 0) DSM = DMNORM (N, ACOR, EWT)/TESCO(2,NQ)
04036 IF (DSM .GT. 1.0D0) GOTO 500
04037 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04038 ! After a successful step, update the YH array.
04039 ! Decrease ICOUNT by 1, and if it is -1, consider switching methods.
04040 ! If a method switch is made, reset various parameters,
04041 ! rescale the YH array, and exit.  If there is no switch,
04042 ! consider changing H if IALTH = 1.  Otherwise decrease IALTH by 1.
04043 ! If IALTH is then 1 and NQ .lt. MAXORD, then ACOR is saved for
04044 ! use in a possible order increase on the next step.
04045 ! If a change in H is considered, an increase or decrease in order
04046 ! by one is considered also.  A change in H is made only if it is by a
04047 ! factor of at least 1.1.  If not, IALTH is set to 3 to prevent
04048 ! testing for that many steps.
04049 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04050 KFLAG = 0
04051 IREDO = 0
04052 NST = NST + 1
04053 HU = H
04054 NQU = NQ
04055 MUSED = METH
04056 DO 460 J = 1,L
04057 DO 460 I = 1,N
04058 460      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J) + EL(J)*ACOR(I)
04059 ICOUNT = ICOUNT - 1
04060 IF (ICOUNT .GE. 0) GOTO 488
04061 IF (METH .EQ. 2) GOTO 480
04062 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04063 ! We are currently using an Adams method.  Consider switching to BDF.
04064 ! If the current order is greater than 5, assume the problem is
04065 ! not stiff, and skip this section.
04066 ! If the Lipschitz constant and error estimate are not polluted
04067 ! by roundoff, GOTO 470 and perform the usual test.
04068 ! Otherwise, switch to the BDF methods if the last step was
04069 ! restricted to insure stability (irflag = 1), and stay with Adams
04070 ! method if not.  When switching to BDF with polluted error estimates,
04071 ! in the absence of other information, double the step size.
04072 !
04073 ! When the estimates are OK, we make the usual test by computing
04074 ! the step size we could have (ideally) used on this step,
04075 ! with the current (Adams) method, and also that for the BDF.
04076 ! If NQ .gt. MXORDS, we consider changing to order MXORDS on switching.
04077 ! Compare the two step sizes to decide whether to switch.
04078 ! The step size advantage must be at least RATIO = 5 to switch.
04079 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04080 IF (NQ .GT. 5) GOTO 488
04081 IF (DSM .GT. 100.0D0*PNORM*UROUND .AND. PDEST .NE. 0.0D0) GOTO 470
04082 IF (IRFLAG .EQ. 0) GOTO 488
04083 RH2 = 2.0D0
04084 NQM2 = MIN(NQ,MXORDS)
04085 GOTO 478
04086 470  CONTINUE
04087 EXSM = 1.0D0/L
04088 RH1 = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
04089 RH1IT = 2.0D0*RH1
04090 PDH = PDLAST*ABS(H)
04091 IF (PDH*RH1 .GT. 0.00001D0) RH1IT = SM1(NQ)/PDH
04092 RH1 = MIN(RH1,RH1IT)
04093 IF (NQ .LE. MXORDS) GOTO 474
04094 NQM2 = MXORDS
04095 LM2 = MXORDS + 1
04096 EXM2 = 1.0D0/LM2
04097 LM2P1 = LM2 + 1
04098 DM2 = DMNORM (N, YH(1,LM2P1), EWT)/CM2(MXORDS)
04099 RH2 = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DM2**EXM2 + 0.0000012D0)
04100 GOTO 476
04101 474  DM2 = DSM*(CM1(NQ)/CM2(NQ))
04102 RH2 = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DM2**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
04103 NQM2 = NQ
04104 476  CONTINUE
04105 IF (RH2 .LT. RATIO*RH1) GOTO 488
04106 ! THE SWITCH TEST PASSED.  RESET RELEVANT QUANTITIES FOR BDF. ----------
04107 478  RH = RH2
04108 ICOUNT = 20
04109 METH = 2
04110 MITER = JTYP
04111 PDLAST = 0.0D0
04112 NQ = NQM2
04113 L = NQ + 1
04114 GOTO 170
04115 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04116 ! We are currently using a BDF method.  Consider switching to Adams.
04117 ! Compute the step size we could have (ideally) used on this step,
04118 ! with the current (BDF) method, and also that for the Adams.
04119 ! If NQ .gt. MXORDN, we consider changing to order MXORDN on switching.
04120 ! Compare the two step sizes to decide whether to switch.
04121 ! The step size advantage must be at least 5/RATIO = 1 to switch.
04122 ! If the step size for Adams would be so small as to cause
04123 ! roundoff pollution, we stay with BDF.
04124 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04125 480  CONTINUE
04126 EXSM = 1.0D0/L
04127 IF (MXORDN .GE. NQ) GOTO 484
04128 NQM1 = MXORDN
04129 LM1 = MXORDN + 1
04130 EXM1 = 1.0D0/LM1
04131 LM1P1 = LM1 + 1
04132 DM1 = DMNORM (N, YH(1,LM1P1), EWT)/CM1(MXORDN)
04133 RH1 = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DM1**EXM1 + 0.0000012D0)
04134 GOTO 486
04135 484  DM1 = DSM*(CM2(NQ)/CM1(NQ))
04136 RH1 = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DM1**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
04137 NQM1 = NQ
04138 EXM1 = EXSM
04139 486  RH1IT = 2.0D0*RH1
04140 PDH = PDNORM*ABS(H)
04141 IF (PDH*RH1 .GT. 0.00001D0) RH1IT = SM1(NQM1)/PDH
04142 RH1 = MIN(RH1,RH1IT)
04143 RH2 = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
04144 IF (RH1*RATIO .LT. 5.0D0*RH2) GOTO 488
04145 ALPHA = MAX(0.001D0,RH1)
04146 DM1 = (ALPHA**EXM1)*DM1
04147 IF (DM1 .LE. 1000.0D0*UROUND*PNORM) GOTO 488
04148 ! The switch test passed.  Reset relevant quantities for Adams. --------
04149 RH = RH1
04150 ICOUNT = 20
04151 METH = 1
04152 MITER = 0
04153 PDLAST = 0.0D0
04154 NQ = NQM1
04155 L = NQ + 1
04156 GOTO 170
04157 !
04158 ! No method switch is being made.  Do the usual step/order selection. --
04159 488  CONTINUE
04160 IALTH = IALTH - 1
04161 IF (IALTH .EQ. 0) GOTO 520
04162 IF (IALTH .GT. 1) GOTO 700
04163 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 700
04164 DO 490 I = 1,N
04165 490    YH(I,LMAX) = ACOR(I)
04166 GOTO 700
04167 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04168 ! The error test failed.  KFLAG keeps track of multiple failures.
04169 ! Restore TN and the YH array to their previous values, and prepare
04170 ! to try the step again.  Compute the optimum step size for this or
04171 ! one lower order.  After 2 or more failures, H is forced to decrease
04172 ! by a factor of 0.2 or less.
04173 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04174 500  KFLAG = KFLAG - 1
04175 TN = TOLD
04176 I1 = NQNYH + 1
04177 DO 515 JB = 1,NQ
04178 I1 = I1 - NYH
04179 !DIR$ IVDEP
04180 DO 510 I = I1,NQNYH
04181 510      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
04182 515    CONTINUE
04183 RMAX = 2.0D0
04184 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 660
04185 IF (KFLAG .LE. -3) GOTO 640
04186 IREDO = 2
04187 RHUP = 0.0D0
04188 GOTO 540
04189 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04190 ! Regardless of the success or failure of the step, factors
04191 ! RHDN, RHSM, and RHUP are computed, by which H could be multiplied
04192 ! at order NQ - 1, order NQ, or order NQ + 1, respectively.
04193 ! In the case of failure, RHUP = 0.0 to avoid an order increase.
04194 ! The largest of these is determined and the new order chosen
04195 ! accordingly.  If the order is to be increased, we compute one
04196 ! additional scaled derivative.
04197 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04198 520  RHUP = 0.0D0
04199 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 540
04200 DO 530 I = 1,N
04201 530    SAVF(I) = ACOR(I) - YH(I,LMAX)
04202 DUP = DMNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(3,NQ)
04203 EXUP = 1.0D0/(L+1)
04204 RHUP = 1.0D0/(1.4D0*DUP**EXUP + 0.0000014D0)
04205 540  EXSM = 1.0D0/L
04206 RHSM = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
04207 RHDN = 0.0D0
04208 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 550
04209 DDN = DMNORM (N, YH(1,L), EWT)/TESCO(1,NQ)
04210 EXDN = 1.0D0/NQ
04211 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
04212 ! If METH = 1, limit RH according to the stability region also. --------
04213 550  IF (METH .EQ. 2) GOTO 560
04214 PDH = MAX(ABS(H)*PDLAST,0.000001D0)
04215 IF (L .LT. LMAX) RHUP = MIN(RHUP,SM1(L)/PDH)
04216 RHSM = MIN(RHSM,SM1(NQ)/PDH)
04217 IF (NQ .GT. 1) RHDN = MIN(RHDN,SM1(NQ-1)/PDH)
04218 PDEST = 0.0D0
04219 560  IF (RHSM .GE. RHUP) GOTO 570
04220 IF (RHUP .GT. RHDN) GOTO 590
04221 GOTO 580
04222 570  IF (RHSM .LT. RHDN) GOTO 580
04223 NEWQ = NQ
04224 RH = RHSM
04225 GOTO 620
04226 580  NEWQ = NQ - 1
04227 RH = RHDN
04228 IF (KFLAG .LT. 0 .AND. RH .GT. 1.0D0) RH = 1.0D0
04229 GOTO 620
04230 590  NEWQ = L
04231 RH = RHUP
04232 IF (RH .LT. 1.1D0) GOTO 610
04233 R = EL(L)/L
04234 DO 600 I = 1,N
04235 600    YH(I,NEWQ+1) = ACOR(I)*R
04236 GOTO 630
04237 610  IALTH = 3
04238 GOTO 700
04239 ! If METH = 1 and H is restricted by stability, bypass 10 percent test.
04240 620  IF (METH .EQ. 2) GOTO 622
04241 IF (RH*PDH*1.00001D0 .GE. SM1(NEWQ)) GOTO 625
04242 622  IF (KFLAG .EQ. 0 .AND. RH .LT. 1.1D0) GOTO 610
04243 625  IF (KFLAG .LE. -2) RH = MIN(RH,0.2D0)
04244 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04245 ! If there is a change of order, reset NQ, L, and the coefficients.
04246 ! In any case H is reset according to RH and the YH array is rescaled.
04247 ! Then exit from 690 if the step was OK, or redo the step otherwise.
04248 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04249 IF (NEWQ .EQ. NQ) GOTO 170
04250 630  NQ = NEWQ
04251 L = NQ + 1
04252 IRET = 2
04253 GOTO 150
04254 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04255 ! Control reaches this section if 3 or more failures have occured.
04256 ! If 10 failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -1.
04257 ! It is assumed that the derivatives that have accumulated in the
04258 ! YH array have errors of the wrong order.  Hence the first
04259 ! derivative is recomputed, and the order is set to 1.  Then
04260 ! H is reduced by a factor of 10, and the step is retried,
04261 ! until it succeeds or H reaches HMIN.
04262 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04263 640  IF (KFLAG .EQ. -10) GOTO 660
04264 RH = 0.1D0
04265 RH = MAX(HMIN/ABS(H),RH)
04266 H = H*RH
04267 DO 645 I = 1,N
04268 645    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
04269 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
04270 NFE = NFE + 1
04271 DO 650 I = 1,N
04272 650    YH(I,2) = H*SAVF(I)
04273 IPUP = MITER
04274 IALTH = 5
04275 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 200
04276 NQ = 1
04277 L = 2
04278 IRET = 3
04279 GOTO 150
04280 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04281 ! All returns are made through this section.  H is saved in HOLD
04282 ! to allow the caller to change H on the next step.
04283 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04284 660  KFLAG = -1
04285 GOTO 720
04286 670  KFLAG = -2
04287 GOTO 720
04288 680  KFLAG = -3
04289 GOTO 720
04290 690  RMAX = 10.0D0
04291 700  R = 1.0D0/TESCO(2,NQU)
04292 DO 710 I = 1,N
04293 710    ACOR(I) = ACOR(I)*R
04294 720  HOLD = H
04295 JSTART = 1
04296 RETURN
04297 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSTODA ----------------------
04298 END
04299 
04300 SUBROUTINE DPRJA (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM, IWM,F, JAC)
04301 EXTERNAL F, JAC
04302 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
04303 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM
04304 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), EWT(*), FTEM(*), SAVF(*),WM(*), IWM(*)
04305 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
04306 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
04307 INTEGER IOWND2, IOWNS2, JTYP, MUSED, MXORDN, MXORDS
04308 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
04309 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWND2, ROWNS2, PDNORM
04310 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
04311 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
04312 COMMON /DLSA01/ ROWND2, ROWNS2(20), PDNORM, IOWND2(3), IOWNS2(2), JTYP, MUSED, MXORDN, MXORDS
04313 INTEGER I, I1, I2, IER, II, J, J1, JJ, LENP, MBA, MBAND, MEB1, MEBAND, ML, ML3, MU, NP1
04314 DOUBLE PRECISION CON, FAC, HL0, R, R0, SRUR, YI, YJ, YJJ, DMNORM, DFNORM, DBNORM
04315 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04316 ! DPRJA is called by DSTODA to compute and process the matrix
04317 ! P = I - H*EL(1)*J , where J is an approximation to the Jacobian.
04318 ! Here J is computed by the user-supplied routine JAC if
04319 ! MITER = 1 or 4 or by finite differencing if MITER = 2 or 5.
04320 ! J, scaled by -H*EL(1), is stored in WM.  Then the norm of J (the
04321 ! matrix norm consistent with the weighted max-norm on vectors given
04322 ! by DMNORM) is computed, and J is overwritten by P.  P is then
04323 ! subjected to LU decomposition in preparation for later solution
04324 ! of linear systems with P as coefficient matrix.  This is done
04325 ! by DGEFA if MITER = 1 or 2, and by DGBFA if MITER = 4 or 5.
04326 !
04327 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
04328 ! with DPRJA uses the following:
04329 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
04330 ! FTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODA).
04331 ! SAVF  = array containing f evaluated at predicted y.
04332 ! WM    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains the
04333 !         LU decomposition of P.
04334 !         Storage of matrix elements starts at WM(3).
04335 !         WM also contains the following matrix-related data:
04336 !         WM(1) = SQRT(UROUND), used in numerical Jacobian increments.
04337 ! IWM   = integer work space containing pivot information, starting at
04338 !         IWM(21).   IWM also contains the band parameters
04339 !         ML = IWM(1) and MU = IWM(2) if MITER is 4 or 5.
04340 ! EL0   = EL(1) (input).
04341 ! PDNORM= norm of Jacobian matrix. (Output).
04342 ! IERPJ = output error flag,  = 0 if no trouble, .gt. 0 if
04343 !         P matrix found to be singular.
04344 ! JCUR  = output flag = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian matrix
04345 !         (or approximation) is now current.
04346 ! This routine also uses the Common variables EL0, H, TN, UROUND,
04347 ! MITER, N, NFE, and NJE.
04348 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04349 NJE = NJE + 1
04350 IERPJ = 0
04351 JCUR = 1
04352 HL0 = H*EL0
04353 GOTO (100, 200, 300, 400, 500), MITER
04354 ! If MITER = 1, call JAC and multiply by scalar. -----------------------
04355 100  LENP = N*N
04356 DO 110 I = 1,LENP
04357 110    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
04358 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, 0, 0, WM(3), N)
04359 CON = -HL0
04360 DO 120 I = 1,LENP
04361 120    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
04362 GOTO 240
04363 ! If MITER = 2, make N calls to F to approximate J. --------------------
04364 200  FAC = DMNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)
04365 R0 = 1000.0D0*ABS(H)*UROUND*N*FAC
04366 IF (R0 .EQ. 0.0D0) R0 = 1.0D0
04367 SRUR = WM(1)
04368 J1 = 2
04369 DO 230 J = 1,N
04370 YJ = Y(J)
04371 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YJ),R0/EWT(J))
04372 Y(J) = Y(J) + R
04373 FAC = -HL0/R
04374 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
04375 DO 220 I = 1,N
04376 220      WM(I+J1) = (FTEM(I) - SAVF(I))*FAC
04377 Y(J) = YJ
04378 J1 = J1 + N
04379 230    CONTINUE
04380 NFE = NFE + N
04381 240  CONTINUE
04382 ! Compute norm of Jacobian. --------------------------------------------
04383 PDNORM = DFNORM (N, WM(3), EWT)/ABS(HL0)
04384 ! Add identity matrix. -------------------------------------------------
04385 J = 3
04386 NP1 = N + 1
04387 DO 250 I = 1,N
04388 WM(J) = WM(J) + 1.0D0
04389 250    J = J + NP1
04390 ! Do LU decomposition on P. --------------------------------------------
04391 CALL DGEFA (WM(3), N, N, IWM(21), IER)
04392 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
04393 RETURN
04394 ! Dummy block only, since MITER is never 3 in this routine. ------------
04395 300  RETURN
04396 ! If MITER = 4, call JAC and multiply by scalar. -----------------------
04397 400  ML = IWM(1)
04398 MU = IWM(2)
04399 ML3 = ML + 3
04400 MBAND = ML + MU + 1
04401 MEBAND = MBAND + ML
04402 LENP = MEBAND*N
04403 DO 410 I = 1,LENP
04404 410    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
04405 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, ML, MU, WM(ML3), MEBAND)
04406 CON = -HL0
04407 DO 420 I = 1,LENP
04408 420    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
04409 GOTO 570
04410 ! If MITER = 5, make MBAND calls to F to approximate J. ----------------
04411 500  ML = IWM(1)
04412 MU = IWM(2)
04413 MBAND = ML + MU + 1
04414 MBA = MIN(MBAND,N)
04415 MEBAND = MBAND + ML
04416 MEB1 = MEBAND - 1
04417 SRUR = WM(1)
04418 FAC = DMNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)
04419 R0 = 1000.0D0*ABS(H)*UROUND*N*FAC
04420 IF (R0 .EQ. 0.0D0) R0 = 1.0D0
04421 DO 560 J = 1,MBA
04422 DO 530 I = J,N,MBAND
04423 YI = Y(I)
04424 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YI),R0/EWT(I))
04425 530      Y(I) = Y(I) + R
04426 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
04427 DO 550 JJ = J,N,MBAND
04428 Y(JJ) = YH(JJ,1)
04429 YJJ = Y(JJ)
04430 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YJJ),R0/EWT(JJ))
04431 FAC = -HL0/R
04432 I1 = MAX(JJ-MU,1)
04433 I2 = MIN(JJ+ML,N)
04434 II = JJ*MEB1 - ML + 2
04435 DO 540 I = I1,I2
04436 540        WM(II+I) = (FTEM(I) - SAVF(I))*FAC
04437 550      CONTINUE
04438 560    CONTINUE
04439 NFE = NFE + MBA
04440 570  CONTINUE
04441 ! Compute norm of Jacobian. --------------------------------------------
04442 PDNORM = DBNORM (N, WM(ML+3), MEBAND, ML, MU, EWT)/ABS(HL0)
04443 ! Add identity matrix. -------------------------------------------------
04444 II = MBAND + 2
04445 DO 580 I = 1,N
04446 WM(II) = WM(II) + 1.0D0
04447 580    II = II + MEBAND
04448 ! Do LU decomposition of P. --------------------------------------------
04449 CALL DGBFA (WM(3), MEBAND, N, ML, MU, IWM(21), IER)
04450 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
04451 RETURN
04452 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPRJA -----------------------
04453 END
04454 
04455 DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DMNORM (N, V, W)
04456 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04457 ! This function routine computes the weighted max-norm
04458 ! of the vector of length N contained in the array V, with weights
04459 ! contained in the array w of length N:
04460 !   DMNORM = MAX(i=1,...,N) ABS(V(i))*W(i)
04461 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04462 INTEGER N,   I
04463 DOUBLE PRECISION V, W,   VM
04464 DIMENSION V(N), W(N)
04465 VM = 0.0D0
04466 DO 10 I = 1,N
04467 10     VM = MAX(VM,ABS(V(I))*W(I))
04468 DMNORM = VM
04469 RETURN
04470 !----------------------- End of Function DMNORM ------------------------
04471 END
04472 
04473 DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DFNORM (N, A, W)
04474 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04475 ! This function computes the norm of a full N by N matrix,
04476 ! stored in the array A, that is consistent with the weighted max-norm
04477 ! on vectors, with weights stored in the array W:
04478 !   DFNORM = MAX(i=1,...,N) ( W(i) * Sum(j=1,...,N) ABS(a(i,j))/W(j) )
04479 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04480 INTEGER N,   I, J
04481 DOUBLE PRECISION A,   W, AN, SUM
04482 DIMENSION A(N,N), W(N)
04483 AN = 0.0D0
04484 DO 20 I = 1,N
04485 SUM = 0.0D0
04486 DO 10 J = 1,N
04487 10       SUM = SUM + ABS(A(I,J))/W(J)
04488 AN = MAX(AN,SUM*W(I))
04489 20     CONTINUE
04490 DFNORM = AN
04491 RETURN
04492 !----------------------- End of Function DFNORM ------------------------
04493 END
04494 
04495 DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DBNORM (N, A, NRA, ML, MU, W)
04496 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04497 ! This function computes the norm of a banded N by N matrix,
04498 ! stored in the array A, that is consistent with the weighted max-norm
04499 ! on vectors, with weights stored in the array W.
04500 ! ML and MU are the lower and upper half-bandwidths of the matrix.
04501 ! NRA is the first dimension of the A array, NRA .ge. ML+MU+1.
04502 ! In terms of the matrix elements a(i,j), the norm is given by:
04503 !   DBNORM = MAX(i=1,...,N) ( W(i) * Sum(j=1,...,N) ABS(a(i,j))/W(j) )
04504 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04505 INTEGER N, NRA, ML, MU
04506 INTEGER I, I1, JLO, JHI, J
04507 DOUBLE PRECISION A, W
04508 DOUBLE PRECISION AN, SUM
04509 DIMENSION A(NRA,N), W(N)
04510 AN = 0.0D0
04511 DO 20 I = 1,N
04512 SUM = 0.0D0
04513 I1 = I + MU + 1
04514 JLO = MAX(I-ML,1)
04515 JHI = MIN(I+MU,N)
04516 DO 10 J = JLO,JHI
04517 10       SUM = SUM + ABS(A(I1-J,J))/W(J)
04518 AN = MAX(AN,SUM*W(I))
04519 20     CONTINUE
04520 DBNORM = AN
04521 RETURN
04522 !----------------------- End of Function DBNORM ------------------------
04523 END
04524 
04525 SUBROUTINE DSRCMA (RSAV, ISAV, JOB)
04526 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04527 ! This routine saves or restores (depending on JOB) the contents of
04528 ! the Common blocks DLS001, DLSA01, which are used
04529 ! internally by one or more ODEPACK solvers.
04530 !
04531 ! RSAV = real array of length 240 or more.
04532 ! ISAV = integer array of length 46 or more.
04533 ! JOB  = flag indicating to save or restore the Common blocks:
04534 !        JOB  = 1 if Common is to be saved (written to RSAV/ISAV)
04535 !        JOB  = 2 if Common is to be restored (read from RSAV/ISAV)
04536 !        A call with JOB = 2 presumes a prior call with JOB = 1.
04537 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04538 INTEGER ISAV, JOB
04539 INTEGER ILS, ILSA
04540 INTEGER I, LENRLS, LENILS, LENRLA, LENILA
04541 DOUBLE PRECISION RSAV
04542 DOUBLE PRECISION RLS, RLSA
04543 DIMENSION RSAV(*), ISAV(*)
04544 SAVE LENRLS, LENILS, LENRLA, LENILA
04545 COMMON /DLS001/ RLS(218), ILS(37)
04546 COMMON /DLSA01/ RLSA(22), ILSA(9)
04547 DATA LENRLS/218/, LENILS/37/, LENRLA/22/, LENILA/9/
04548 !
04549 IF (JOB .EQ. 2) GOTO 100
04550 DO 10 I = 1,LENRLS
04551 10     RSAV(I) = RLS(I)
04552 DO 15 I = 1,LENRLA
04553 15     RSAV(LENRLS+I) = RLSA(I)
04554 !
04555 DO 20 I = 1,LENILS
04556 20     ISAV(I) = ILS(I)
04557 DO 25 I = 1,LENILA
04558 25     ISAV(LENILS+I) = ILSA(I)
04559 !
04560 RETURN
04561 !
04562 100  CONTINUE
04563 DO 110 I = 1,LENRLS
04564 110     RLS(I) = RSAV(I)
04565 DO 115 I = 1,LENRLA
04566 115     RLSA(I) = RSAV(LENRLS+I)
04567 !
04568 DO 120 I = 1,LENILS
04569 120     ILS(I) = ISAV(I)
04570 DO 125 I = 1,LENILA
04571 125     ILSA(I) = ISAV(LENILS+I)
04572 !
04573 RETURN
04574 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSRCMA ----------------------
04575 END
04576 
04577 SUBROUTINE DRCHEK (JOB, G, NEQ, Y, YH,NYH, G0, G1, GX, JROOT, IRT)
04578 EXTERNAL G
04579 INTEGER JOB, NEQ, NYH, JROOT, IRT
04580 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, G0, G1, GX
04581 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), G0(*), G1(*), GX(*), JROOT(*)
04582 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
04583 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
04584 INTEGER IOWND3, IOWNR3, IRFND, ITASKC, NGC, NGE
04585 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
04586 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNR3, T0, TLAST, TOUTC
04587 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
04588 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
04589 COMMON /DLSR01/ ROWNR3(2), T0, TLAST, TOUTC, IOWND3(3), IOWNR3(2), IRFND, ITASKC, NGC, NGE
04590 INTEGER I, IFLAG, JFLAG
04591 DOUBLE PRECISION HMING, T1, TEMP1, TEMP2, X
04592 LOGICAL ZROOT
04593 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04594 ! This routine checks for the presence of a root in the vicinity of
04595 ! the current T, in a manner depending on the input flag JOB.  It calls
04596 ! Subroutine DROOTS to locate the root as precisely as possible.
04597 !
04598 ! In addition to variables described previously, DRCHEK
04599 ! uses the following for communication:
04600 ! JOB    = integer flag indicating type of call:
04601 !          JOB = 1 means the problem is being initialized, and DRCHEK
04602 !                  is to look for a root at or very near the initial T.
04603 !          JOB = 2 means a continuation call to the solver was just
04604 !                  made, and DRCHEK is to check for a root in the
04605 !                  relevant part of the step last taken.
04606 !          JOB = 3 means a successful step was just taken, and DRCHEK
04607 !                  is to look for a root in the interval of the step.
04608 ! G0     = array of length NG, containing the value of g at T = T0.
04609 !          G0 is input for JOB .ge. 2, and output in all cases.
04610 ! G1,GX  = arrays of length NG for work space.
04611 ! IRT    = completion flag:
04612 !          IRT = 0  means no root was found.
04613 !          IRT = -1 means JOB = 1 and a root was found too near to T.
04614 !          IRT = 1  means a legitimate root was found (JOB = 2 or 3).
04615 !                   On return, T0 is the root location, and Y is the
04616 !                   corresponding solution vector.
04617 ! T0     = value of T at one endpoint of interval of interest.  Only
04618 !          roots beyond T0 in the direction of integration are sought.
04619 !          T0 is input if JOB .ge. 2, and output in all cases.
04620 !          T0 is updated by DRCHEK, whether a root is found or not.
04621 ! TLAST  = last value of T returned by the solver (input only).
04622 ! TOUTC  = copy of TOUT (input only).
04623 ! IRFND  = input flag showing whether the last step taken had a root.
04624 !          IRFND = 1 if it did, = 0 if not.
04625 ! ITASKC = copy of ITASK (input only).
04626 ! NGC    = copy of NG (input only).
04627 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04628 IRT = 0
04629 DO 10 I = 1,NGC
04630 10     JROOT(I) = 0
04631 HMING = (ABS(TN) + ABS(H))*UROUND*100.0D0
04632 !
04633 GOTO (100, 200, 300), JOB
04634 !
04635 ! Evaluate g at initial T, and check for zero values. ------------------
04636 100  CONTINUE
04637 T0 = TN
04638 CALL G (NEQ, T0, Y, NGC, G0)
04639 NGE = 1
04640 ZROOT = .FALSE.
04641 DO 110 I = 1,NGC
04642 110    IF (ABS(G0(I)) .LE. 0.0D0) ZROOT = .TRUE.
04643 IF (.NOT. ZROOT) GOTO 190
04644 ! g has a zero at T.  Look at g at T + (small increment). --------------
04645 TEMP2 = MAX(HMING/ABS(H), 0.1D0)
04646 TEMP1 = TEMP2*H
04647 T0 = T0 + TEMP1
04648 DO 120 I = 1,N
04649 120    Y(I) = Y(I) + TEMP2*YH(I,2)
04650 CALL G (NEQ, T0, Y, NGC, G0)
04651 NGE = NGE + 1
04652 ZROOT = .FALSE.
04653 DO 130 I = 1,NGC
04654 130    IF (ABS(G0(I)) .LE. 0.0D0) ZROOT = .TRUE.
04655 IF (.NOT. ZROOT) GOTO 190
04656 ! g has a zero at T and also close to T.  Take error return. -----------
04657 IRT = -1
04658 RETURN
04659 !
04660 190  CONTINUE
04661 RETURN
04662 !
04663 !
04664 200  CONTINUE
04665 IF (IRFND .EQ. 0) GOTO 260
04666 ! If a root was found on the previous step, evaluate G0 = g(T0). -------
04667 CALL DINTDY (T0, 0, YH, NYH, Y, IFLAG)
04668 CALL G (NEQ, T0, Y, NGC, G0)
04669 NGE = NGE + 1
04670 ZROOT = .FALSE.
04671 DO 210 I = 1,NGC
04672 210    IF (ABS(G0(I)) .LE. 0.0D0) ZROOT = .TRUE.
04673 IF (.NOT. ZROOT) GOTO 260
04674 ! g has a zero at T0.  Look at g at T + (small increment). -------------
04675 TEMP1 = SIGN(HMING,H)
04676 T0 = T0 + TEMP1
04677 IF ((T0 - TN)*H .LT. 0.0D0) GOTO 230
04678 TEMP2 = TEMP1/H
04679 DO 220 I = 1,N
04680 220    Y(I) = Y(I) + TEMP2*YH(I,2)
04681 GOTO 240
04682 230  CALL DINTDY (T0, 0, YH, NYH, Y, IFLAG)
04683 240  CALL G (NEQ, T0, Y, NGC, G0)
04684 NGE = NGE + 1
04685 ZROOT = .FALSE.
04686 DO 250 I = 1,NGC
04687 IF (ABS(G0(I)) .GT. 0.0D0) GOTO 250
04688 JROOT(I) = 1
04689 ZROOT = .TRUE.
04690 250    CONTINUE
04691 IF (.NOT. ZROOT) GOTO 260
04692 ! g has a zero at T0 and also close to T0.  Return root. ---------------
04693 IRT = 1
04694 RETURN
04695 ! G0 has no zero components.  Proceed to check relevant interval. ------
04696 260  IF (TN .EQ. TLAST) GOTO 390
04697 !
04698 300  CONTINUE
04699 ! Set T1 to TN or TOUTC, whichever comes first, and get g at T1. -------
04700 IF (ITASKC.EQ.2 .OR. ITASKC.EQ.3 .OR. ITASKC.EQ.5) GOTO 310
04701 IF ((TOUTC - TN)*H .GE. 0.0D0) GOTO 310
04702 T1 = TOUTC
04703 IF ((T1 - T0)*H .LE. 0.0D0) GOTO 390
04704 CALL DINTDY (T1, 0, YH, NYH, Y, IFLAG)
04705 GOTO 330
04706 310  T1 = TN
04707 DO 320 I = 1,N
04708 320    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
04709 330  CALL G (NEQ, T1, Y, NGC, G1)
04710 NGE = NGE + 1
04711 ! Call DROOTS to search for root in interval from T0 to T1. ------------
04712 JFLAG = 0
04713 350  CONTINUE
04714 CALL DROOTS (NGC, HMING, JFLAG, T0, T1, G0, G1, GX, X, JROOT)
04715 IF (JFLAG .GT. 1) GOTO 360
04716 CALL DINTDY (X, 0, YH, NYH, Y, IFLAG)
04717 CALL G (NEQ, X, Y, NGC, GX)
04718 NGE = NGE + 1
04719 GOTO 350
04720 360  T0 = X
04721 CALL DCOPY (NGC, GX, 1, G0, 1)
04722 IF (JFLAG .EQ. 4) GOTO 390
04723 ! Found a root.  Interpolate to X and return. --------------------------
04724 CALL DINTDY (X, 0, YH, NYH, Y, IFLAG)
04725 IRT = 1
04726 RETURN
04727 !
04728 390  CONTINUE
04729 RETURN
04730 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DRCHEK ----------------------
04731 END
04732 
04733 SUBROUTINE DROOTS (NG, HMIN, JFLAG, X0, X1, G0, G1, GX, X, JROOT)
04734 INTEGER NG, JFLAG, JROOT
04735 DOUBLE PRECISION HMIN, X0, X1, G0, G1, GX, X
04736 DIMENSION G0(NG), G1(NG), GX(NG), JROOT(NG)
04737 INTEGER IOWND3, IMAX, LAST, IDUM3
04738 DOUBLE PRECISION ALPHA, X2, RDUM3
04739 COMMON /DLSR01/ ALPHA, X2, RDUM3(3), IOWND3(3), IMAX, LAST, IDUM3(4)
04740 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04741 ! This subroutine finds the leftmost root of a set of arbitrary
04742 ! functions gi(x) (i = 1,...,NG) in an interval (X0,X1).  Only roots
04743 ! of odd multiplicity (i.e. changes of sign of the gi) are found.
04744 ! Here the sign of X1 - X0 is arbitrary, but is constant for a given
04745 ! problem, and -leftmost- means nearest to X0.
04746 ! The values of the vector-valued function g(x) = (gi, i=1...NG)
04747 ! are communicated through the call sequence of DROOTS.
04748 ! The method used is the Illinois algorithm.
04749 !
04750 ! Reference:
04751 ! Kathie L. Hiebert and Lawrence F. Shampine, Implicitly Defined
04752 ! Output Points for Solutions of ODEs, Sandia Report SAND80-0180,
04753 ! February 1980.
04754 !
04755 ! Description of parameters.
04756 !
04757 ! NG     = number of functions gi, or the number of components of
04758 !          the vector valued function g(x).  Input only.
04759 !
04760 ! HMIN   = resolution parameter in X.  Input only.  When a root is
04761 !          found, it is located only to within an error of HMIN in X.
04762 !          Typically, HMIN should be set to something on the order of
04763 !               100 * UROUND * MAX(ABS(X0),ABS(X1)),
04764 !          where UROUND is the unit roundoff of the machine.
04765 !
04766 ! JFLAG  = integer flag for input and output communication.
04767 !
04768 !          On input, set JFLAG = 0 on the first call for the problem,
04769 !          and leave it unchanged until the problem is completed.
04770 !          (The problem is completed when JFLAG .ge. 2 on return.)
04771 !
04772 !          On output, JFLAG has the following values and meanings:
04773 !          JFLAG = 1 means DROOTS needs a value of g(x).  Set GX = g(X)
04774 !                    and call DROOTS again.
04775 !          JFLAG = 2 means a root has been found.  The root is
04776 !                    at X, and GX contains g(X).  (Actually, X is the
04777 !                    rightmost approximation to the root on an interval
04778 !                    (X0,X1) of size HMIN or less.)
04779 !          JFLAG = 3 means X = X1 is a root, with one or more of the gi
04780 !                    being zero at X1 and no sign changes in (X0,X1).
04781 !                    GX contains g(X) on output.
04782 !          JFLAG = 4 means no roots (of odd multiplicity) were
04783 !                    found in (X0,X1) (no sign changes).
04784 !
04785 ! X0,X1  = endpoints of the interval where roots are sought.
04786 !          X1 and X0 are input when JFLAG = 0 (first call), and
04787 !          must be left unchanged between calls until the problem is
04788 !          completed.  X0 and X1 must be distinct, but X1 - X0 may be
04789 !          of either sign.  However, the notion of -left- and -right-
04790 !          will be used to mean nearer to X0 or X1, respectively.
04791 !          When JFLAG .ge. 2 on return, X0 and X1 are output, and
04792 !          are the endpoints of the relevant interval.
04793 !
04794 ! G0,G1  = arrays of length NG containing the vectors g(X0) and g(X1),
04795 !          respectively.  When JFLAG = 0, G0 and G1 are input and
04796 !          none of the G0(i) should be zero.
04797 !          When JFLAG .ge. 2 on return, G0 and G1 are output.
04798 !
04799 ! GX     = array of length NG containing g(X).  GX is input
04800 !          when JFLAG = 1, and output when JFLAG .ge. 2.
04801 !
04802 ! X      = independent variable value.  Output only.
04803 !          When JFLAG = 1 on output, X is the point at which g(x)
04804 !          is to be evaluated and loaded into GX.
04805 !          When JFLAG = 2 or 3, X is the root.
04806 !          When JFLAG = 4, X is the right endpoint of the interval, X1.
04807 !
04808 ! JROOT  = integer array of length NG.  Output only.
04809 !          When JFLAG = 2 or 3, JROOT indicates which components
04810 !          of g(x) have a root at X.  JROOT(i) is 1 if the i-th
04811 !          component has a root, and JROOT(i) = 0 otherwise.
04812 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04813 INTEGER I, IMXOLD, NXLAST
04814 DOUBLE PRECISION T2, TMAX, FRACINT, FRACSUB, ZERO,HALF,TENTH,FIVE
04815 LOGICAL ZROOT, SGNCHG, XROOT
04816 SAVE ZERO, HALF, TENTH, FIVE
04817 DATA ZERO/0.0D0/, HALF/0.5D0/, TENTH/0.1D0/, FIVE/5.0D0/
04818 !
04819 IF (JFLAG .EQ. 1) GOTO 200
04820 ! JFLAG .ne. 1.  Check for change in sign of g or zero at X1. ----------
04821 IMAX = 0
04822 TMAX = ZERO
04823 ZROOT = .FALSE.
04824 DO 120 I = 1,NG
04825 IF (ABS(G1(I)) .GT. ZERO) GOTO 110
04826 ZROOT = .TRUE.
04827 GOTO 120
04828 ! At this point, G0(i) has been checked and cannot be zero. ------------
04829 110    IF (SIGN(1.0D0,G0(I)) .EQ. SIGN(1.0D0,G1(I))) GOTO 120
04830 T2 = ABS(G1(I)/(G1(I)-G0(I)))
04831 IF (T2 .LE. TMAX) GOTO 120
04832 TMAX = T2
04833 IMAX = I
04834 120    CONTINUE
04835 IF (IMAX .GT. 0) GOTO 130
04836 SGNCHG = .FALSE.
04837 GOTO 140
04838 130  SGNCHG = .TRUE.
04839 140  IF (.NOT. SGNCHG) GOTO 400
04840 ! There is a sign change.  Find the first root in the interval. --------
04841 XROOT = .FALSE.
04842 NXLAST = 0
04843 LAST = 1
04844 !
04845 ! Repeat until the first root in the interval is found.  Loop point. ---
04846 150  CONTINUE
04847 IF (XROOT) GOTO 300
04848 IF (NXLAST .EQ. LAST) GOTO 160
04849 ALPHA = 1.0D0
04850 GOTO 180
04851 160  IF (LAST .EQ. 0) GOTO 170
04852 ALPHA = 0.5D0*ALPHA
04853 GOTO 180
04854 170  ALPHA = 2.0D0*ALPHA
04855 180  X2 = X1 - (X1 - X0)*G1(IMAX) / (G1(IMAX) - ALPHA*G0(IMAX))
04856 ! If X2 is too close to X0 or X1, adjust it inward, by a fractional ----
04857 ! distance that is between 0.1 and 0.5. --------------------------------
04858 IF (ABS(X2 - X0) < HALF*HMIN) THEN
04859 FRACINT = ABS(X1 - X0)/HMIN
04860 FRACSUB = TENTH
04861 IF (FRACINT .LE. FIVE) FRACSUB = HALF/FRACINT
04862 X2 = X0 + FRACSUB*(X1 - X0)
04863 ENDIF
04864 IF (ABS(X1 - X2) < HALF*HMIN) THEN
04865 FRACINT = ABS(X1 - X0)/HMIN
04866 FRACSUB = TENTH
04867 IF (FRACINT .LE. FIVE) FRACSUB = HALF/FRACINT
04868 X2 = X1 - FRACSUB*(X1 - X0)
04869 ENDIF
04870 JFLAG = 1
04871 X = X2
04872 ! Return to the calling routine to get a value of GX = g(X). -----------
04873 RETURN
04874 ! Check to see in which interval g changes sign. -----------------------
04875 200  IMXOLD = IMAX
04876 IMAX = 0
04877 TMAX = ZERO
04878 ZROOT = .FALSE.
04879 DO 220 I = 1,NG
04880 IF (ABS(GX(I)) .GT. ZERO) GOTO 210
04881 ZROOT = .TRUE.
04882 GOTO 220
04883 ! Neither G0(i) nor GX(i) can be zero at this point. -------------------
04884 210    IF (SIGN(1.0D0,G0(I)) .EQ. SIGN(1.0D0,GX(I))) GOTO 220
04885 T2 = ABS(GX(I)/(GX(I) - G0(I)))
04886 IF (T2 .LE. TMAX) GOTO 220
04887 TMAX = T2
04888 IMAX = I
04889 220    CONTINUE
04890 IF (IMAX .GT. 0) GOTO 230
04891 SGNCHG = .FALSE.
04892 IMAX = IMXOLD
04893 GOTO 240
04894 230  SGNCHG = .TRUE.
04895 240  NXLAST = LAST
04896 IF (.NOT. SGNCHG) GOTO 250
04897 ! Sign change between X0 and X2, so replace X1 with X2. ----------------
04898 X1 = X2
04899 CALL DCOPY (NG, GX, 1, G1, 1)
04900 LAST = 1
04901 XROOT = .FALSE.
04902 GOTO 270
04903 250  IF (.NOT. ZROOT) GOTO 260
04904 ! Zero value at X2 and no sign change in (X0,X2), so X2 is a root. -----
04905 X1 = X2
04906 CALL DCOPY (NG, GX, 1, G1, 1)
04907 XROOT = .TRUE.
04908 GOTO 270
04909 ! No sign change between X0 and X2.  Replace X0 with X2. ---------------
04910 260  CONTINUE
04911 CALL DCOPY (NG, GX, 1, G0, 1)
04912 X0 = X2
04913 LAST = 0
04914 XROOT = .FALSE.
04915 270  IF (ABS(X1-X0) .LE. HMIN) XROOT = .TRUE.
04916 GOTO 150
04917 !
04918 ! Return with X1 as the root.  Set JROOT.  Set X = X1 and GX = G1. -----
04919 300  JFLAG = 2
04920 X = X1
04921 CALL DCOPY (NG, G1, 1, GX, 1)
04922 DO 320 I = 1,NG
04923 JROOT(I) = 0
04924 IF (ABS(G1(I)) .GT. ZERO) GOTO 310
04925 JROOT(I) = 1
04926 GOTO 320
04927 310    IF (SIGN(1.0D0,G0(I)) .NE. SIGN(1.0D0,G1(I))) JROOT(I) = 1
04928 320    CONTINUE
04929 RETURN
04930 !
04931 ! No sign change in the interval.  Check for zero at right endpoint. ---
04932 400  IF (.NOT. ZROOT) GOTO 420
04933 !
04934 ! Zero value at X1 and no sign change in (X0,X1).  Return JFLAG = 3. ---
04935 X = X1
04936 CALL DCOPY (NG, G1, 1, GX, 1)
04937 DO 410 I = 1,NG
04938 JROOT(I) = 0
04939 IF (ABS(G1(I)) .LE. ZERO) JROOT (I) = 1
04940 410  CONTINUE
04941 JFLAG = 3
04942 RETURN
04943 !
04944 ! No sign changes in this interval.  Set X = X1, return JFLAG = 4. -----
04945 420  CALL DCOPY (NG, G1, 1, GX, 1)
04946 X = X1
04947 JFLAG = 4
04948 RETURN
04949 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DROOTS ----------------------
04950 END
04951 
04952 SUBROUTINE DSRCAR (RSAV, ISAV, JOB)
04953 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04954 ! This routine saves or restores (depending on JOB) the contents of
04955 ! the Common blocks DLS001, DLSA01, DLSR01, which are used
04956 ! internally by one or more ODEPACK solvers.
04957 !
04958 ! RSAV = real array of length 245 or more.
04959 ! ISAV = integer array of length 55 or more.
04960 ! JOB  = flag indicating to save or restore the Common blocks:
04961 !        JOB  = 1 if Common is to be saved (written to RSAV/ISAV)
04962 !        JOB  = 2 if Common is to be restored (read from RSAV/ISAV)
04963 !        A call with JOB = 2 presumes a prior call with JOB = 1.
04964 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
04965 INTEGER ISAV, JOB
04966 INTEGER ILS, ILSA, ILSR
04967 INTEGER I, IOFF, LENRLS, LENILS, LENRLA, LENILA, LENRLR, LENILR
04968 DOUBLE PRECISION RSAV
04969 DOUBLE PRECISION RLS, RLSA, RLSR
04970 DIMENSION RSAV(*), ISAV(*)
04971 SAVE LENRLS, LENILS, LENRLA, LENILA, LENRLR, LENILR
04972 COMMON /DLS001/ RLS(218), ILS(37)
04973 COMMON /DLSA01/ RLSA(22), ILSA(9)
04974 COMMON /DLSR01/ RLSR(5), ILSR(9)
04975 DATA LENRLS/218/, LENILS/37/, LENRLA/22/, LENILA/9/
04976 DATA LENRLR/5/, LENILR/9/
04977 !
04978 IF (JOB .EQ. 2) GOTO 100
04979 DO 10 I = 1,LENRLS
04980 10     RSAV(I) = RLS(I)
04981 DO 15 I = 1,LENRLA
04982 15     RSAV(LENRLS+I) = RLSA(I)
04983 IOFF = LENRLS + LENRLA
04984 DO 20 I = 1,LENRLR
04985 20     RSAV(IOFF+I) = RLSR(I)
04986 !
04987 DO 30 I = 1,LENILS
04988 30     ISAV(I) = ILS(I)
04989 DO 35 I = 1,LENILA
04990 35     ISAV(LENILS+I) = ILSA(I)
04991 IOFF = LENILS + LENILA
04992 DO 40 I = 1,LENILR
04993 40     ISAV(IOFF+I) = ILSR(I)
04994 !
04995 RETURN
04996 !
04997 100  CONTINUE
04998 DO 110 I = 1,LENRLS
04999 110     RLS(I) = RSAV(I)
05000 DO 115 I = 1,LENRLA
05001 115     RLSA(I) = RSAV(LENRLS+I)
05002 IOFF = LENRLS + LENRLA
05003 DO 120 I = 1,LENRLR
05004 120     RLSR(I) = RSAV(IOFF+I)
05005 !
05006 DO 130 I = 1,LENILS
05007 130     ILS(I) = ISAV(I)
05008 DO 135 I = 1,LENILA
05009 135     ILSA(I) = ISAV(LENILS+I)
05010 IOFF = LENILS + LENILA
05011 DO 140 I = 1,LENILR
05012 140     ILSR(I) = ISAV(IOFF+I)
05013 !
05014 RETURN
05015 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSRCAR ----------------------
05016 END
05017 
05018 SUBROUTINE DSTODPK (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, SAVX, ACOR, WM, IWM, F, JAC, PSOL)
05019 EXTERNAL F, JAC, PSOL
05020 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
05021 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, SAVX, ACOR, WM
05022 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), YH1(*), EWT(*), SAVF(*), SAVX(*), ACOR(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
05023 INTEGER IOWND, IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM
05024 INTEGER LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05025 INTEGER JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
05026 DOUBLE PRECISION CONIT, CRATE, EL, ELCO, HOLD, RMAX, TESCO, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
05027 DOUBLE PRECISION DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN
05028 COMMON /DLS001/ CONIT, CRATE, EL(13), ELCO(13,12), HOLD, RMAX, TESCO(3,12), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, &
05029 IOWND(6), IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, &
05030 LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05031 COMMON /DLPK01/ DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN, JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
05032 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05033 ! DSTODPK performs one step of the integration of an initial value
05034 ! problem for a system of Ordinary Differential Equations.
05035 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05036 ! The following changes were made to generate Subroutine DSTODPK
05037 ! from Subroutine DSTODE:
05038 ! 1. The array SAVX was added to the call sequence.
05039 ! 2. PJAC and SLVS were replaced by PSOL in the call sequence.
05040 ! 3. The Common block /DLPK01/ was added for communication.
05041 ! 4. The test constant EPCON is loaded into Common below statement
05042 !    numbers 125 and 155, and used below statement 400.
05043 ! 5. The Newton iteration counter MNEWT is set below 220 and 400.
05044 ! 6. The call to PJAC was replaced with a call to DPKSET (fixed name),
05045 !    with a longer call sequence, called depending on JACFLG.
05046 ! 7. The corrector residual is stored in SAVX (not Y) at 360,
05047 !    and the solution vector is in SAVX in the 380 loop.
05048 ! 8. SLVS was renamed DSOLPK and includes NEQ, SAVX, EWT, F, and JAC.
05049 !    SAVX was added because DSOLPK now needs Y and SAVF undisturbed.
05050 ! 9. The nonlinear convergence failure count NCFN is set at 430.
05051 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05052 ! Note: DSTODPK is independent of the value of the iteration method
05053 ! indicator MITER, when this is .ne. 0, and hence is independent
05054 ! of the type of chord method used, or the Jacobian structure.
05055 ! Communication with DSTODPK is done with the following variables:
05056 !
05057 ! NEQ    = integer array containing problem size in NEQ(1), and
05058 !          passed as the NEQ argument in all calls to F and JAC.
05059 ! Y      = an array of length .ge. N used as the Y argument in
05060 !          all calls to F and JAC.
05061 ! YH     = an NYH by LMAX array containing the dependent variables
05062 !          and their approximate scaled derivatives, where
05063 !          LMAX = MAXORD + 1.  YH(i,j+1) contains the approximate
05064 !          j-th derivative of y(i), scaled by H**j/factorial(j)
05065 !          (j = 0,1,...,NQ).  On entry for the first step, the first
05066 !          two columns of YH must be set from the initial values.
05067 ! NYH    = a constant integer .ge. N, the first dimension of YH.
05068 ! YH1    = a one-dimensional array occupying the same space as YH.
05069 ! EWT    = an array of length N containing multiplicative weights
05070 !          for local error measurements.  Local errors in y(i) are
05071 !          compared to 1.0/EWT(i) in various error tests.
05072 ! SAVF   = an array of working storage, of length N.
05073 !          Also used for input of YH(*,MAXORD+2) when JSTART = -1
05074 !          and MAXORD .lt. the current order NQ.
05075 ! SAVX   = an array of working storage, of length N.
05076 ! ACOR   = a work array of length N, used for the accumulated
05077 !          corrections.  On a successful return, ACOR(i) contains
05078 !          the estimated one-step local error in y(i).
05079 ! WM,IWM = real and integer work arrays associated with matrix
05080 !          operations in chord iteration (MITER .ne. 0).
05081 ! CCMAX  = maximum relative change in H*EL0 before DPKSET is called.
05082 ! H      = the step size to be attempted on the next step.
05083 !          H is altered by the error control algorithm during the
05084 !          problem.  H can be either positive or negative, but its
05085 !          sign must remain constant throughout the problem.
05086 ! HMIN   = the minimum absolute value of the step size H to be used.
05087 ! HMXI   = inverse of the maximum absolute value of H to be used.
05088 !          HMXI = 0.0 is allowed and corresponds to an infinite HMAX.
05089 !          HMIN and HMXI may be changed at any time, but will not
05090 !          take effect until the next change of H is considered.
05091 ! TN     = the independent variable. TN is updated on each step taken.
05092 ! JSTART = an integer used for input only, with the following
05093 !          values and meanings:
05094 !               0  perform the first step.
05095 !           .gt.0  take a new step continuing from the last.
05096 !              -1  take the next step with a new value of H, MAXORD,
05097 !                    N, METH, MITER, and/or matrix parameters.
05098 !              -2  take the next step with a new value of H,
05099 !                    but with other inputs unchanged.
05100 !          On return, JSTART is set to 1 to facilitate continuation.
05101 ! KFLAG  = a completion code with the following meanings:
05102 !               0  the step was succesful.
05103 !              -1  the requested error could not be achieved.
05104 !              -2  corrector convergence could not be achieved.
05105 !              -3  fatal error in DPKSET or DSOLPK.
05106 !          A return with KFLAG = -1 or -2 means either
05107 !          ABS(H) = HMIN or 10 consecutive failures occurred.
05108 !          On a return with KFLAG negative, the values of TN and
05109 !          the YH array are as of the beginning of the last
05110 !          step, and H is the last step size attempted.
05111 ! MAXORD = the maximum order of integration method to be allowed.
05112 ! MAXCOR = the maximum number of corrector iterations allowed.
05113 ! MSBP   = maximum number of steps between DPKSET calls (MITER .gt. 0).
05114 ! MXNCF  = maximum number of convergence failures allowed.
05115 ! METH/MITER = the method flags.  See description in driver.
05116 ! N      = the number of first-order differential equations.
05117 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05118 INTEGER I, I1, IREDO, IRET, J, JB, M, NCF, NEWQ
05119 DOUBLE PRECISION DCON, DDN, DEL, DELP, DSM, DUP, EXDN, EXSM, EXUP, R, RH, RHDN, RHSM, RHUP, TOLD, DVNORM
05120 !
05121 KFLAG = 0
05122 TOLD = TN
05123 NCF = 0
05124 IERPJ = 0
05125 IERSL = 0
05126 JCUR = 0
05127 ICF = 0
05128 DELP = 0.0D0
05129 IF (JSTART .GT. 0) GOTO 200
05130 IF (JSTART .EQ. -1) GOTO 100
05131 IF (JSTART .EQ. -2) GOTO 160
05132 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05133 ! On the first call, the order is set to 1, and other variables are
05134 ! initialized.  RMAX is the maximum ratio by which H can be increased
05135 ! in a single step.  It is initially 1.E4 to compensate for the small
05136 ! initial H, but then is normally equal to 10.  If a failure
05137 ! occurs (in corrector convergence or error test), RMAX is set at 2
05138 ! for the next increase.
05139 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05140 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
05141 NQ = 1
05142 L = 2
05143 IALTH = 2
05144 RMAX = 10000.0D0
05145 RC = 0.0D0
05146 EL0 = 1.0D0
05147 CRATE = 0.7D0
05148 HOLD = H
05149 MEO = METH
05150 NSLP = 0
05151 IPUP = MITER
05152 IRET = 3
05153 GOTO 140
05154 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05155 ! The following block handles preliminaries needed when JSTART = -1.
05156 ! IPUP is set to MITER to force a matrix update.
05157 ! If an order increase is about to be considered (IALTH = 1),
05158 ! IALTH is reset to 2 to postpone consideration one more step.
05159 ! If the caller has changed METH, DCFODE is called to reset
05160 ! the coefficients of the method.
05161 ! If the caller has changed MAXORD to a value less than the current
05162 ! order NQ, NQ is reduced to MAXORD, and a new H chosen accordingly.
05163 ! If H is to be changed, YH must be rescaled.
05164 ! If H or METH is being changed, IALTH is reset to L = NQ + 1
05165 ! to prevent further changes in H for that many steps.
05166 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05167 100  IPUP = MITER
05168 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
05169 IF (IALTH .EQ. 1) IALTH = 2
05170 IF (METH .EQ. MEO) GOTO 110
05171 CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
05172 MEO = METH
05173 IF (NQ .GT. MAXORD) GOTO 120
05174 IALTH = L
05175 IRET = 1
05176 GOTO 150
05177 110  IF (NQ .LE. MAXORD) GOTO 160
05178 120  NQ = MAXORD
05179 L = LMAX
05180 DO 125 I = 1,L
05181 125    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
05182 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
05183 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
05184 EL0 = EL(1)
05185 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
05186 EPCON = CONIT*TESCO(2,NQ)
05187 DDN = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(1,L)
05188 EXDN = 1.0D0/L
05189 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
05190 RH = MIN(RHDN,1.0D0)
05191 IREDO = 3
05192 IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 170
05193 RH = MIN(RH,ABS(H/HOLD))
05194 H = HOLD
05195 GOTO 175
05196 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05197 ! DCFODE is called to get all the integration coefficients for the
05198 ! current METH.  Then the EL vector and related constants are reset
05199 ! whenever the order NQ is changed, or at the start of the problem.
05200 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05201 140  CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
05202 150  DO 155 I = 1,L
05203 155    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
05204 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
05205 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
05206 EL0 = EL(1)
05207 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
05208 EPCON = CONIT*TESCO(2,NQ)
05209 GOTO (160, 170, 200), IRET
05210 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05211 ! If H is being changed, the H ratio RH is checked against
05212 ! RMAX, HMIN, and HMXI, and the YH array rescaled.  IALTH is set to
05213 ! L = NQ + 1 to prevent a change of H for that many steps, unless
05214 ! forced by a convergence or error test failure.
05215 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05216 160  IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 200
05217 RH = H/HOLD
05218 H = HOLD
05219 IREDO = 3
05220 GOTO 175
05221 170  RH = MAX(RH,HMIN/ABS(H))
05222 175  RH = MIN(RH,RMAX)
05223 RH = RH/MAX(1.0D0,ABS(H)*HMXI*RH)
05224 R = 1.0D0
05225 DO 180 J = 2,L
05226 R = R*RH
05227 DO 180 I = 1,N
05228 180      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J)*R
05229 H = H*RH
05230 RC = RC*RH
05231 IALTH = L
05232 IF (IREDO .EQ. 0) GOTO 690
05233 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05234 ! This section computes the predicted values by effectively
05235 ! multiplying the YH array by the Pascal triangle matrix.
05236 ! The flag IPUP is set according to whether matrix data is involved
05237 ! (JACFLG .ne. 0) or not (JACFLG = 0), to trigger a call to DPKSET.
05238 ! IPUP is set to MITER when RC differs from 1 by more than CCMAX,
05239 ! and at least every MSBP steps, when JACFLG = 1.
05240 ! RC is the ratio of new to old values of the coefficient  H*EL(1).
05241 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05242 200  IF (JACFLG .NE. 0) GOTO 202
05243 IPUP = 0
05244 CRATE = 0.7D0
05245 GOTO 205
05246 202  IF (ABS(RC-1.0D0) .GT. CCMAX) IPUP = MITER
05247 IF (NST .GE. NSLP+MSBP) IPUP = MITER
05248 205  TN = TN + H
05249 I1 = NQNYH + 1
05250 DO 215 JB = 1,NQ
05251 I1 = I1 - NYH
05252 !DIR$ IVDEP
05253 DO 210 I = I1,NQNYH
05254 210      YH1(I) = YH1(I) + YH1(I+NYH)
05255 215    CONTINUE
05256 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05257 ! Up to MAXCOR corrector iterations are taken.  A convergence test is
05258 ! made on the RMS-norm of each correction, weighted by the error
05259 ! weight vector EWT.  The sum of the corrections is accumulated in the
05260 ! vector ACOR(i).  The YH array is not altered in the corrector loop.
05261 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05262 220  M = 0
05263 MNEWT = 0
05264 DO 230 I = 1,N
05265 230    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
05266 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
05267 NFE = NFE + 1
05268 IF (IPUP .LE. 0) GOTO 250
05269 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05270 ! If indicated, DPKSET is called to update any matrix data needed,
05271 ! before starting the corrector iteration.
05272 ! IPUP is set to 0 as an indicator that this has been done.
05273 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05274 CALL DPKSET (NEQ, Y, YH1, EWT, ACOR, SAVF, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
05275 IPUP = 0
05276 RC = 1.0D0
05277 NSLP = NST
05278 CRATE = 0.7D0
05279 IF (IERPJ .NE. 0) GOTO 430
05280 250  DO 260 I = 1,N
05281 260    ACOR(I) = 0.0D0
05282 270  IF (MITER .NE. 0) GOTO 350
05283 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05284 ! In the case of functional iteration, update Y directly from
05285 ! the result of the last function evaluation.
05286 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05287 DO 290 I = 1,N
05288 SAVF(I) = H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2)
05289 290    Y(I) = SAVF(I) - ACOR(I)
05290 DEL = DVNORM (N, Y, EWT)
05291 DO 300 I = 1,N
05292 Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*SAVF(I)
05293 300    ACOR(I) = SAVF(I)
05294 GOTO 400
05295 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05296 ! In the case of the chord method, compute the corrector error,
05297 ! and solve the linear system with that as right-hand side and
05298 ! P as coefficient matrix.
05299 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05300 350  DO 360 I = 1,N
05301 360    SAVX(I) = H*SAVF(I) - (YH(I,2) + ACOR(I))
05302 CALL DSOLPK (NEQ, Y, SAVF, SAVX, EWT, WM, IWM, F, PSOL)
05303 IF (IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 430
05304 IF (IERSL .GT. 0) GOTO 410
05305 DEL = DVNORM (N, SAVX, EWT)
05306 DO 380 I = 1,N
05307 ACOR(I) = ACOR(I) + SAVX(I)
05308 380    Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*ACOR(I)
05309 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05310 ! Test for convergence.  If M .gt. 0, an estimate of the convergence
05311 ! rate constant is stored in CRATE, and this is used in the test.
05312 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05313 400  IF (M .NE. 0) CRATE = MAX(0.2D0*CRATE,DEL/DELP)
05314 DCON = DEL*MIN(1.0D0,1.5D0*CRATE)/EPCON
05315 IF (DCON .LE. 1.0D0) GOTO 450
05316 M = M + 1
05317 IF (M .EQ. MAXCOR) GOTO 410
05318 IF (M .GE. 2 .AND. DEL .GT. 2.0D0*DELP) GOTO 410
05319 MNEWT = M
05320 DELP = DEL
05321 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
05322 NFE = NFE + 1
05323 GOTO 270
05324 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05325 ! The corrector iteration failed to converge.
05326 ! If MITER .ne. 0 and the Jacobian is out of date, DPKSET is called for
05327 ! the next try.  Otherwise the YH array is retracted to its values
05328 ! before prediction, and H is reduced, if possible.  If H cannot be
05329 ! reduced or MXNCF failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -2.
05330 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05331 410  IF (MITER.EQ.0 .OR. JCUR.EQ.1 .OR. JACFLG.EQ.0) GOTO 430
05332 ICF = 1
05333 IPUP = MITER
05334 GOTO 220
05335 430  ICF = 2
05336 NCF = NCF + 1
05337 NCFN = NCFN + 1
05338 RMAX = 2.0D0
05339 TN = TOLD
05340 I1 = NQNYH + 1
05341 DO 445 JB = 1,NQ
05342 I1 = I1 - NYH
05343 !DIR$ IVDEP
05344 DO 440 I = I1,NQNYH
05345 440      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
05346 445    CONTINUE
05347 IF (IERPJ .LT. 0 .OR. IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 680
05348 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 670
05349 IF (NCF .EQ. MXNCF) GOTO 670
05350 RH = 0.5D0
05351 IPUP = MITER
05352 IREDO = 1
05353 GOTO 170
05354 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05355 ! The corrector has converged.  JCUR is set to 0
05356 ! to signal that the Jacobian involved may need updating later.
05357 ! The local error test is made and control passes to statement 500
05358 ! if it fails.
05359 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05360 450  JCUR = 0
05361 IF (M .EQ. 0) DSM = DEL/TESCO(2,NQ)
05362 IF (M .GT. 0) DSM = DVNORM (N, ACOR, EWT)/TESCO(2,NQ)
05363 IF (DSM .GT. 1.0D0) GOTO 500
05364 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05365 ! After a successful step, update the YH array.
05366 ! Consider changing H if IALTH = 1.  Otherwise decrease IALTH by 1.
05367 ! If IALTH is then 1 and NQ .lt. MAXORD, then ACOR is saved for
05368 ! use in a possible order increase on the next step.
05369 ! If a change in H is considered, an increase or decrease in order
05370 ! by one is considered also.  A change in H is made only if it is by a
05371 ! factor of at least 1.1.  If not, IALTH is set to 3 to prevent
05372 ! testing for that many steps.
05373 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05374 KFLAG = 0
05375 IREDO = 0
05376 NST = NST + 1
05377 HU = H
05378 NQU = NQ
05379 DO 470 J = 1,L
05380 DO 470 I = 1,N
05381 470      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J) + EL(J)*ACOR(I)
05382 IALTH = IALTH - 1
05383 IF (IALTH .EQ. 0) GOTO 520
05384 IF (IALTH .GT. 1) GOTO 700
05385 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 700
05386 DO 490 I = 1,N
05387 490    YH(I,LMAX) = ACOR(I)
05388 GOTO 700
05389 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05390 ! The error test failed.  KFLAG keeps track of multiple failures.
05391 ! Restore TN and the YH array to their previous values, and prepare
05392 ! to try the step again.  Compute the optimum step size for this or
05393 ! one lower order.  After 2 or more failures, H is forced to decrease
05394 ! by a factor of 0.2 or less.
05395 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05396 500  KFLAG = KFLAG - 1
05397 TN = TOLD
05398 I1 = NQNYH + 1
05399 DO 515 JB = 1,NQ
05400 I1 = I1 - NYH
05401 !DIR$ IVDEP
05402 DO 510 I = I1,NQNYH
05403 510      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
05404 515    CONTINUE
05405 RMAX = 2.0D0
05406 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 660
05407 IF (KFLAG .LE. -3) GOTO 640
05408 IREDO = 2
05409 RHUP = 0.0D0
05410 GOTO 540
05411 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05412 ! Regardless of the success or failure of the step, factors
05413 ! RHDN, RHSM, and RHUP are computed, by which H could be multiplied
05414 ! at order NQ - 1, order NQ, or order NQ + 1, respectively.
05415 ! In the case of failure, RHUP = 0.0 to avoid an order increase.
05416 ! the largest of these is determined and the new order chosen
05417 ! accordingly.  If the order is to be increased, we compute one
05418 ! additional scaled derivative.
05419 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05420 520  RHUP = 0.0D0
05421 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 540
05422 DO 530 I = 1,N
05423 530    SAVF(I) = ACOR(I) - YH(I,LMAX)
05424 DUP = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(3,NQ)
05425 EXUP = 1.0D0/(L+1)
05426 RHUP = 1.0D0/(1.4D0*DUP**EXUP + 0.0000014D0)
05427 540  EXSM = 1.0D0/L
05428 RHSM = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
05429 RHDN = 0.0D0
05430 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 560
05431 DDN = DVNORM (N, YH(1,L), EWT)/TESCO(1,NQ)
05432 EXDN = 1.0D0/NQ
05433 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
05434 560  IF (RHSM .GE. RHUP) GOTO 570
05435 IF (RHUP .GT. RHDN) GOTO 590
05436 GOTO 580
05437 570  IF (RHSM .LT. RHDN) GOTO 580
05438 NEWQ = NQ
05439 RH = RHSM
05440 GOTO 620
05441 580  NEWQ = NQ - 1
05442 RH = RHDN
05443 IF (KFLAG .LT. 0 .AND. RH .GT. 1.0D0) RH = 1.0D0
05444 GOTO 620
05445 590  NEWQ = L
05446 RH = RHUP
05447 IF (RH .LT. 1.1D0) GOTO 610
05448 R = EL(L)/L
05449 DO 600 I = 1,N
05450 600    YH(I,NEWQ+1) = ACOR(I)*R
05451 GOTO 630
05452 610  IALTH = 3
05453 GOTO 700
05454 620  IF ((KFLAG .EQ. 0) .AND. (RH .LT. 1.1D0)) GOTO 610
05455 IF (KFLAG .LE. -2) RH = MIN(RH,0.2D0)
05456 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05457 ! If there is a change of order, reset NQ, L, and the coefficients.
05458 ! In any case H is reset according to RH and the YH array is rescaled.
05459 ! Then exit from 690 if the step was OK, or redo the step otherwise.
05460 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05461 IF (NEWQ .EQ. NQ) GOTO 170
05462 630  NQ = NEWQ
05463 L = NQ + 1
05464 IRET = 2
05465 GOTO 150
05466 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05467 ! Control reaches this section if 3 or more failures have occured.
05468 ! If 10 failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -1.
05469 ! It is assumed that the derivatives that have accumulated in the
05470 ! YH array have errors of the wrong order.  Hence the first
05471 ! derivative is recomputed, and the order is set to 1.  Then
05472 ! H is reduced by a factor of 10, and the step is retried,
05473 ! until it succeeds or H reaches HMIN.
05474 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05475 640  IF (KFLAG .EQ. -10) GOTO 660
05476 RH = 0.1D0
05477 RH = MAX(HMIN/ABS(H),RH)
05478 H = H*RH
05479 DO 645 I = 1,N
05480 645    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
05481 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
05482 NFE = NFE + 1
05483 DO 650 I = 1,N
05484 650    YH(I,2) = H*SAVF(I)
05485 IPUP = MITER
05486 IALTH = 5
05487 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 200
05488 NQ = 1
05489 L = 2
05490 IRET = 3
05491 GOTO 150
05492 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05493 ! All returns are made through this section.  H is saved in HOLD
05494 ! to allow the caller to change H on the next step.
05495 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05496 660  KFLAG = -1
05497 GOTO 720
05498 670  KFLAG = -2
05499 GOTO 720
05500 680  KFLAG = -3
05501 GOTO 720
05502 690  RMAX = 10.0D0
05503 700  R = 1.0D0/TESCO(2,NQU)
05504 DO 710 I = 1,N
05505 710    ACOR(I) = ACOR(I)*R
05506 720  HOLD = H
05507 JSTART = 1
05508 RETURN
05509 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSTODPK ---------------------
05510 END
05511 
05512 SUBROUTINE DPKSET (NEQ, Y, YSV, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
05513 EXTERNAL F, JAC
05514 INTEGER NEQ, IWM
05515 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YSV, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM
05516 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YSV(*), EWT(*), FTEM(*), SAVF(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
05517 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
05518 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05519 INTEGER JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
05520 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
05521 DOUBLE PRECISION DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN
05522 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
05523 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05524 COMMON /DLPK01/ DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN, JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
05525 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05526 ! DPKSET is called by DSTODPK to interface with the user-supplied
05527 ! routine JAC, to compute and process relevant parts of
05528 ! the matrix P = I - H*EL(1)*J , where J is the Jacobian df/dy,
05529 ! as need for preconditioning matrix operations later.
05530 !
05531 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
05532 ! with DPKSET uses the following:
05533 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
05534 ! YSV   = array containing predicted y, to be saved (YH1 in DSTODPK).
05535 ! FTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODPK).
05536 ! SAVF  = array containing f evaluated at predicted y.
05537 ! WM    = real work space for matrices.
05538 !         Space for preconditioning data starts at WM(LOCWP).
05539 ! IWM   = integer work space.
05540 !         Space for preconditioning data starts at IWM(LOCIWP).
05541 ! IERPJ = output error flag,  = 0 if no trouble, .gt. 0 if
05542 !         JAC returned an error flag.
05543 ! JCUR  = output flag = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian matrix
05544 !         (or approximation) is now current.
05545 ! This routine also uses Common variables EL0, H, TN, IERPJ, JCUR, NJE.
05546 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05547 INTEGER IER
05548 DOUBLE PRECISION HL0
05549 !
05550 IERPJ = 0
05551 JCUR = 1
05552 HL0 = EL0*H
05553 CALL JAC (F, NEQ, TN, Y, YSV, EWT, SAVF, FTEM, HL0, WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), IER)
05554 NJE = NJE + 1
05555 IF (IER .EQ. 0) RETURN
05556 IERPJ = 1
05557 RETURN
05558 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPKSET ----------------------
05559 END
05560 
05561 SUBROUTINE DSOLPK (NEQ, Y, SAVF, X, EWT, WM, IWM, F, PSOL)
05562 EXTERNAL F, PSOL
05563 INTEGER NEQ, IWM
05564 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, SAVF, X, EWT, WM
05565 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), X(*), EWT(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
05566 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
05567 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05568 INTEGER JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
05569 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
05570 DOUBLE PRECISION DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN
05571 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
05572 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05573 COMMON /DLPK01/ DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN, JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
05574 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05575 ! This routine interfaces to one of DSPIOM, DSPIGMR, DPCG, DPCGS, or
05576 ! DUSOL, for the solution of the linear system arising from a Newton
05577 ! iteration.  It is called if MITER .ne. 0.
05578 ! In addition to variables described elsewhere,
05579 ! communication with DSOLPK uses the following variables:
05580 ! WM    = real work space containing data for the algorithm
05581 !         (Krylov basis vectors, Hessenberg matrix, etc.)
05582 ! IWM   = integer work space containing data for the algorithm
05583 ! X     = the right-hand side vector on input, and the solution vector
05584 !         on output, of length N.
05585 ! IERSL = output flag (in Common):
05586 !         IERSL =  0 means no trouble occurred.
05587 !         IERSL =  1 means the iterative method failed to converge.
05588 !                    If the preconditioner is out of date, the step
05589 !                    is repeated with a new preconditioner.
05590 !                    Otherwise, the stepsize is reduced (forcing a
05591 !                    new evaluation of the preconditioner) and the
05592 !                    step is repeated.
05593 !         IERSL = -1 means there was a nonrecoverable error in the
05594 !                    iterative solver, and an error exit occurs.
05595 ! This routine also uses the Common variables TN, EL0, H, N, MITER,
05596 ! DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN, MAXL, KMP, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFL,
05597 ! LOCWP, LOCIWP.
05598 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05599 INTEGER IFLAG, LB, LDL, LHES, LIOM, LGMR, LPCG, LP, LQ, LR, LV, LW, LWK, LZ, MAXLP1, NPSL
05600 DOUBLE PRECISION DELTA, HL0
05601 !
05602 IERSL = 0
05603 HL0 = H*EL0
05604 DELTA = DELT*EPCON
05605 GOTO (100, 200, 300, 400, 900, 900, 900, 900, 900), MITER
05606 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05607 ! Use the SPIOM algorithm to solve the linear system P*x = -f.
05608 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05609 100  CONTINUE
05610 LV = 1
05611 LB = LV + N*MAXL
05612 LHES = LB + N
05613 LWK = LHES + MAXL*MAXL
05614 CALL DCOPY (N, X, 1, WM(LB), 1)
05615 CALL DSCAL (N, RSQRTN, EWT, 1)
05616 CALL DSPIOM (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WM(LB), EWT, N, MAXL, KMP, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, WM(LV), WM(LHES), IWM,&
05617 LIOM, WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), WM(LWK), IFLAG)
05618 NNI = NNI + 1
05619 NLI = NLI + LIOM
05620 NPS = NPS + NPSL
05621 CALL DSCAL (N, SQRTN, EWT, 1)
05622 IF (IFLAG .NE. 0) NCFL = NCFL + 1
05623 IF (IFLAG .GE. 2) IERSL = 1
05624 IF (IFLAG .LT. 0) IERSL = -1
05625 RETURN
05626 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05627 ! Use the SPIGMR algorithm to solve the linear system P*x = -f.
05628 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05629 200  CONTINUE
05630 MAXLP1 = MAXL + 1
05631 LV = 1
05632 LB = LV + N*MAXL
05633 LHES = LB + N + 1
05634 LQ = LHES + MAXL*MAXLP1
05635 LWK = LQ + 2*MAXL
05636 LDL = LWK + MIN(1,MAXL-KMP)*N
05637 CALL DCOPY (N, X, 1, WM(LB), 1)
05638 CALL DSCAL (N, RSQRTN, EWT, 1)
05639 CALL DSPIGMR (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WM(LB), EWT, N, MAXL, MAXLP1, KMP, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, WM(LV), &
05640 WM(LHES), WM(LQ), LGMR, WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), WM(LWK), WM(LDL), IFLAG)
05641 NNI = NNI + 1
05642 NLI = NLI + LGMR
05643 NPS = NPS + NPSL
05644 CALL DSCAL (N, SQRTN, EWT, 1)
05645 IF (IFLAG .NE. 0) NCFL = NCFL + 1
05646 IF (IFLAG .GE. 2) IERSL = 1
05647 IF (IFLAG .LT. 0) IERSL = -1
05648 RETURN
05649 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05650 ! Use DPCG to solve the linear system P*x = -f
05651 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05652 300  CONTINUE
05653 LR = 1
05654 LP = LR + N
05655 LW = LP + N
05656 LZ = LW + N
05657 LWK = LZ + N
05658 CALL DCOPY (N, X, 1, WM(LR), 1)
05659 CALL DPCG (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WM(LR), EWT, N, MAXL, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, WM(LP), WM(LW), WM(LZ), LPCG,&
05660 WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), WM(LWK), IFLAG)
05661 NNI = NNI + 1
05662 NLI = NLI + LPCG
05663 NPS = NPS + NPSL
05664 IF (IFLAG .NE. 0) NCFL = NCFL + 1
05665 IF (IFLAG .GE. 2) IERSL = 1
05666 IF (IFLAG .LT. 0) IERSL = -1
05667 RETURN
05668 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05669 ! Use DPCGS to solve the linear system P*x = -f
05670 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05671 400  CONTINUE
05672 LR = 1
05673 LP = LR + N
05674 LW = LP + N
05675 LZ = LW + N
05676 LWK = LZ + N
05677 CALL DCOPY (N, X, 1, WM(LR), 1)
05678 CALL DPCGS (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WM(LR), EWT, N, MAXL, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, WM(LP), WM(LW), WM(LZ), &
05679 LPCG, WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), WM(LWK), IFLAG)
05680 NNI = NNI + 1
05681 NLI = NLI + LPCG
05682 NPS = NPS + NPSL
05683 IF (IFLAG .NE. 0) NCFL = NCFL + 1
05684 IF (IFLAG .GE. 2) IERSL = 1
05685 IF (IFLAG .LT. 0) IERSL = -1
05686 RETURN
05687 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05688 ! Use DUSOL, which interfaces to PSOL, to solve the linear system
05689 ! (no Krylov iteration).
05690 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05691 900  CONTINUE
05692 LB = 1
05693 LWK = LB + N
05694 CALL DCOPY (N, X, 1, WM(LB), 1)
05695 CALL DUSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WM(LB), EWT, N, DELTA, HL0, MNEWT, PSOL, NPSL, X, WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), WM(LWK), IFLAG)
05696 NNI = NNI + 1
05697 NPS = NPS + NPSL
05698 IF (IFLAG .NE. 0) NCFL = NCFL + 1
05699 IF (IFLAG .EQ. 3) IERSL = 1
05700 IF (IFLAG .LT. 0) IERSL = -1
05701 RETURN
05702 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSOLPK ----------------------
05703 END
05704 
05705 SUBROUTINE DSPIOM (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, B, WGHT, N, MAXL, KMP, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, V, HES, IPVT, LIOM, &
05706 WP, IWP, WK, IFLAG)
05707 EXTERNAL F, PSOL
05708 INTEGER NEQ,N,MAXL,KMP,JPRE,MNEWT,NPSL,IPVT,LIOM,IWP,IFLAG
05709 DOUBLE PRECISION TN,Y,SAVF,B,WGHT,DELTA,HL0,X,V,HES,WP,WK
05710 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), B(*), WGHT(*), X(*), V(N,*), HES(MAXL,MAXL), IPVT(*), WP(*), IWP(*), WK(*)
05711 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
