05712 ! This routine solves the linear system A * x = b using a scaled
05713 ! preconditioned version of the Incomplete Orthogonalization Method.
05714 ! An initial guess of x = 0 is assumed.
05715 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05716 !
05717 !      On entry
05718 !
05719 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
05720 !
05721 !           TN = current value of t.
05722 !
05723 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
05724 !
05725 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
05726 !
05727 !         B    = the right hand side of the system A*x = b.
05728 !                B is also used as work space when computing the
05729 !                final approximation.
05730 !                (B is the same as V(*,MAXL+1) in the call to DSPIOM.)
05731 !
05732 !         WGHT = array of length N containing scale factors.
05733 !                1/WGHT(i) are the diagonal elements of the diagonal
05734 !                scaling matrix D.
05735 !
05736 !         N    = the order of the matrix A, and the lengths
05737 !                of the vectors Y, SAVF, B, WGHT, and X.
05738 !
05739 !         MAXL = the maximum allowable order of the matrix HES.
05740 !
05741 !          KMP = the number of previous vectors the new vector VNEW
05742 !                must be made orthogonal to.  KMP .le. MAXL.
05743 !
05744 !        DELTA = tolerance on residuals b - A*x in weighted RMS-norm.
05745 !
05746 !          HL0 = current value of (step size h) * (coefficient l0).
05747 !
05748 !         JPRE = preconditioner type flag.
05749 !
05750 !        MNEWT = Newton iteration counter (.ge. 0).
05751 !
05752 !           WK = real work array of length N used by DATV and PSOL.
05753 !
05754 !           WP = real work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
05755 !
05756 !          IWP = integer work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
05757 !
05758 !      On return
05759 !
05760 !         X    = the final computed approximation to the solution
05761 !                of the system A*x = b.
05762 !
05763 !         V    = the N by (LIOM+1) array containing the LIOM
05764 !                orthogonal vectors V(*,1) to V(*,LIOM).
05765 !
05766 !         HES  = the LU factorization of the LIOM by LIOM upper
05767 !                Hessenberg matrix whose entries are the
05768 !                scaled inner products of A*V(*,k) and V(*,i).
05769 !
05770 !         IPVT = an integer array containg pivoting information.
05771 !                It is loaded in DHEFA and used in DHESL.
05772 !
05773 !         LIOM = the number of iterations performed, and current
05774 !                order of the upper Hessenberg matrix HES.
05775 !
05776 !         NPSL = the number of calls to PSOL.
05777 !
05778 !        IFLAG = integer error flag:
05779 !                0 means convergence in LIOM iterations, LIOM.le.MAXL.
05780 !                1 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
05781 !                  iterations, but the residual norm is .lt. 1,
05782 !                  or .lt. norm(b) if MNEWT = 0, and so X is computed.
05783 !                2 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
05784 !                  iterations, residual .gt. 1, and X is undefined.
05785 !                3 means there was a recoverable error in PSOL
05786 !                  caused by the preconditioner being out of date.
05787 !               -1 means there was a nonrecoverable error in PSOL.
05788 !
05789 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05790 INTEGER I, IER, INFO, J, K, LL, LM1
05791 DOUBLE PRECISION BNRM, BNRM0, PROD, RHO, SNORMW, DNRM2, TEM
05792 !
05793 IFLAG = 0
05794 LIOM = 0
05795 NPSL = 0
05796 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05797 ! The initial residual is the vector b.  Apply scaling to b, and test
05798 ! for an immediate return with X = 0 or X = b.
05799 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05800 DO 10 I = 1,N
05801 10     V(I,1) = B(I)*WGHT(I)
05802 BNRM0 = DNRM2 (N, V, 1)
05803 BNRM = BNRM0
05804 IF (BNRM0 .GT. DELTA) GOTO 30
05805 IF (MNEWT .GT. 0) GOTO 20
05806 CALL DCOPY (N, B, 1, X, 1)
05807 RETURN
05808 20   DO 25 I = 1,N
05809 25     X(I) = 0.0D0
05810 RETURN
05811 30   CONTINUE
05812 ! Apply inverse of left preconditioner to vector b. --------------------
05813 IER = 0
05814 IF (JPRE .EQ. 0 .OR. JPRE .EQ. 2) GOTO 55
05815 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, B, 1, IER)
05816 NPSL = 1
05817 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 300
05818 ! Calculate norm of scaled vector V(*,1) and normalize it. -------------
05819 DO 50 I = 1,N
05820 50     V(I,1) = B(I)*WGHT(I)
05821 BNRM = DNRM2(N, V, 1)
05822 DELTA = DELTA*(BNRM/BNRM0)
05823 55   TEM = 1.0D0/BNRM
05824 CALL DSCAL (N, TEM, V(1,1), 1)
05825 ! Zero out the HES array. ----------------------------------------------
05826 DO 65 J = 1,MAXL
05827 DO 60 I = 1,MAXL
05828 60       HES(I,J) = 0.0D0
05829 65     CONTINUE
05830 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05831 ! Main loop on LL = l to compute the vectors V(*,2) to V(*,MAXL).
05832 ! The running product PROD is needed for the convergence test.
05833 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05834 PROD = 1.0D0
05835 DO 90 LL = 1,MAXL
05836 LIOM = LL
05837 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05838 ! Call routine DATV to compute VNEW = Abar*v(l), where Abar is
05839 ! the matrix A with scaling and inverse preconditioner factors applied.
05840 ! Call routine DORTHOG to orthogonalize the new vector vnew = V(*,l+1).
05841 ! Call routine DHEFA to update the factors of HES.
05842 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05843 CALL DATV (NEQ, Y, SAVF, V(1,LL), WGHT, X, F, PSOL, V(1,LL+1), WK, WP, IWP, HL0, JPRE, IER, NPSL)
05844 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 300
05845 CALL DORTHOG (V(1,LL+1), V, HES, N, LL, MAXL, KMP, SNORMW)
05846 CALL DHEFA (HES, MAXL, LL, IPVT, INFO, LL)
05847 LM1 = LL - 1
05848 IF (LL .GT. 1 .AND. IPVT(LM1) .EQ. LM1) PROD = PROD*HES(LL,LM1)
05849 IF (INFO .NE. LL) GOTO 70
05850 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05851 ! The last pivot in HES was found to be zero.
05852 ! If vnew = 0 or l = MAXL, take an error return with IFLAG = 2.
05853 ! otherwise, continue the iteration without a convergence test.
05854 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05855 IF (SNORMW .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 120
05856 IF (LL .EQ. MAXL) GOTO 120
05857 GOTO 80
05858 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05859 ! Update RHO, the estimate of the norm of the residual b - A*x(l).
05860 ! test for convergence.  If passed, compute approximation x(l).
05861 ! If failed and l .lt. MAXL, then continue iterating.
05862 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05863 70     CONTINUE
05864 RHO = BNRM*SNORMW*ABS(PROD/HES(LL,LL))
05865 IF (RHO .LE. DELTA) GOTO 200
05866 IF (LL .EQ. MAXL) GOTO 100
05867 ! If l .lt. MAXL, store HES(l+1,l) and normalize the vector v(*,l+1).
05868 80     CONTINUE
05869 HES(LL+1,LL) = SNORMW
05870 TEM = 1.0D0/SNORMW
05871 CALL DSCAL (N, TEM, V(1,LL+1), 1)
05872 90     CONTINUE
05873 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05874 ! l has reached MAXL without passing the convergence test:
05875 ! If RHO is not too large, compute a solution anyway and return with
05876 ! IFLAG = 1.  Otherwise return with IFLAG = 2.
05877 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05878 100  CONTINUE
05879 IF (RHO .LE. 1.0D0) GOTO 150
05880 IF (RHO .LE. BNRM .AND. MNEWT .EQ. 0) GOTO 150
05881 120  CONTINUE
05882 IFLAG = 2
05883 RETURN
05884 150  IFLAG = 1
05885 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05886 ! Compute the approximation x(l) to the solution.
05887 ! Since the vector X was used as work space, and the initial guess
05888 ! of the Newton correction is zero, X must be reset to zero.
05889 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05890 200  CONTINUE
05891 LL = LIOM
05892 DO 210 K = 1,LL
05893 210    B(K) = 0.0D0
05894 B(1) = BNRM
05895 CALL DHESL (HES, MAXL, LL, IPVT, B)
05896 DO 220 K = 1,N
05897 220    X(K) = 0.0D0
05898 DO 230 I = 1,LL
05899 CALL DAXPY (N, B(I), V(1,I), 1, X, 1)
05900 230    CONTINUE
05901 DO 240 I = 1,N
05902 240    X(I) = X(I)/WGHT(I)
05903 IF (JPRE .LE. 1) RETURN
05904 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, X, 2, IER)
05905 NPSL = NPSL + 1
05906 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 300
05907 RETURN
05908 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05909 ! This block handles error returns forced by routine PSOL.
05910 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05911 300  CONTINUE
05912 IF (IER .LT. 0) IFLAG = -1
05913 IF (IER .GT. 0) IFLAG = 3
05914 RETURN
05915 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSPIOM ----------------------
05916 END
05917 
05918 SUBROUTINE DATV (NEQ, Y, SAVF, V, WGHT, FTEM, F, PSOL, Z, VTEM, WP, IWP, HL0, JPRE, IER, NPSL)
05919 EXTERNAL F, PSOL
05920 INTEGER NEQ, IWP, JPRE, IER, NPSL
05921 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, SAVF, V, WGHT, FTEM, Z, VTEM, WP, HL0
05922 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), V(*), WGHT(*), FTEM(*), Z(*), VTEM(*), WP(*), IWP(*)
05923 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
05924 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05925 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
05926 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
05927 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
05928 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05929 ! This routine computes the product
05930 !
05931 !   (D-inverse)*(P1-inverse)*(I - hl0*df/dy)*(P2-inverse)*(D*v),
05932 !
05933 ! where D is a diagonal scaling matrix, and P1 and P2 are the
05934 ! left and right preconditioning matrices, respectively.
05935 ! v is assumed to have WRMS norm equal to 1.
05936 ! The product is stored in z.  This is computed by a
05937 ! difference quotient, a call to F, and two calls to PSOL.
05938 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05939 !
05940 !      On entry
05941 !
05942 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
05943 !
05944 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
05945 !
05946 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
05947 !
05948 !            V = real array of length N (can be the same array as Z).
05949 !
05950 !         WGHT = array of length N containing scale factors.
05951 !                1/WGHT(i) are the diagonal elements of the matrix D.
05952 !
05953 !         FTEM = work array of length N.
05954 !
05955 !         VTEM = work array of length N used to store the
05956 !                unscaled version of V.
05957 !
05958 !           WP = real work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
05959 !
05960 !          IWP = integer work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
05961 !
05962 !          HL0 = current value of (step size h) * (coefficient l0).
05963 !
05964 !         JPRE = preconditioner type flag.
05965 !
05966 !
05967 !      On return
05968 !
05969 !            Z = array of length N containing desired scaled
05970 !                matrix-vector product.
05971 !
05972 !          IER = error flag from PSOL.
05973 !
05974 !         NPSL = the number of calls to PSOL.
05975 !
05976 ! In addition, this routine uses the Common variables TN, N, NFE.
05977 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
05978 INTEGER I
05979 DOUBLE PRECISION FAC, RNORM, DNRM2, TEMPN
05980 !
05981 ! Set VTEM = D * V.
05982 DO 10 I = 1,N
05983 10     VTEM(I) = V(I)/WGHT(I)
05984 IER = 0
05985 IF (JPRE .GE. 2) GOTO 30
05986 !
05987 ! JPRE = 0 or 1.  Save Y in Z and increment Y by VTEM.
05988 CALL DCOPY (N, Y, 1, Z, 1)
05989 DO 20 I = 1,N
05990 20     Y(I) = Z(I) + VTEM(I)
05991 FAC = HL0
05992 GOTO 60
05993 !
05994 ! JPRE = 2 or 3.  Apply inverse of right preconditioner to VTEM.
05995 30   CONTINUE
05996 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, FTEM, HL0, WP, IWP, VTEM, 2, IER)
05997 NPSL = NPSL + 1
05998 IF (IER .NE. 0) RETURN
05999 ! Calculate L-2 norm of (D-inverse) * VTEM.
06000 DO 40 I = 1,N
06001 40     Z(I) = VTEM(I)*WGHT(I)
06002 TEMPN = DNRM2 (N, Z, 1)
06003 RNORM = 1.0D0/TEMPN
06004 ! Save Y in Z and increment Y by VTEM/norm.
06005 CALL DCOPY (N, Y, 1, Z, 1)
06006 DO 50 I = 1,N
06007 50     Y(I) = Z(I) + VTEM(I)*RNORM
06008 FAC = HL0*TEMPN
06009 !
06010 ! For all JPRE, call F with incremented Y argument, and restore Y.
06011 60   CONTINUE
06012 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, FTEM)
06013 NFE = NFE + 1
06014 CALL DCOPY (N, Z, 1, Y, 1)
06015 ! Set Z = (identity - hl0*Jacobian) * VTEM, using difference quotient.
06016 DO 70 I = 1,N
06017 70     Z(I) = FTEM(I) - SAVF(I)
06018 DO 80 I = 1,N
06019 80     Z(I) = VTEM(I) - FAC*Z(I)
06020 ! Apply inverse of left preconditioner to Z, if nontrivial.
06021 IF (JPRE .EQ. 0 .OR. JPRE .EQ. 2) GOTO 85
06022 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, FTEM, HL0, WP, IWP, Z, 1, IER)
06023 NPSL = NPSL + 1
06024 IF (IER .NE. 0) RETURN
06025 85   CONTINUE
06026 ! Apply D-inverse to Z and return.
06027 DO 90 I = 1,N
06028 90     Z(I) = Z(I)*WGHT(I)
06029 RETURN
06030 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DATV ------------------------
06031 END
06032 
06033 SUBROUTINE DORTHOG (VNEW, V, HES, N, LL, LDHES, KMP, SNORMW)
06034 INTEGER N, LL, LDHES, KMP
06035 DOUBLE PRECISION VNEW, V, HES, SNORMW
06036 DIMENSION VNEW(*), V(N,*), HES(LDHES,*)
06037 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06038 ! This routine orthogonalizes the vector VNEW against the previous
06039 ! KMP vectors in the V array.  It uses a modified Gram-Schmidt
06040 ! orthogonalization procedure with conditional reorthogonalization.
06041 ! This is the version of 28 may 1986.
06042 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06043 !
06044 !      On entry
06045 !
06046 !         VNEW = the vector of length N containing a scaled product
06047 !                of the Jacobian and the vector V(*,LL).
06048 !
06049 !         V    = the N x l array containing the previous LL
06050 !                orthogonal vectors v(*,1) to v(*,LL).
06051 !
06052 !         HES  = an LL x LL upper Hessenberg matrix containing,
06053 !                in HES(i,k), k.lt.LL, scaled inner products of
06054 !                A*V(*,k) and V(*,i).
06055 !
06056 !        LDHES = the leading dimension of the HES array.
06057 !
06058 !         N    = the order of the matrix A, and the length of VNEW.
06059 !
06060 !         LL   = the current order of the matrix HES.
06061 !
06062 !          KMP = the number of previous vectors the new vector VNEW
06063 !                must be made orthogonal to (KMP .le. MAXL).
06064 !
06065 !
06066 !      On return
06067 !
06068 !         VNEW = the new vector orthogonal to V(*,i0) to V(*,LL),
06069 !                where i0 = MAX(1, LL-KMP+1).
06070 !
06071 !         HES  = upper Hessenberg matrix with column LL filled in with
06072 !                scaled inner products of A*V(*,LL) and V(*,i).
06073 !
06074 !       SNORMW = L-2 norm of VNEW.
06075 !
06076 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06077 INTEGER I, I0
06078 DOUBLE PRECISION ARG, DDOT, DNRM2, SUMDSQ, TEM, VNRM
06079 !
06080 ! Get norm of unaltered VNEW for later use. ----------------------------
06081 VNRM = DNRM2 (N, VNEW, 1)
06082 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06083 ! Do modified Gram-Schmidt on VNEW = A*v(LL).
06084 ! Scaled inner products give new column of HES.
06085 ! Projections of earlier vectors are subtracted from VNEW.
06086 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06087 I0 = MAX(1,LL-KMP+1)
06088 DO 10 I = I0,LL
06089 HES(I,LL) = DDOT (N, V(1,I), 1, VNEW, 1)
06090 TEM = -HES(I,LL)
06091 CALL DAXPY (N, TEM, V(1,I), 1, VNEW, 1)
06092 10     CONTINUE
06093 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06094 ! Compute SNORMW = norm of VNEW.
06095 ! If VNEW is small compared to its input value (in norm), then
06096 ! reorthogonalize VNEW to V(*,1) through V(*,LL).
06097 ! Correct if relative correction exceeds 1000*(unit roundoff).
06098 ! finally, correct SNORMW using the dot products involved.
06099 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06100 SNORMW = DNRM2 (N, VNEW, 1)
06101 IF (VNRM + 0.001D0*SNORMW .NE. VNRM) RETURN
06102 SUMDSQ = 0.0D0
06103 DO 30 I = I0,LL
06104 TEM = -DDOT (N, V(1,I), 1, VNEW, 1)
06105 IF (HES(I,LL) + 0.001D0*TEM .EQ. HES(I,LL)) GOTO 30
06106 HES(I,LL) = HES(I,LL) - TEM
06107 CALL DAXPY (N, TEM, V(1,I), 1, VNEW, 1)
06108 SUMDSQ = SUMDSQ + TEM**2
06109 30     CONTINUE
06110 IF (SUMDSQ .EQ. 0.0D0) RETURN
06111 ARG = MAX(0.0D0,SNORMW**2 - SUMDSQ)
06112 SNORMW = SQRT(ARG)
06113 !
06114 RETURN
06115 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DORTHOG ---------------------
06116 END
06117 
06118 SUBROUTINE DSPIGMR (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, B, WGHT, N, MAXL, MAXLP1, KMP, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, V, HES, Q, &
06119 LGMR, WP, IWP, WK, DL, IFLAG)
06120 EXTERNAL F, PSOL
06121 INTEGER NEQ,N,MAXL,MAXLP1,KMP,JPRE,MNEWT,NPSL,LGMR,IWP,IFLAG
06122 DOUBLE PRECISION TN,Y,SAVF,B,WGHT,DELTA,HL0,X,V,HES,Q,WP,WK,DL
06123 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), B(*), WGHT(*), X(*), V(N,*), HES(MAXLP1,*), Q(*), WP(*), IWP(*), WK(*), DL(*)
06124 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06125 ! This routine solves the linear system A * x = b using a scaled
06126 ! preconditioned version of the Generalized Minimal Residual method.
06127 ! An initial guess of x = 0 is assumed.
06128 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06129 !
06130 !      On entry
06131 !
06132 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
06133 !
06134 !           TN = current value of t.
06135 !
06136 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
06137 !
06138 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
06139 !
06140 !            B = the right hand side of the system A*x = b.
06141 !                B is also used as work space when computing
06142 !                the final approximation.
06143 !                (B is the same as V(*,MAXL+1) in the call to DSPIGMR.)
06144 !
06145 !         WGHT = the vector of length N containing the nonzero
06146 !                elements of the diagonal scaling matrix.
06147 !
06148 !            N = the order of the matrix A, and the lengths
06149 !                of the vectors WGHT, B and X.
06150 !
06151 !         MAXL = the maximum allowable order of the matrix HES.
06152 !
06153 !       MAXLP1 = MAXL + 1, used for dynamic dimensioning of HES.
06154 !
06155 !          KMP = the number of previous vectors the new vector VNEW
06156 !                must be made orthogonal to.  KMP .le. MAXL.
06157 !
06158 !        DELTA = tolerance on residuals b - A*x in weighted RMS-norm.
06159 !
06160 !          HL0 = current value of (step size h) * (coefficient l0).
06161 !
06162 !         JPRE = preconditioner type flag.
06163 !
06164 !        MNEWT = Newton iteration counter (.ge. 0).
06165 !
06166 !           WK = real work array used by routine DATV and PSOL.
06167 !
06168 !           DL = real work array used for calculation of the residual
06169 !                norm RHO when the method is incomplete (KMP .lt. MAXL).
06170 !                Not needed or referenced in complete case (KMP = MAXL).
06171 !
06172 !           WP = real work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06173 !
06174 !          IWP = integer work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06175 !
06176 !      On return
06177 !
06178 !         X    = the final computed approximation to the solution
06179 !                of the system A*x = b.
06180 !
06181 !         LGMR = the number of iterations performed and
06182 !                the current order of the upper Hessenberg
06183 !                matrix HES.
06184 !
06185 !         NPSL = the number of calls to PSOL.
06186 !
06187 !         V    = the N by (LGMR+1) array containing the LGMR
06188 !                orthogonal vectors V(*,1) to V(*,LGMR).
06189 !
06190 !         HES  = the upper triangular factor of the QR decomposition
06191 !                of the (LGMR+1) by lgmr upper Hessenberg matrix whose
06192 !                entries are the scaled inner-products of A*V(*,i)
06193 !                and V(*,k).
06194 !
06195 !         Q    = real array of length 2*MAXL containing the components
06196 !                of the Givens rotations used in the QR decomposition
06197 !                of HES.  It is loaded in DHEQR and used in DHELS.
06198 !
06199 !        IFLAG = integer error flag:
06200 !                0 means convergence in LGMR iterations, LGMR .le. MAXL.
06201 !                1 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
06202 !                  iterations, but the residual norm is .lt. 1,
06203 !                  or .lt. norm(b) if MNEWT = 0, and so x is computed.
06204 !                2 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
06205 !                  iterations, residual .gt. 1, and X is undefined.
06206 !                3 means there was a recoverable error in PSOL
06207 !                  caused by the preconditioner being out of date.
06208 !               -1 means there was a nonrecoverable error in PSOL.
06209 !
06210 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06211 INTEGER I, IER, INFO, IP1, I2, J, K, LL, LLP1
06212 DOUBLE PRECISION BNRM,BNRM0,C,DLNRM,PROD,RHO,S,SNORMW,DNRM2,TEM
06213 !
06214 IFLAG = 0
06215 LGMR = 0
06216 NPSL = 0
06217 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06218 ! The initial residual is the vector b.  Apply scaling to b, and test
06219 ! for an immediate return with X = 0 or X = b.
06220 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06221 DO 10 I = 1,N
06222 10     V(I,1) = B(I)*WGHT(I)
06223 BNRM0 = DNRM2 (N, V, 1)
06224 BNRM = BNRM0
06225 IF (BNRM0 .GT. DELTA) GOTO 30
06226 IF (MNEWT .GT. 0) GOTO 20
06227 CALL DCOPY (N, B, 1, X, 1)
06228 RETURN
06229 20   DO 25 I = 1,N
06230 25     X(I) = 0.0D0
06231 RETURN
06232 30   CONTINUE
06233 ! Apply inverse of left preconditioner to vector b. --------------------
06234 IER = 0
06235 IF (JPRE .EQ. 0 .OR. JPRE .EQ. 2) GOTO 55
06236 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, B, 1, IER)
06237 NPSL = 1
06238 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 300
06239 ! Calculate norm of scaled vector V(*,1) and normalize it. -------------
06240 DO 50 I = 1,N
06241 50     V(I,1) = B(I)*WGHT(I)
06242 BNRM = DNRM2 (N, V, 1)
06243 DELTA = DELTA*(BNRM/BNRM0)
06244 55   TEM = 1.0D0/BNRM
06245 CALL DSCAL (N, TEM, V(1,1), 1)
06246 ! Zero out the HES array. ----------------------------------------------
06247 DO 65 J = 1,MAXL
06248 DO 60 I = 1,MAXLP1
06249 60       HES(I,J) = 0.0D0
06250 65     CONTINUE
06251 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06252 ! Main loop to compute the vectors V(*,2) to V(*,MAXL).
06253 ! The running product PROD is needed for the convergence test.
06254 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06255 PROD = 1.0D0
06256 DO 90 LL = 1,MAXL
06257 LGMR = LL
06258 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06259 ! Call routine DATV to compute VNEW = Abar*v(ll), where Abar is
06260 ! the matrix A with scaling and inverse preconditioner factors applied.
06261 ! Call routine DORTHOG to orthogonalize the new vector VNEW = V(*,LL+1).
06262 ! Call routine DHEQR to update the factors of HES.
06263 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06264 CALL DATV (NEQ, Y, SAVF, V(1,LL), WGHT, X, F, PSOL, V(1,LL+1), WK, WP, IWP, HL0, JPRE, IER, NPSL)
06265 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 300
06266 CALL DORTHOG (V(1,LL+1), V, HES, N, LL, MAXLP1, KMP, SNORMW)
06267 HES(LL+1,LL) = SNORMW
06268 CALL DHEQR (HES, MAXLP1, LL, Q, INFO, LL)
06269 IF (INFO .EQ. LL) GOTO 120
06270 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06271 ! Update RHO, the estimate of the norm of the residual b - A*xl.
06272 ! If KMP .lt. MAXL, then the vectors V(*,1),...,V(*,LL+1) are not
06273 ! necessarily orthogonal for LL .gt. KMP.  The vector DL must then
06274 ! be computed, and its norm used in the calculation of RHO.
06275 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06276 PROD = PROD*Q(2*LL)
06277 RHO = ABS(PROD*BNRM)
06278 IF ((LL.GT.KMP) .AND. (KMP.LT.MAXL)) THEN
06279 IF (LL .EQ. KMP+1) THEN
06280 CALL DCOPY (N, V(1,1), 1, DL, 1)
06281 DO 75 I = 1,KMP
06282 IP1 = I + 1
06283 I2 = I*2
06284 S = Q(I2)
06285 C = Q(I2-1)
06286 DO 70 K = 1,N
06287 70             DL(K) = S*DL(K) + C*V(K,IP1)
06288 75           CONTINUE
06289 ENDIF
06290 S = Q(2*LL)
06291 C = Q(2*LL-1)/SNORMW
06292 LLP1 = LL + 1
06293 DO 80 K = 1,N
06294 80         DL(K) = S*DL(K) + C*V(K,LLP1)
06295 DLNRM = DNRM2 (N, DL, 1)
06296 RHO = RHO*DLNRM
06297 ENDIF
06298 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06299 ! Test for convergence.  If passed, compute approximation xl.
06300 ! if failed and LL .lt. MAXL, then continue iterating.
06301 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06302 IF (RHO .LE. DELTA) GOTO 200
06303 IF (LL .EQ. MAXL) GOTO 100
06304 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06305 ! Rescale so that the norm of V(1,LL+1) is one.
06306 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06307 TEM = 1.0D0/SNORMW
06308 CALL DSCAL (N, TEM, V(1,LL+1), 1)
06309 90     CONTINUE
06310 100  CONTINUE
06311 IF (RHO .LE. 1.0D0) GOTO 150
06312 IF (RHO .LE. BNRM .AND. MNEWT .EQ. 0) GOTO 150
06313 120  CONTINUE
06314 IFLAG = 2
06315 RETURN
06316 150  IFLAG = 1
06317 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06318 ! Compute the approximation xl to the solution.
06319 ! Since the vector X was used as work space, and the initial guess
06320 ! of the Newton correction is zero, X must be reset to zero.
06321 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06322 200  CONTINUE
06323 LL = LGMR
06324 LLP1 = LL + 1
06325 DO 210 K = 1,LLP1
06326 210    B(K) = 0.0D0
06327 B(1) = BNRM
06328 CALL DHELS (HES, MAXLP1, LL, Q, B)
06329 DO 220 K = 1,N
06330 220    X(K) = 0.0D0
06331 DO 230 I = 1,LL
06332 CALL DAXPY (N, B(I), V(1,I), 1, X, 1)
06333 230    CONTINUE
06334 DO 240 I = 1,N
06335 240    X(I) = X(I)/WGHT(I)
06336 IF (JPRE .LE. 1) RETURN
06337 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, X, 2, IER)
06338 NPSL = NPSL + 1
06339 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 300
06340 RETURN
06341 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06342 ! This block handles error returns forced by routine PSOL.
06343 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06344 300  CONTINUE
06345 IF (IER .LT. 0) IFLAG = -1
06346 IF (IER .GT. 0) IFLAG = 3
06347 !
06348 RETURN
06349 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSPIGMR ---------------------
06350 END
06351 
06352 SUBROUTINE DPCG (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, R, WGHT, N, MAXL, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, P, W, Z, &
06353 LPCG, WP, IWP, WK, IFLAG)
06354 EXTERNAL F, PSOL
06355 INTEGER NEQ, N, MAXL, JPRE, MNEWT, NPSL, LPCG, IWP, IFLAG
06356 DOUBLE PRECISION TN,Y,SAVF,R,WGHT,DELTA,HL0,X,P,W,Z,WP,WK
06357 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), R(*), WGHT(*), X(*), P(*), W(*), Z(*), WP(*), IWP(*), WK(*)
06358 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06359 ! This routine computes the solution to the system A*x = b using a
06360 ! preconditioned version of the Conjugate Gradient algorithm.
06361 ! It is assumed here that the matrix A and the preconditioner
06362 ! matrix M are symmetric positive definite or nearly so.
06363 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06364 !
06365 !      On entry
06366 !
06367 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
06368 !
06369 !           TN = current value of t.
06370 !
06371 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
06372 !
06373 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
06374 !
06375 !            R = the right hand side of the system A*x = b.
06376 !
06377 !         WGHT = array of length N containing scale factors.
06378 !                1/WGHT(i) are the diagonal elements of the diagonal
06379 !                scaling matrix D.
06380 !
06381 !            N = the order of the matrix A, and the lengths
06382 !                of the vectors Y, SAVF, R, WGHT, P, W, Z, WK, and X.
06383 !
06384 !         MAXL = the maximum allowable number of iterates.
06385 !
06386 !        DELTA = tolerance on residuals b - A*x in weighted RMS-norm.
06387 !
06388 !          HL0 = current value of (step size h) * (coefficient l0).
06389 !
06390 !         JPRE = preconditioner type flag.
06391 !
06392 !        MNEWT = Newton iteration counter (.ge. 0).
06393 !
06394 !           WK = real work array used by routine DATP.
06395 !
06396 !           WP = real work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06397 !
06398 !          IWP = integer work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06399 !
06400 !      On return
06401 !
06402 !         X    = the final computed approximation to the solution
06403 !                of the system A*x = b.
06404 !
06405 !         LPCG = the number of iterations performed, and current
06406 !                order of the upper Hessenberg matrix HES.
06407 !
06408 !         NPSL = the number of calls to PSOL.
06409 !
06410 !        IFLAG = integer error flag:
06411 !                0 means convergence in LPCG iterations, LPCG .le. MAXL.
06412 !                1 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
06413 !                  iterations, but the residual norm is .lt. 1,
06414 !                  or .lt. norm(b) if MNEWT = 0, and so X is computed.
06415 !                2 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
06416 !                  iterations, residual .gt. 1, and X is undefined.
06417 !                3 means there was a recoverable error in PSOL
06418 !                  caused by the preconditioner being out of date.
06419 !                4 means there was a zero denominator in the algorithm.
06420 !                  The system matrix or preconditioner matrix is not
06421 !                  sufficiently close to being symmetric pos. definite.
06422 !               -1 means there was a nonrecoverable error in PSOL.
06423 !
06424 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06425 INTEGER I, IER
06426 DOUBLE PRECISION ALPHA,BETA,BNRM,PTW,RNRM,DDOT,DVNORM,ZTR,ZTR0
06427 !
06428 IFLAG = 0
06429 NPSL = 0
06430 LPCG = 0
06431 DO 10 I = 1,N
06432 10     X(I) = 0.0D0
06433 BNRM = DVNORM (N, R, WGHT)
06434 ! Test for immediate return with X = 0 or X = b. -----------------------
06435 IF (BNRM .GT. DELTA) GOTO 20
06436 IF (MNEWT .GT. 0) RETURN
06437 CALL DCOPY (N, R, 1, X, 1)
06438 RETURN
06439 !
06440 20   ZTR = 0.0D0
06441 ! Loop point for PCG iterations. ---------------------------------------
06442 30   CONTINUE
06443 LPCG = LPCG + 1
06444 CALL DCOPY (N, R, 1, Z, 1)
06445 IER = 0
06446 IF (JPRE .EQ. 0) GOTO 40
06447 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, Z, 3, IER)
06448 NPSL = NPSL + 1
06449 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 100
06450 40   CONTINUE
06451 ZTR0 = ZTR
06452 ZTR = DDOT (N, Z, 1, R, 1)
06453 IF (LPCG .NE. 1) GOTO 50
06454 CALL DCOPY (N, Z, 1, P, 1)
06455 GOTO 70
06456 50   CONTINUE
06457 IF (ZTR0 .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 200
06458 BETA = ZTR/ZTR0
06459 DO 60 I = 1,N
06460 60     P(I) = Z(I) + BETA*P(I)
06461 70   CONTINUE
06462 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06463 !  Call DATP to compute A*p and return the answer in W.
06464 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06465 CALL DATP (NEQ, Y, SAVF, P, WGHT, HL0, WK, F, W)
06466 !
06467 PTW = DDOT (N, P, 1, W, 1)
06468 IF (PTW .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 200
06469 ALPHA = ZTR/PTW
06470 CALL DAXPY (N, ALPHA, P, 1, X, 1)
06471 ALPHA = -ALPHA
06472 CALL DAXPY (N, ALPHA, W, 1, R, 1)
06473 RNRM = DVNORM (N, R, WGHT)
06474 IF (RNRM .LE. DELTA) RETURN
06475 IF (LPCG .LT. MAXL) GOTO 30
06476 IFLAG = 2
06477 IF (RNRM .LE. 1.0D0) IFLAG = 1
06478 IF (RNRM .LE. BNRM .AND. MNEWT .EQ. 0) IFLAG = 1
06479 RETURN
06480 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06481 ! This block handles error returns from PSOL.
06482 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06483 100  CONTINUE
06484 IF (IER .LT. 0) IFLAG = -1
06485 IF (IER .GT. 0) IFLAG = 3
06486 RETURN
06487 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06488 ! This block handles division by zero errors.
06489 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06490 200  CONTINUE
06491 IFLAG = 4
06492 RETURN
06493 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPCG ------------------------
06494 END
06495 
06496 SUBROUTINE DPCGS (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, R, WGHT, N, MAXL, DELTA, HL0, JPRE, MNEWT, F, PSOL, NPSL, X, P, W, Z, LPCG, WP, &
06497 IWP, WK, IFLAG)
06498 EXTERNAL F, PSOL
06499 INTEGER NEQ, N, MAXL, JPRE, MNEWT, NPSL, LPCG, IWP, IFLAG
06500 DOUBLE PRECISION TN,Y,SAVF,R,WGHT,DELTA,HL0,X,P,W,Z,WP,WK
06501 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), R(*), WGHT(*), X(*), P(*), W(*), Z(*), WP(*), IWP(*), WK(*)
06502 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06503 ! This routine computes the solution to the system A*x = b using a
06504 ! scaled preconditioned version of the Conjugate Gradient algorithm.
06505 ! It is assumed here that the scaled matrix D**-1 * A * D and the
06506 ! scaled preconditioner D**-1 * M * D are close to being
06507 ! symmetric positive definite.
06508 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06509 !
06510 !      On entry
06511 !
06512 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
06513 !
06514 !           TN = current value of t.
06515 !
06516 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
06517 !
06518 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
06519 !
06520 !            R = the right hand side of the system A*x = b.
06521 !
06522 !         WGHT = array of length N containing scale factors.
06523 !                1/WGHT(i) are the diagonal elements of the diagonal
06524 !                scaling matrix D.
06525 !
06526 !            N = the order of the matrix A, and the lengths
06527 !                of the vectors Y, SAVF, R, WGHT, P, W, Z, WK, and X.
06528 !
06529 !         MAXL = the maximum allowable number of iterates.
06530 !
06531 !        DELTA = tolerance on residuals b - A*x in weighted RMS-norm.
06532 !
06533 !          HL0 = current value of (step size h) * (coefficient l0).
06534 !
06535 !         JPRE = preconditioner type flag.
06536 !
06537 !        MNEWT = Newton iteration counter (.ge. 0).
06538 !
06539 !           WK = real work array used by routine DATP.
06540 !
06541 !           WP = real work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06542 !
06543 !          IWP = integer work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06544 !
06545 !      On return
06546 !
06547 !         X    = the final computed approximation to the solution
06548 !                of the system A*x = b.
06549 !
06550 !         LPCG = the number of iterations performed, and current
06551 !                order of the upper Hessenberg matrix HES.
06552 !
06553 !         NPSL = the number of calls to PSOL.
06554 !
06555 !        IFLAG = integer error flag:
06556 !                0 means convergence in LPCG iterations, LPCG .le. MAXL.
06557 !                1 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
06558 !                  iterations, but the residual norm is .lt. 1,
06559 !                  or .lt. norm(b) if MNEWT = 0, and so X is computed.
06560 !                2 means the convergence test did not pass in MAXL
06561 !                  iterations, residual .gt. 1, and X is undefined.
06562 !                3 means there was a recoverable error in PSOL
06563 !                  caused by the preconditioner being out of date.
06564 !                4 means there was a zero denominator in the algorithm.
06565 !                  the scaled matrix or scaled preconditioner is not
06566 !                  sufficiently close to being symmetric pos. definite.
06567 !               -1 means there was a nonrecoverable error in PSOL.
06568 !
06569 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06570 INTEGER I, IER
06571 DOUBLE PRECISION ALPHA, BETA, BNRM, PTW, RNRM, DVNORM, ZTR, ZTR0
06572 !
06573 IFLAG = 0
06574 NPSL = 0
06575 LPCG = 0
06576 DO 10 I = 1,N
06577 10     X(I) = 0.0D0
06578 BNRM = DVNORM (N, R, WGHT)
06579 ! Test for immediate return with X = 0 or X = b. -----------------------
06580 IF (BNRM .GT. DELTA) GOTO 20
06581 IF (MNEWT .GT. 0) RETURN
06582 CALL DCOPY (N, R, 1, X, 1)
06583 RETURN
06584 !
06585 20   ZTR = 0.0D0
06586 ! Loop point for PCG iterations. ---------------------------------------
06587 30   CONTINUE
06588 LPCG = LPCG + 1
06589 CALL DCOPY (N, R, 1, Z, 1)
06590 IER = 0
06591 IF (JPRE .EQ. 0) GOTO 40
06592 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, Z, 3, IER)
06593 NPSL = NPSL + 1
06594 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 100
06595 40   CONTINUE
06596 ZTR0 = ZTR
06597 ZTR = 0.0D0
06598 DO 45 I = 1,N
06599 45     ZTR = ZTR + Z(I)*R(I)*WGHT(I)**2
06600 IF (LPCG .NE. 1) GOTO 50
06601 CALL DCOPY (N, Z, 1, P, 1)
06602 GOTO 70
06603 50   CONTINUE
06604 IF (ZTR0 .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 200
06605 BETA = ZTR/ZTR0
06606 DO 60 I = 1,N
06607 60     P(I) = Z(I) + BETA*P(I)
06608 70   CONTINUE
06609 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06610 !  Call DATP to compute A*p and return the answer in W.
06611 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06612 CALL DATP (NEQ, Y, SAVF, P, WGHT, HL0, WK, F, W)
06613 !
06614 PTW = 0.0D0
06615 DO 80 I = 1,N
06616 80     PTW = PTW + P(I)*W(I)*WGHT(I)**2
06617 IF (PTW .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 200
06618 ALPHA = ZTR/PTW
06619 CALL DAXPY (N, ALPHA, P, 1, X, 1)
06620 ALPHA = -ALPHA
06621 CALL DAXPY (N, ALPHA, W, 1, R, 1)
06622 RNRM = DVNORM (N, R, WGHT)
06623 IF (RNRM .LE. DELTA) RETURN
06624 IF (LPCG .LT. MAXL) GOTO 30
06625 IFLAG = 2
06626 IF (RNRM .LE. 1.0D0) IFLAG = 1
06627 IF (RNRM .LE. BNRM .AND. MNEWT .EQ. 0) IFLAG = 1
06628 RETURN
06629 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06630 ! This block handles error returns from PSOL.
06631 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06632 100  CONTINUE
06633 IF (IER .LT. 0) IFLAG = -1
06634 IF (IER .GT. 0) IFLAG = 3
06635 RETURN
06636 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06637 ! This block handles division by zero errors.
06638 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06639 200  CONTINUE
06640 IFLAG = 4
06641 RETURN
06642 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPCGS -----------------------
06643 END
06644 
06645 SUBROUTINE DATP (NEQ, Y, SAVF, P, WGHT, HL0, WK, F, W)
06646 EXTERNAL F
06647 INTEGER NEQ
06648 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, SAVF, P, WGHT, HL0, WK, W
06649 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), P(*), WGHT(*), WK(*), W(*)
06650 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, 
06651 MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
06652 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
06653 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
06654 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
06655 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06656 ! This routine computes the product
06657 !
06658 !              w = (I - hl0*df/dy)*p
06659 !
06660 ! This is computed by a call to F and a difference quotient.
06661 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06662 !
06663 !      On entry
06664 !
06665 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
06666 !
06667 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
06668 !
06669 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
06670 !
06671 !            P = real array of length N.
06672 !
06673 !         WGHT = array of length N containing scale factors.
06674 !                1/WGHT(i) are the diagonal elements of the matrix D.
06675 !
06676 !           WK = work array of length N.
06677 !
06678 !      On return
06679 !
06680 !
06681 !            W = array of length N containing desired
06682 !                matrix-vector product.
06683 !
06684 ! In addition, this routine uses the Common variables TN, N, NFE.
06685 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06686 INTEGER I
06687 DOUBLE PRECISION FAC, PNRM, RPNRM, DVNORM
06688 !
06689 PNRM = DVNORM (N, P, WGHT)
06690 RPNRM = 1.0D0/PNRM
06691 CALL DCOPY (N, Y, 1, W, 1)
06692 DO 20 I = 1,N
06693 20     Y(I) = W(I) + P(I)*RPNRM
06694 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, WK)
06695 NFE = NFE + 1
06696 CALL DCOPY (N, W, 1, Y, 1)
06697 FAC = HL0*PNRM
06698 DO 40 I = 1,N
06699 40     W(I) = P(I) - FAC*(WK(I) - SAVF(I))
06700 RETURN
06701 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DATP ------------------------
06702 END
06703 
06704 SUBROUTINE DUSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, B, WGHT, N, DELTA, HL0, MNEWT, PSOL, NPSL, X, WP, IWP, WK, IFLAG)
06705 EXTERNAL PSOL
06706 INTEGER NEQ, N, MNEWT, NPSL, IWP, IFLAG
06707 DOUBLE PRECISION TN, Y, SAVF, B, WGHT, DELTA, HL0, X, WP, WK
06708 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), SAVF(*), B(*), WGHT(*), X(*), WP(*), IWP(*), WK(*)
06709 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06710 ! This routine solves the linear system A * x = b using only a call
06711 ! to the user-supplied routine PSOL (no Krylov iteration).
06712 ! If the norm of the right-hand side vector b is smaller than DELTA,
06713 ! the vector X returned is X = b (if MNEWT = 0) or X = 0 otherwise.
06714 ! PSOL is called with an LR argument of 0.
06715 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06716 !
06717 !      On entry
06718 !
06719 !          NEQ = problem size, passed to F and PSOL (NEQ(1) = N).
06720 !
06721 !           TN = current value of t.
06722 !
06723 !            Y = array containing current dependent variable vector.
06724 !
06725 !         SAVF = array containing current value of f(t,y).
06726 !
06727 !            B = the right hand side of the system A*x = b.
06728 !
06729 !         WGHT = the vector of length N containing the nonzero
06730 !                elements of the diagonal scaling matrix.
06731 !
06732 !            N = the order of the matrix A, and the lengths
06733 !                of the vectors WGHT, B and X.
06734 !
06735 !        DELTA = tolerance on residuals b - A*x in weighted RMS-norm.
06736 !
06737 !          HL0 = current value of (step size h) * (coefficient l0).
06738 !
06739 !        MNEWT = Newton iteration counter (.ge. 0).
06740 !
06741 !           WK = real work array used by PSOL.
06742 !
06743 !           WP = real work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06744 !
06745 !          IWP = integer work array used by preconditioner PSOL.
06746 !
06747 !      On return
06748 !
06749 !         X    = the final computed approximation to the solution
06750 !                of the system A*x = b.
06751 !
06752 !         NPSL = the number of calls to PSOL.
06753 !
06754 !        IFLAG = integer error flag:
06755 !                0 means no trouble occurred.
06756 !                3 means there was a recoverable error in PSOL
06757 !                  caused by the preconditioner being out of date.
06758 !               -1 means there was a nonrecoverable error in PSOL.
06759 !
06760 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06761 INTEGER I, IER
06762 DOUBLE PRECISION BNRM, DVNORM
06763 !
06764 IFLAG = 0
06765 NPSL = 0
06766 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06767 ! Test for an immediate return with X = 0 or X = b.
06768 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06769 BNRM = DVNORM (N, B, WGHT)
06770 IF (BNRM .GT. DELTA) GOTO 30
06771 IF (MNEWT .GT. 0) GOTO 10
06772 CALL DCOPY (N, B, 1, X, 1)
06773 RETURN
06774 10   DO 20 I = 1,N
06775 20     X(I) = 0.0D0
06776 RETURN
06777 ! Make call to PSOL and copy result from B to X. -----------------------
06778 30   IER = 0
06779 CALL PSOL (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, WK, HL0, WP, IWP, B, 0, IER)
06780 NPSL = 1
06781 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 100
06782 CALL DCOPY (N, B, 1, X, 1)
06783 RETURN
06784 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06785 ! This block handles error returns forced by routine PSOL.
06786 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06787 100  CONTINUE
06788 IF (IER .LT. 0) IFLAG = -1
06789 IF (IER .GT. 0) IFLAG = 3
06790 RETURN
06791 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DUSOL -----------------------
06792 END
06793 
06794 SUBROUTINE DSRCPK (RSAV, ISAV, JOB)
06795 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06796 ! This routine saves or restores (depending on JOB) the contents of
06797 ! the Common blocks DLS001, DLPK01, which are used
06798 ! internally by the DLSODPK solver.
06799 !
06800 ! RSAV = real array of length 222 or more.
06801 ! ISAV = integer array of length 50 or more.
06802 ! JOB  = flag indicating to save or restore the Common blocks:
06803 !        JOB  = 1 if Common is to be saved (written to RSAV/ISAV)
06804 !        JOB  = 2 if Common is to be restored (read from RSAV/ISAV)
06805 !        A call with JOB = 2 presumes a prior call with JOB = 1.
06806 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06807 INTEGER ISAV, JOB
06808 INTEGER ILS, ILSP
06809 INTEGER I, LENILP, LENRLP, LENILS, LENRLS
06810 DOUBLE PRECISION RSAV,   RLS, RLSP
06811 DIMENSION RSAV(*), ISAV(*)
06812 SAVE LENRLS, LENILS, LENRLP, LENILP
06813 COMMON /DLS001/ RLS(218), ILS(37)
06814 COMMON /DLPK01/ RLSP(4), ILSP(13)
06815 DATA LENRLS/218/, LENILS/37/, LENRLP/4/, LENILP/13/
06816 !
06817 IF (JOB .EQ. 2) GOTO 100
06818 CALL DCOPY (LENRLS, RLS, 1, RSAV, 1)
06819 CALL DCOPY (LENRLP, RLSP, 1, RSAV(LENRLS+1), 1)
06820 DO 20 I = 1,LENILS
06821 20     ISAV(I) = ILS(I)
06822 DO 40 I = 1,LENILP
06823 40     ISAV(LENILS+I) = ILSP(I)
06824 RETURN
06825 !
06826 100  CONTINUE
06827 CALL DCOPY (LENRLS, RSAV, 1, RLS, 1)
06828 CALL DCOPY (LENRLP, RSAV(LENRLS+1), 1, RLSP, 1)
06829 DO 120 I = 1,LENILS
06830 120     ILS(I) = ISAV(I)
06831 DO 140 I = 1,LENILP
06832 140     ILSP(I) = ISAV(LENILS+I)
06833 RETURN
06834 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSRCPK ----------------------
06835 END
06836 
06837 SUBROUTINE DHEFA (A, LDA, N, IPVT, INFO, JOB)
06838 INTEGER LDA, N, IPVT(*), INFO, JOB
06839 DOUBLE PRECISION A(LDA,*)
06840 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06841 !     This routine is a modification of the LINPACK routine DGEFA and
06842 !     performs an LU decomposition of an upper Hessenberg matrix A.
06843 !     There are two options available:
06844 !
06845 !          (1)  performing a fresh factorization
06846 !          (2)  updating the LU factors by adding a row and a
06847 !               column to the matrix A.
06848 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06849 !     DHEFA factors an upper Hessenberg matrix by elimination.
06850 !
06851 !     On entry
06852 !
06853 !        A       DOUBLE PRECISION(LDA, N)
06854 !                the matrix to be factored.
06855 !
06856 !        LDA     INTEGER
06857 !                the leading dimension of the array  A .
06858 !
06859 !        N       INTEGER
06860 !                the order of the matrix  A .
06861 !
06862 !        JOB     INTEGER
06863 !                JOB = 1    means that a fresh factorization of the
06864 !                           matrix A is desired.
06865 !                JOB .ge. 2 means that the current factorization of A
06866 !                           will be updated by the addition of a row
06867 !                           and a column.
06868 !
06869 !     On return
06870 !
06871 !        A       an upper triangular matrix and the multipliers
06872 !                which were used to obtain it.
06873 !                The factorization can be written  A = L*U  where
06874 !                L  is a product of permutation and unit lower
06875 !                triangular matrices and  U  is upper triangular.
06876 !
06877 !        IPVT    INTEGER(N)
06878 !                an integer vector of pivot indices.
06879 !
06880 !        INFO    INTEGER
06881 !                = 0  normal value.
06882 !                = k  if  U(k,k) .eq. 0.0 .  This is not an error
06883 !                     condition for this subroutine, but it does
06884 !                     indicate that DHESL will divide by zero if called.
06885 !
06886 !     Modification of LINPACK, by Peter Brown, LLNL.
06887 !     Written 7/20/83.  This version dated 6/20/01.
06888 !    
06889 !     BLAS called: DAXPY, IDAMAX
06890 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
06891 INTEGER IDAMAX, J, K, KM1, KP1, L, NM1
06892 DOUBLE PRECISION T
06893 !
06894 IF (JOB .GT. 1) GOTO 80
06895 !
06896 ! A new facorization is desired.  This is essentially the LINPACK
06897 ! code with the exception that we know there is only one nonzero
06898 ! element below the main diagonal.
06899 !
06900 !     Gaussian elimination with partial pivoting
06901 !
06902 INFO = 0
06903 NM1 = N - 1
06904 IF (NM1 .LT. 1) GOTO 70
06905 DO 60 K = 1, NM1
06906 KP1 = K + 1
06907 !
06908 !        Find L = pivot index
06909 !
06910 L = IDAMAX (2, A(K,K), 1) + K - 1
06911 IPVT(K) = L
06912 !
06913 !        Zero pivot implies this column already triangularized
06914 !
06915 IF (A(L,K) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 40
06916 !
06917 !           Interchange if necessary
06918 !
06919 IF (L .EQ. K) GOTO 10
06920 T = A(L,K)
06921 A(L,K) = A(K,K)
06922 A(K,K) = T
06923 10       CONTINUE
06924 !
06925 !           Compute multipliers
06926 !
06927 T = -1.0D0/A(K,K)
06928 A(K+1,K) = A(K+1,K)*T
06929 !
06930 !           Row elimination with column indexing
06931 !
06932 DO 30 J = KP1, N
06933 T = A(L,J)
06934 IF (L .EQ. K) GOTO 20
06935 A(L,J) = A(K,J)
06936 A(K,J) = T
06937 20          CONTINUE
06938 CALL DAXPY (N-K, T, A(K+1,K), 1, A(K+1,J), 1)
06939 30       CONTINUE
06940 GOTO 50
06941 40    CONTINUE
06942 INFO = K
06943 50    CONTINUE
06944 60 CONTINUE
06945 70 CONTINUE
06946 IPVT(N) = N
06947 IF (A(N,N) .EQ. 0.0D0) INFO = N
06948 RETURN
06949 !
06950 ! The old factorization of A will be updated.  A row and a column
06951 ! has been added to the matrix A.
06952 ! N-1 is now the old order of the matrix.
06953 !
06954 80  CONTINUE
06955 NM1 = N - 1
06956 !
06957 ! Perform row interchanges on the elements of the new column, and
06958 ! perform elimination operations on the elements using the multipliers.
06959 !
06960 IF (NM1 .LE. 1) GOTO 105
06961 DO 100 K = 2,NM1
06962 KM1 = K - 1
06963 L = IPVT(KM1)
06964 T = A(L,N)
06965 IF (L .EQ. KM1) GOTO 90
06966 A(L,N) = A(KM1,N)
06967 A(KM1,N) = T
06968 90    CONTINUE
06969 A(K,N) = A(K,N) + A(K,KM1)*T
06970 100    CONTINUE
06971 105  CONTINUE
06972 !
06973 ! Complete update of factorization by decomposing last 2x2 block.
06974 !
06975 INFO = 0
06976 !
06977 !        Find L = pivot index
06978 !
06979 L = IDAMAX (2, A(NM1,NM1), 1) + NM1 - 1
06980 IPVT(NM1) = L
06981 !
06982 !        Zero pivot implies this column already triangularized
06983 !
06984 IF (A(L,NM1) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 140
06985 !
06986 !           Interchange if necessary
06987 !
06988 IF (L .EQ. NM1) GOTO 110
06989 T = A(L,NM1)
06990 A(L,NM1) = A(NM1,NM1)
06991 A(NM1,NM1) = T
06992 110       CONTINUE
06993 !
06994 !           Compute multipliers
06995 !
06996 T = -1.0D0/A(NM1,NM1)
06997 A(N,NM1) = A(N,NM1)*T
06998 !
06999 !           Row elimination with column indexing
07000 !
07001 T = A(L,N)
07002 IF (L .EQ. NM1) GOTO 120
07003 A(L,N) = A(NM1,N)
07004 A(NM1,N) = T
07005 120          CONTINUE
07006 A(N,N) = A(N,N) + T*A(N,NM1)
07007 GOTO 150
07008 140    CONTINUE
07009 INFO = NM1
07010 150    CONTINUE
07011 IPVT(N) = N
07012 IF (A(N,N) .EQ. 0.0D0) INFO = N
07013 RETURN
07014 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DHEFA -----------------------
07015 END
07016 
07017 SUBROUTINE DHESL (A, LDA, N, IPVT, B)
07018 INTEGER LDA, N, IPVT(*)
07019 DOUBLE PRECISION A(LDA,*), B(*)
07020 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07021 ! This is essentially the LINPACK routine DGESL except for changes
07022 ! due to the fact that A is an upper Hessenberg matrix.
07023 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07024 !     DHESL solves the real system A * x = b
07025 !     using the factors computed by DHEFA.
07026 !
07027 !     On entry
07028 !
07029 !        A       DOUBLE PRECISION(LDA, N)
07030 !                the output from DHEFA.
07031 !
07032 !        LDA     INTEGER
07033 !                the leading dimension of the array  A .
07034 !
07035 !        N       INTEGER
07036 !                the order of the matrix  A .
07037 !
07038 !        IPVT    INTEGER(N)
07039 !                the pivot vector from DHEFA.
07040 !
07041 !        B       DOUBLE PRECISION(N)
07042 !                the right hand side vector.
07043 !
07044 !     On return
07045 !
07046 !        B       the solution vector  x .
07047 !
07048 !     Modification of LINPACK, by Peter Brown, LLNL.
07049 !     Written 7/20/83.  This version dated 6/20/01.
07050 !
07051 !     BLAS called: DAXPY
07052 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07053 INTEGER K, KB, L, NM1
07054 DOUBLE PRECISION T
07055 !
07056 NM1 = N - 1
07057 !
07058 !        Solve  A * x = b
07059 !        First solve  L*y = b
07060 !
07061 IF (NM1 .LT. 1) GOTO 30
07062 DO 20 K = 1, NM1
07063 L = IPVT(K)
07064 T = B(L)
07065 IF (L .EQ. K) GOTO 10
07066 B(L) = B(K)
07067 B(K) = T
07068 10       CONTINUE
07069 B(K+1) = B(K+1) + T*A(K+1,K)
07070 20    CONTINUE
07071 30    CONTINUE
07072 !
07073 !        Now solve  U*x = y
07074 !
07075 DO 40 KB = 1, N
07076 K = N + 1 - KB
07077 B(K) = B(K)/A(K,K)
07078 T = -B(K)
07079 CALL DAXPY (K-1, T, A(1,K), 1, B(1), 1)
07080 40    CONTINUE
07081 RETURN
07082 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DHESL -----------------------
07083 END
07084 
07085 SUBROUTINE DHEQR (A, LDA, N, Q, INFO, IJOB)
07086 INTEGER LDA, N, INFO, IJOB
07087 DOUBLE PRECISION A(LDA,*), Q(*)
07088 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07089 !     This routine performs a QR decomposition of an upper
07090 !     Hessenberg matrix A.  There are two options available:
07091 !
07092 !          (1)  performing a fresh decomposition
07093 !          (2)  updating the QR factors by adding a row and a
07094 !               column to the matrix A.
07095 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07096 !     DHEQR decomposes an upper Hessenberg matrix by using Givens
07097 !     rotations.
07098 !
07099 !     On entry
07100 !
07101 !        A       DOUBLE PRECISION(LDA, N)
07102 !                the matrix to be decomposed.
07103 !
07104 !        LDA     INTEGER
07105 !                the leading dimension of the array  A .
07106 !
07107 !        N       INTEGER
07108 !                A is an (N+1) by N Hessenberg matrix.
07109 !
07110 !        IJOB    INTEGER
07111 !                = 1     means that a fresh decomposition of the
07112 !                        matrix A is desired.
07113 !                .ge. 2  means that the current decomposition of A
07114 !                        will be updated by the addition of a row
07115 !                        and a column.
07116 !     On return
07117 !
07118 !        A       the upper triangular matrix R.
07119 !                The factorization can be written Q*A = R, where
07120 !                Q is a product of Givens rotations and R is upper
07121 !                triangular.
07122 !
07123 !        Q       DOUBLE PRECISION(2*N)
07124 !                the factors c and s of each Givens rotation used
07125 !                in decomposing A.
07126 !
07127 !        INFO    INTEGER
07128 !                = 0  normal value.
07129 !                = k  if  A(k,k) .eq. 0.0 .  This is not an error
07130 !                     condition for this subroutine, but it does
07131 !                     indicate that DHELS will divide by zero
07132 !                     if called.
07133 !
07134 !     Modification of LINPACK, by Peter Brown, LLNL.
07135 !     Written 1/13/86.  This version dated 6/20/01.
07136 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07137 INTEGER I, IQ, J, K, KM1, KP1, NM1
07138 DOUBLE PRECISION C, S, T, T1, T2
07139 !
07140 IF (IJOB .GT. 1) GOTO 70
07141 !
07142 ! A new facorization is desired.
07143 !
07144 !     QR decomposition without pivoting
07145 !
07146 INFO = 0
07147 DO 60 K = 1, N
07148 KM1 = K - 1
07149 KP1 = K + 1
07150 !
07151 !           Compute kth column of R.
07152 !           First, multiply the kth column of A by the previous
07153 !           k-1 Givens rotations.
07154 !
07155 IF (KM1 .LT. 1) GOTO 20
07156 DO 10 J = 1, KM1
07157 I = 2*(J-1) + 1
07158 T1 = A(J,K)
07159 T2 = A(J+1,K)
07160 C = Q(I)
07161 S = Q(I+1)
07162 A(J,K) = C*T1 - S*T2
07163 A(J+1,K) = S*T1 + C*T2
07164 10         CONTINUE
07165 !
07166 !           Compute Givens components c and s
07167 !
07168 20       CONTINUE
07169 IQ = 2*KM1 + 1
07170 T1 = A(K,K)
07171 T2 = A(KP1,K)
07172 IF (T2 .NE. 0.0D0) GOTO 30
07173 C = 1.0D0
07174 S = 0.0D0
07175 GOTO 50
07176 30       CONTINUE
07177 IF (ABS(T2) .LT. ABS(T1)) GOTO 40
07178 T = T1/T2
07179 S = -1.0D0/SQRT(1.0D0+T*T)
07180 C = -S*T
07181 GOTO 50
07182 40       CONTINUE
07183 T = T2/T1
07184 C = 1.0D0/SQRT(1.0D0+T*T)
07185 S = -C*T
07186 50       CONTINUE
07187 Q(IQ) = C
07188 Q(IQ+1) = S
07189 A(K,K) = C*T1 - S*T2
07190 IF (A(K,K) .EQ. 0.0D0) INFO = K
07191 60 CONTINUE
07192 RETURN
07193 !
07194 ! The old factorization of A will be updated.  A row and a column
07195 ! has been added to the matrix A.
07196 ! N by N-1 is now the old size of the matrix.
07197 !
07198 70  CONTINUE
07199 NM1 = N - 1
07200 !
07201 ! Multiply the new column by the N previous Givens rotations.
07202 !
07203 DO 100 K = 1,NM1
07204 I = 2*(K-1) + 1
07205 T1 = A(K,N)
07206 T2 = A(K+1,N)
07207 C = Q(I)
07208 S = Q(I+1)
07209 A(K,N) = C*T1 - S*T2
07210 A(K+1,N) = S*T1 + C*T2
07211 100    CONTINUE
07212 !
07213 ! Complete update of decomposition by forming last Givens rotation,
07214 ! and multiplying it times the column vector (A(N,N), A(N+1,N)).
07215 !
07216 INFO = 0
07217 T1 = A(N,N)
07218 T2 = A(N+1,N)
07219 IF (T2 .NE. 0.0D0) GOTO 110
07220 C = 1.0D0
07221 S = 0.0D0
07222 GOTO 130
07223 110  CONTINUE
07224 IF (ABS(T2) .LT. ABS(T1)) GOTO 120
07225 T = T1/T2
07226 S = -1.0D0/SQRT(1.0D0+T*T)
07227 C = -S*T
07228 GOTO 130
07229 120  CONTINUE
07230 T = T2/T1
07231 C = 1.0D0/SQRT(1.0D0+T*T)
07232 S = -C*T
07233 130  CONTINUE
07234 IQ = 2*N - 1
07235 Q(IQ) = C
07236 Q(IQ+1) = S
07237 A(N,N) = C*T1 - S*T2
07238 IF (A(N,N) .EQ. 0.0D0) INFO = N
07239 RETURN
07240 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DHEQR -----------------------
07241 END
07242 
07243 SUBROUTINE DHELS (A, LDA, N, Q, B)
07244 INTEGER LDA, N
07245 DOUBLE PRECISION A(LDA,*), B(*), Q(*)
07246 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07247 ! This is part of the LINPACK routine DGESL with changes
07248 ! due to the fact that A is an upper Hessenberg matrix.
07249 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07250 !     DHELS solves the least squares problem
07251 !
07252 !           min (b-A*x, b-A*x)
07253 !
07254 !     using the factors computed by DHEQR.
07255 !
07256 !     On entry
07257 !
07258 !        A       DOUBLE PRECISION(LDA, N)
07259 !                the output from DHEQR which contains the upper
07260 !                triangular factor R in the QR decomposition of A.
07261 !
07262 !        LDA     INTEGER
07263 !                the leading dimension of the array  A .
07264 !
07265 !        N       INTEGER
07266 !                A is originally an (N+1) by N matrix.
07267 !
07268 !        Q       DOUBLE PRECISION(2*N)
07269 !                The coefficients of the N givens rotations
07270 !                used in the QR factorization of A.
07271 !
07272 !        B       DOUBLE PRECISION(N+1)
07273 !                the right hand side vector.
07274 !
07275 !     On return
07276 !
07277 !        B       the solution vector  x .
07278 !
07279 !     Modification of LINPACK, by Peter Brown, LLNL.
07280 !     Written 1/13/86.  This version dated 6/20/01.
07281 !
07282 !     BLAS called: DAXPY
07283 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07284 INTEGER IQ, K, KB, KP1
07285 DOUBLE PRECISION C, S, T, T1, T2
07286 !
07287 !        Minimize (b-A*x, b-A*x)
07288 !        First form Q*b.
07289 !
07290 DO 20 K = 1, N
07291 KP1 = K + 1
07292 IQ = 2*(K-1) + 1
07293 C = Q(IQ)
07294 S = Q(IQ+1)
07295 T1 = B(K)
07296 T2 = B(KP1)
07297 B(K) = C*T1 - S*T2
07298 B(KP1) = S*T1 + C*T2
07299 20    CONTINUE
07300 !
07301 !        Now solve  R*x = Q*b.
07302 !
07303 DO 40 KB = 1, N
07304 K = N + 1 - KB
07305 B(K) = B(K)/A(K,K)
07306 T = -B(K)
07307 CALL DAXPY (K-1, T, A(1,K), 1, B(1), 1)
07308 40    CONTINUE
07309 RETURN
07310 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DHELS -----------------------
07311 END
07312 
07313 SUBROUTINE DLHIN (NEQ, N, T0, Y0, YDOT, F, TOUT, UROUND, EWT, ITOL, ATOL, Y, TEMP, H0, NITER, IER)
07314 EXTERNAL F
07315 DOUBLE PRECISION T0, Y0, YDOT, TOUT, UROUND, EWT, ATOL, Y, TEMP, H0
07316 INTEGER NEQ, N, ITOL, NITER, IER
07317 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y0(*), YDOT(*), EWT(*), ATOL(*), Y(*), TEMP(*)
07318 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07319 ! Call sequence input -- NEQ, N, T0, Y0, YDOT, F, TOUT, UROUND,
07320 !                        EWT, ITOL, ATOL, Y, TEMP
07321 ! Call sequence output -- H0, NITER, IER
07322 ! Common block variables accessed -- None
07323 !
07324 ! Subroutines called by DLHIN: F, DCOPY
07325 ! Function routines called by DLHIN: DVNORM
07326 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07327 ! This routine computes the step size, H0, to be attempted on the
07328 ! first step, when the user has not supplied a value for this.
07329 !
07330 ! First we check that TOUT - T0 differs significantly from zero.  Then
07331 ! an iteration is done to approximate the initial second derivative
07332 ! and this is used to define H from WRMS-norm(H**2 * yddot / 2) = 1.
07333 ! A bias factor of 1/2 is applied to the resulting h.
07334 ! The sign of H0 is inferred from the initial values of TOUT and T0.
07335 !
07336 ! Communication with DLHIN is done with the following variables:
07337 !
07338 ! NEQ    = NEQ array of solver, passed to F.
07339 ! N      = size of ODE system, input.
07340 ! T0     = initial value of independent variable, input.
07341 ! Y0     = vector of initial conditions, input.
07342 ! YDOT   = vector of initial first derivatives, input.
07343 ! F      = name of subroutine for right-hand side f(t,y), input.
07344 ! TOUT   = first output value of independent variable
07345 ! UROUND = machine unit roundoff
07346 ! EWT, ITOL, ATOL = error weights and tolerance parameters
07347 !                   as described in the driver routine, input.
07348 ! Y, TEMP = work arrays of length N.
07349 ! H0     = step size to be attempted, output.
07350 ! NITER  = number of iterations (and of f evaluations) to compute H0,
07351 !          output.
07352 ! IER    = the error flag, returned with the value
07353 !          IER = 0  if no trouble occurred, or
07354 !          IER = -1 if TOUT and t0 are considered too close to proceed.
07355 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07356 !
07357 ! Type declarations for local variables --------------------------------
07358 !
07359 DOUBLE PRECISION AFI, ATOLI, DELYI, HALF, HG, HLB, HNEW, HRAT, HUB, HUN, PT1, T1, TDIST, TROUND, TWO, DVNORM, YDDNRM
07360 INTEGER I, ITER
07361 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07362 ! The following Fortran-77 declaration is to cause the values of the
07363 ! listed (local) variables to be saved between calls to this integrator.
07364 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07365 SAVE HALF, HUN, PT1, TWO
07366 DATA HALF /0.5D0/, HUN /100.0D0/, PT1 /0.1D0/, TWO /2.0D0/
07367 !
07368 NITER = 0
07369 TDIST = ABS(TOUT - T0)
07370 TROUND = UROUND*MAX(ABS(T0),ABS(TOUT))
07371 IF (TDIST .LT. TWO*TROUND) GOTO 100
07372 !
07373 ! Set a lower bound on H based on the roundoff level in T0 and TOUT. ---
07374 HLB = HUN*TROUND
07375 ! Set an upper bound on H based on TOUT-T0 and the initial Y and YDOT. -
07376 HUB = PT1*TDIST
07377 ATOLI = ATOL(1)
07378 DO 10 I = 1,N
07379 IF (ITOL .EQ. 2 .OR. ITOL .EQ. 4) ATOLI = ATOL(I)
07380 DELYI = PT1*ABS(Y0(I)) + ATOLI
07381 AFI = ABS(YDOT(I))
07382 IF (AFI*HUB .GT. DELYI) HUB = DELYI/AFI
07383 10     CONTINUE
07384 !
07385 ! Set initial guess for H as geometric mean of upper and lower bounds. -
07386 ITER = 0
07387 HG = SQRT(HLB*HUB)
07388 ! If the bounds have crossed, exit with the mean value. ----------------
07389 IF (HUB .LT. HLB) THEN
07390 H0 = HG
07391 GOTO 90
07392 ENDIF
07393 !
07394 ! Looping point for iteration. -----------------------------------------
07395 50   CONTINUE
07396 ! Estimate the second derivative as a difference quotient in f. --------
07397 T1 = T0 + HG
07398 DO 60 I = 1,N
07399 60     Y(I) = Y0(I) + HG*YDOT(I)
07400 CALL F (NEQ, T1, Y, TEMP)
07401 DO 70 I = 1,N
07402 70     TEMP(I) = (TEMP(I) - YDOT(I))/HG
07403 YDDNRM = DVNORM (N, TEMP, EWT)
07404 ! Get the corresponding new value of H. --------------------------------
07405 IF (YDDNRM*HUB*HUB .GT. TWO) THEN
07406 HNEW = SQRT(TWO/YDDNRM)
07407 ELSE
07408 HNEW = SQRT(HG*HUB)
07409 ENDIF
07410 ITER = ITER + 1
07411 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07412 ! Test the stopping conditions.
07413 ! Stop if the new and previous H values differ by a factor of .lt. 2.
07414 ! Stop if four iterations have been done.  Also, stop with previous H
07415 ! if hnew/hg .gt. 2 after first iteration, as this probably means that
07416 ! the second derivative value is bad because of cancellation error.
07417 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07418 IF (ITER .GE. 4) GOTO 80
07419 HRAT = HNEW/HG
07420 IF ( (HRAT .GT. HALF) .AND. (HRAT .LT. TWO) ) GOTO 80
07421 IF ( (ITER .GE. 2) .AND. (HNEW .GT. TWO*HG) ) THEN
07422 HNEW = HG
07423 GOTO 80
07424 ENDIF
07425 HG = HNEW
07426 GOTO 50
07427 !
07428 ! Iteration done.  Apply bounds, bias factor, and sign. ----------------
07429 80   H0 = HNEW*HALF
07430 IF (H0 .LT. HLB) H0 = HLB
07431 IF (H0 .GT. HUB) H0 = HUB
07432 90   H0 = SIGN(H0, TOUT - T0)
07433 ! Restore Y array from Y0, then exit. ----------------------------------
07434 CALL DCOPY (N, Y0, 1, Y, 1)
07435 NITER = ITER
07436 IER = 0
07437 RETURN
07438 ! Error return for TOUT - T0 too small. --------------------------------
07439 100  IER = -1
07440 RETURN
07441 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DLHIN -----------------------
07442 END
07443 
07444 SUBROUTINE DSTOKA (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, SAVX, ACOR, WM, IWM, F, JAC, PSOL)
07445 EXTERNAL F, JAC, PSOL
07446 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
07447 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, SAVX, ACOR, WM
07448 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), YH1(*), EWT(*), SAVF(*), SAVX(*), ACOR(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
07449 INTEGER IOWND, IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM
07450 INTEGER LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
07451 INTEGER NEWT, NSFI, NSLJ, NJEV
07452 INTEGER JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
07453 DOUBLE PRECISION CONIT, CRATE, EL, ELCO, HOLD, RMAX, TESCO, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
07454 DOUBLE PRECISION STIFR
07455 DOUBLE PRECISION DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN
07456 COMMON /DLS001/ CONIT, CRATE, EL(13), ELCO(13,12), HOLD, RMAX, TESCO(3,12), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND,& 
07457 IOWND(6), IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, &
07458 LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
07459 COMMON /DLS002/ STIFR, NEWT, NSFI, NSLJ, NJEV
07460 COMMON /DLPK01/ DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN, JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
07461 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07462 ! DSTOKA performs one step of the integration of an initial value
07463 ! problem for a system of Ordinary Differential Equations.
07464 !
07465 ! This routine was derived from Subroutine DSTODPK in the DLSODPK
07466 ! package by the addition of automatic functional/Newton iteration
07467 ! switching and logic for re-use of Jacobian data.
07468 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07469 ! Note: DSTOKA is independent of the value of the iteration method
07470 ! indicator MITER, when this is .ne. 0, and hence is independent
07471 ! of the type of chord method used, or the Jacobian structure.
07472 ! Communication with DSTOKA is done with the following variables:
07473 !
07474 ! NEQ    = integer array containing problem size in NEQ(1), and
07475 !          passed as the NEQ argument in all calls to F and JAC.
07476 ! Y      = an array of length .ge. N used as the Y argument in
07477 !          all calls to F and JAC.
07478 ! YH     = an NYH by LMAX array containing the dependent variables
07479 !          and their approximate scaled derivatives, where
07480 !          LMAX = MAXORD + 1.  YH(i,j+1) contains the approximate
07481 !          j-th derivative of y(i), scaled by H**j/factorial(j)
07482 !          (j = 0,1,...,NQ).  On entry for the first step, the first
07483 !          two columns of YH must be set from the initial values.
07484 ! NYH    = a constant integer .ge. N, the first dimension of YH.
07485 ! YH1    = a one-dimensional array occupying the same space as YH.
07486 ! EWT    = an array of length N containing multiplicative weights
07487 !          for local error measurements.  Local errors in y(i) are
07488 !          compared to 1.0/EWT(i) in various error tests.
07489 ! SAVF   = an array of working storage, of length N.
07490 !          Also used for input of YH(*,MAXORD+2) when JSTART = -1
07491 !          and MAXORD .lt. the current order NQ.
07492 ! SAVX   = an array of working storage, of length N.
07493 ! ACOR   = a work array of length N, used for the accumulated
07494 !          corrections.  On a successful return, ACOR(i) contains
07495 !          the estimated one-step local error in y(i).
07496 ! WM,IWM = real and integer work arrays associated with matrix
07497 !          operations in chord iteration (MITER .ne. 0).
07498 ! CCMAX  = maximum relative change in H*EL0 before DSETPK is called.
07499 ! H      = the step size to be attempted on the next step.
07500 !          H is altered by the error control algorithm during the
07501 !          problem.  H can be either positive or negative, but its
07502 !          sign must remain constant throughout the problem.
07503 ! HMIN   = the minimum absolute value of the step size H to be used.
07504 ! HMXI   = inverse of the maximum absolute value of H to be used.
07505 !          HMXI = 0.0 is allowed and corresponds to an infinite HMAX.
07506 !          HMIN and HMXI may be changed at any time, but will not
07507 !          take effect until the next change of H is considered.
07508 ! TN     = the independent variable. TN is updated on each step taken.
07509 ! JSTART = an integer used for input only, with the following
07510 !          values and meanings:
07511 !               0  perform the first step.
07512 !           .gt.0  take a new step continuing from the last.
07513 !              -1  take the next step with a new value of H, MAXORD,
07514 !                    N, METH, MITER, and/or matrix parameters.
07515 !              -2  take the next step with a new value of H,
07516 !                    but with other inputs unchanged.
07517 !          On return, JSTART is set to 1 to facilitate continuation.
07518 ! KFLAG  = a completion code with the following meanings:
07519 !               0  the step was succesful.
07520 !              -1  the requested error could not be achieved.
07521 !              -2  corrector convergence could not be achieved.
07522 !              -3  fatal error in DSETPK or DSOLPK.
07523 !          A return with KFLAG = -1 or -2 means either
07524 !          ABS(H) = HMIN or 10 consecutive failures occurred.
07525 !          On a return with KFLAG negative, the values of TN and
07526 !          the YH array are as of the beginning of the last
07527 !          step, and H is the last step size attempted.
07528 ! MAXORD = the maximum order of integration method to be allowed.
07529 ! MAXCOR = the maximum number of corrector iterations allowed.
07530 ! MSBP   = maximum number of steps between DSETPK calls (MITER .gt. 0).
07531 ! MXNCF  = maximum number of convergence failures allowed.
07532 ! METH/MITER = the method flags.  See description in driver.
07533 ! N      = the number of first-order differential equations.
07534 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07535 INTEGER I, I1, IREDO, IRET, J, JB, JOK, M, NCF, NEWQ, NSLOW
07536 DOUBLE PRECISION DCON, DDN, DEL, DELP, DRC, DSM, DUP, EXDN, EXSM, EXUP, DFNORM, R, RH
07537 DOUBLE PRECISION RHDN, RHSM, RHUP, ROC, STIFF, TOLD, DVNORM
07538 !
07539 KFLAG = 0
07540 TOLD = TN
07541 NCF = 0
07542 IERPJ = 0
07543 IERSL = 0
07544 JCUR = 0
07545 ICF = 0
07546 DELP = 0.0D0
07547 IF (JSTART .GT. 0) GOTO 200
07548 IF (JSTART .EQ. -1) GOTO 100
07549 IF (JSTART .EQ. -2) GOTO 160
07550 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07551 ! On the first call, the order is set to 1, and other variables are
07552 ! initialized.  RMAX is the maximum ratio by which H can be increased
07553 ! in a single step.  It is initially 1.E4 to compensate for the small
07554 ! initial H, but then is normally equal to 10.  If a failure
07555 ! occurs (in corrector convergence or error test), RMAX is set at 2
07556 ! for the next increase.
07557 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07558 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
07559 NQ = 1
07560 L = 2
07561 IALTH = 2
07562 RMAX = 10000.0D0
07563 RC = 0.0D0
07564 EL0 = 1.0D0
07565 CRATE = 0.7D0
07566 HOLD = H
07567 MEO = METH
07568 NSLP = 0
07569 NSLJ = 0
07570 IPUP = 0
07571 IRET = 3
07572 NEWT = 0
07573 STIFR = 0.0D0
07574 GOTO 140
07575 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07576 ! The following block handles preliminaries needed when JSTART = -1.
07577 ! IPUP is set to MITER to force a matrix update.
07578 ! If an order increase is about to be considered (IALTH = 1),
07579 ! IALTH is reset to 2 to postpone consideration one more step.
07580 ! If the caller has changed METH, DCFODE is called to reset
07581 ! the coefficients of the method.
07582 ! If the caller has changed MAXORD to a value less than the current
07583 ! order NQ, NQ is reduced to MAXORD, and a new H chosen accordingly.
07584 ! If H is to be changed, YH must be rescaled.
07585 ! If H or METH is being changed, IALTH is reset to L = NQ + 1
07586 ! to prevent further changes in H for that many steps.
07587 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07588 100  IPUP = MITER
07589 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
07590 IF (IALTH .EQ. 1) IALTH = 2
07591 IF (METH .EQ. MEO) GOTO 110
07592 CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
07593 MEO = METH
07594 IF (NQ .GT. MAXORD) GOTO 120
07595 IALTH = L
07596 IRET = 1
07597 GOTO 150
07598 110  IF (NQ .LE. MAXORD) GOTO 160
07599 120  NQ = MAXORD
07600 L = LMAX
07601 DO 125 I = 1,L
07602 125    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
07603 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
07604 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
07605 EL0 = EL(1)
07606 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
07607 EPCON = CONIT*TESCO(2,NQ)
07608 DDN = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(1,L)
07609 EXDN = 1.0D0/L
07610 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
07611 RH = MIN(RHDN,1.0D0)
07612 IREDO = 3
07613 IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 170
07614 RH = MIN(RH,ABS(H/HOLD))
07615 H = HOLD
07616 GOTO 175
07617 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07618 ! DCFODE is called to get all the integration coefficients for the
07619 ! current METH.  Then the EL vector and related constants are reset
07620 ! whenever the order NQ is changed, or at the start of the problem.
07621 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07622 140  CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
07623 150  DO 155 I = 1,L
07624 155    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
07625 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
07626 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
07627 EL0 = EL(1)
07628 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
07629 EPCON = CONIT*TESCO(2,NQ)
07630 GOTO (160, 170, 200), IRET
07631 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07632 ! If H is being changed, the H ratio RH is checked against
07633 ! RMAX, HMIN, and HMXI, and the YH array rescaled.  IALTH is set to
07634 ! L = NQ + 1 to prevent a change of H for that many steps, unless
07635 ! forced by a convergence or error test failure.
07636 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07637 160  IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 200
07638 RH = H/HOLD
07639 H = HOLD
07640 IREDO = 3
07641 GOTO 175
07642 170  RH = MAX(RH,HMIN/ABS(H))
07643 175  RH = MIN(RH,RMAX)
07644 RH = RH/MAX(1.0D0,ABS(H)*HMXI*RH)
07645 R = 1.0D0
07646 DO 180 J = 2,L
07647 R = R*RH
07648 DO 180 I = 1,N
07649 180      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J)*R
07650 H = H*RH
07651 RC = RC*RH
07652 IALTH = L
07653 IF (IREDO .EQ. 0) GOTO 690
07654 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07655 ! This section computes the predicted values by effectively
07656 ! multiplying the YH array by the Pascal triangle matrix.
07657 ! The flag IPUP is set according to whether matrix data is involved
07658 ! (NEWT .gt. 0 .and. JACFLG .ne. 0) or not, to trigger a call to DSETPK.
07659 ! IPUP is set to MITER when RC differs from 1 by more than CCMAX,
07660 ! and at least every MSBP steps, when JACFLG = 1.
07661 ! RC is the ratio of new to old values of the coefficient  H*EL(1).
07662 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07663 200  IF (NEWT .EQ. 0 .OR. JACFLG .EQ. 0) THEN
07664 DRC = 0.0D0
07665 IPUP = 0
07666 CRATE = 0.7D0
07667 ELSE
07668 DRC = ABS(RC - 1.0D0)
07669 IF (DRC .GT. CCMAX) IPUP = MITER
07670 IF (NST .GE. NSLP+MSBP) IPUP = MITER
07671 ENDIF
07672 TN = TN + H
07673 I1 = NQNYH + 1
07674 DO 215 JB = 1,NQ
07675 I1 = I1 - NYH
07676 !DIR$ IVDEP
