07677 DO 210 I = I1,NQNYH
07678 210      YH1(I) = YH1(I) + YH1(I+NYH)
07679 215    CONTINUE
07680 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07681 ! Up to MAXCOR corrector iterations are taken.  A convergence test is
07682 ! made on the RMS-norm of each correction, weighted by the error
07683 ! weight vector EWT.  The sum of the corrections is accumulated in the
07684 ! vector ACOR(i).  The YH array is not altered in the corrector loop.
07685 ! Within the corrector loop, an estimated rate of convergence (ROC)
07686 ! and a stiffness ratio estimate (STIFF) are kept.  Corresponding
07687 ! global estimates are kept as CRATE and stifr.
07688 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07689 220  M = 0
07690 MNEWT = 0
07691 STIFF = 0.0D0
07692 ROC = 0.05D0
07693 NSLOW = 0
07694 DO 230 I = 1,N
07695 230    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
07696 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
07697 NFE = NFE + 1
07698 IF (NEWT .EQ. 0 .OR. IPUP .LE. 0) GOTO 250
07699 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07700 ! If indicated, DSETPK is called to update any matrix data needed,
07701 ! before starting the corrector iteration.
07702 ! JOK is set to indicate if the matrix data need not be recomputed.
07703 ! IPUP is set to 0 as an indicator that the matrix data is up to date.
07704 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07705 JOK = 1
07706 IF (NST .EQ. 0 .OR. NST .GT. NSLJ+50) JOK = -1
07707 IF (ICF .EQ. 1 .AND. DRC .LT. 0.2D0) JOK = -1
07708 IF (ICF .EQ. 2) JOK = -1
07709 IF (JOK .EQ. -1) THEN
07710 NSLJ = NST
07711 NJEV = NJEV + 1
07712 ENDIF
07713 CALL DSETPK (NEQ, Y, YH1, EWT, ACOR, SAVF, JOK, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
07714 IPUP = 0
07715 RC = 1.0D0
07716 DRC = 0.0D0
07717 NSLP = NST
07718 CRATE = 0.7D0
07719 IF (IERPJ .NE. 0) GOTO 430
07720 250  DO 260 I = 1,N
07721 260    ACOR(I) = 0.0D0
07722 270  IF (NEWT .NE. 0) GOTO 350
07723 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07724 ! In the case of functional iteration, update Y directly from
07725 ! the result of the last function evaluation, and STIFF is set to 1.0.
07726 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07727 DO 290 I = 1,N
07728 SAVF(I) = H*SAVF(I) - YH(I,2)
07729 290    Y(I) = SAVF(I) - ACOR(I)
07730 DEL = DVNORM (N, Y, EWT)
07731 DO 300 I = 1,N
07732 Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*SAVF(I)
07733 300    ACOR(I) = SAVF(I)
07734 STIFF = 1.0D0
07735 GOTO 400
07736 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07737 ! In the case of the chord method, compute the corrector error,
07738 ! and solve the linear system with that as right-hand side and
07739 ! P as coefficient matrix.  STIFF is set to the ratio of the norms
07740 ! of the residual and the correction vector.
07741 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07742 350  DO 360 I = 1,N
07743 360    SAVX(I) = H*SAVF(I) - (YH(I,2) + ACOR(I))
07744 DFNORM = DVNORM (N, SAVX, EWT)
07745 CALL DSOLPK (NEQ, Y, SAVF, SAVX, EWT, WM, IWM, F, PSOL)
07746 IF (IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 430
07747 IF (IERSL .GT. 0) GOTO 410
07748 DEL = DVNORM (N, SAVX, EWT)
07749 IF (DEL .GT. 1.0D-8) STIFF = MAX(STIFF, DFNORM/DEL)
07750 DO 380 I = 1,N
07751 ACOR(I) = ACOR(I) + SAVX(I)
07752 380    Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL(1)*ACOR(I)
07753 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07754 ! Test for convergence.  If M .gt. 0, an estimate of the convergence
07755 ! rate constant is made for the iteration switch, and is also used
07756 ! in the convergence test.   If the iteration seems to be diverging or
07757 ! converging at a slow rate (.gt. 0.8 more than once), it is stopped.
07758 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07759 400  IF (M .NE. 0) THEN
07760 ROC = MAX(0.05D0, DEL/DELP)
07761 CRATE = MAX(0.2D0*CRATE,ROC)
07762 ENDIF
07763 DCON = DEL*MIN(1.0D0,1.5D0*CRATE)/EPCON
07764 IF (DCON .LE. 1.0D0) GOTO 450
07765 M = M + 1
07766 IF (M .EQ. MAXCOR) GOTO 410
07767 IF (M .GE. 2 .AND. DEL .GT. 2.0D0*DELP) GOTO 410
07768 IF (ROC .GT. 10.0D0) GOTO 410
07769 IF (ROC .GT. 0.8D0) NSLOW = NSLOW + 1
07770 IF (NSLOW .GE. 2) GOTO 410
07771 MNEWT = M
07772 DELP = DEL
07773 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
07774 NFE = NFE + 1
07775 GOTO 270
07776 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07777 ! The corrector iteration failed to converge.
07778 ! If functional iteration is being done (NEWT = 0) and MITER .gt. 0
07779 ! (and this is not the first step), then switch to Newton
07780 ! (NEWT = MITER), and retry the step.  (Setting STIFR = 1023 insures
07781 ! that a switch back will not occur for 10 step attempts.)
07782 ! If Newton iteration is being done, but using a preconditioner that
07783 ! is out of date (JACFLG .ne. 0 .and. JCUR = 0), then signal for a
07784 ! re-evalutation of the preconditioner, and retry the step.
07785 ! In all other cases, the YH array is retracted to its values
07786 ! before prediction, and H is reduced, if possible.  If H cannot be
07787 ! reduced or MXNCF failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -2.
07788 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07789 410  ICF = 1
07790 IF (NEWT .EQ. 0) THEN
07791 IF (NST .EQ. 0) GOTO 430
07792 IF (MITER .EQ. 0) GOTO 430
07793 NEWT = MITER
07794 STIFR = 1023.0D0
07795 IPUP = MITER
07796 GOTO 220
07797 ENDIF
07798 IF (JCUR.EQ.1 .OR. JACFLG.EQ.0) GOTO 430
07799 IPUP = MITER
07800 GOTO 220
07801 430  ICF = 2
07802 NCF = NCF + 1
07803 NCFN = NCFN + 1
07804 RMAX = 2.0D0
07805 TN = TOLD
07806 I1 = NQNYH + 1
07807 DO 445 JB = 1,NQ
07808 I1 = I1 - NYH
07809 !DIR$ IVDEP
07810 DO 440 I = I1,NQNYH
07811 440      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
07812 445    CONTINUE
07813 IF (IERPJ .LT. 0 .OR. IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 680
07814 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 670
07815 IF (NCF .EQ. MXNCF) GOTO 670
07816 RH = 0.5D0
07817 IPUP = MITER
07818 IREDO = 1
07819 GOTO 170
07820 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07821 ! The corrector has converged.  JCUR is set to 0 to signal that the
07822 ! preconditioner involved may need updating later.
07823 ! The stiffness ratio STIFR is updated using the latest STIFF value.
07824 ! The local error test is made and control passes to statement 500
07825 ! if it fails.
07826 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07827 450  JCUR = 0
07828 IF (NEWT .GT. 0) STIFR = 0.5D0*(STIFR + STIFF)
07829 IF (M .EQ. 0) DSM = DEL/TESCO(2,NQ)
07830 IF (M .GT. 0) DSM = DVNORM (N, ACOR, EWT)/TESCO(2,NQ)
07831 IF (DSM .GT. 1.0D0) GOTO 500
07832 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07833 ! After a successful step, update the YH array.
07834 ! If Newton iteration is being done and STIFR is less than 1.5,
07835 ! then switch to functional iteration.
07836 ! Consider changing H if IALTH = 1.  Otherwise decrease IALTH by 1.
07837 ! If IALTH is then 1 and NQ .lt. MAXORD, then ACOR is saved for
07838 ! use in a possible order increase on the next step.
07839 ! If a change in H is considered, an increase or decrease in order
07840 ! by one is considered also.  A change in H is made only if it is by a
07841 ! factor of at least 1.1.  If not, IALTH is set to 3 to prevent
07842 ! testing for that many steps.
07843 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07844 KFLAG = 0
07845 IREDO = 0
07846 NST = NST + 1
07847 IF (NEWT .EQ. 0) NSFI = NSFI + 1
07848 IF (NEWT .GT. 0 .AND. STIFR .LT. 1.5D0) NEWT = 0
07849 HU = H
07850 NQU = NQ
07851 DO 470 J = 1,L
07852 DO 470 I = 1,N
07853 470      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J) + EL(J)*ACOR(I)
07854 IALTH = IALTH - 1
07855 IF (IALTH .EQ. 0) GOTO 520
07856 IF (IALTH .GT. 1) GOTO 700
07857 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 700
07858 DO 490 I = 1,N
07859 490    YH(I,LMAX) = ACOR(I)
07860 GOTO 700
07861 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07862 ! The error test failed.  KFLAG keeps track of multiple failures.
07863 ! Restore TN and the YH array to their previous values, and prepare
07864 ! to try the step again.  Compute the optimum step size for this or
07865 ! one lower order.  After 2 or more failures, H is forced to decrease
07866 ! by a factor of 0.2 or less.
07867 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07868 500  KFLAG = KFLAG - 1
07869 TN = TOLD
07870 I1 = NQNYH + 1
07871 DO 515 JB = 1,NQ
07872 I1 = I1 - NYH
07873 !DIR$ IVDEP
07874 DO 510 I = I1,NQNYH
07875 510      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
07876 515    CONTINUE
07877 RMAX = 2.0D0
07878 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 660
07879 IF (KFLAG .LE. -3) GOTO 640
07880 IREDO = 2
07881 RHUP = 0.0D0
07882 GOTO 540
07883 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07884 ! Regardless of the success or failure of the step, factors
07885 ! RHDN, RHSM, and RHUP are computed, by which H could be multiplied
07886 ! at order NQ - 1, order NQ, or order NQ + 1, respectively.
07887 ! in the case of failure, RHUP = 0.0 to avoid an order increase.
07888 ! the largest of these is determined and the new order chosen
07889 ! accordingly.  If the order is to be increased, we compute one
07890 ! additional scaled derivative.
07891 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07892 520  RHUP = 0.0D0
07893 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 540
07894 DO 530 I = 1,N
07895 530    SAVF(I) = ACOR(I) - YH(I,LMAX)
07896 DUP = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(3,NQ)
07897 EXUP = 1.0D0/(L+1)
07898 RHUP = 1.0D0/(1.4D0*DUP**EXUP + 0.0000014D0)
07899 540  EXSM = 1.0D0/L
07900 RHSM = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
07901 RHDN = 0.0D0
07902 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 560
07903 DDN = DVNORM (N, YH(1,L), EWT)/TESCO(1,NQ)
07904 EXDN = 1.0D0/NQ
07905 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
07906 560  IF (RHSM .GE. RHUP) GOTO 570
07907 IF (RHUP .GT. RHDN) GOTO 590
07908 GOTO 580
07909 570  IF (RHSM .LT. RHDN) GOTO 580
07910 NEWQ = NQ
07911 RH = RHSM
07912 GOTO 620
07913 580  NEWQ = NQ - 1
07914 RH = RHDN
07915 IF (KFLAG .LT. 0 .AND. RH .GT. 1.0D0) RH = 1.0D0
07916 GOTO 620
07917 590  NEWQ = L
07918 RH = RHUP
07919 IF (RH .LT. 1.1D0) GOTO 610
07920 R = EL(L)/L
07921 DO 600 I = 1,N
07922 600    YH(I,NEWQ+1) = ACOR(I)*R
07923 GOTO 630
07924 610  IALTH = 3
07925 GOTO 700
07926 620  IF ((KFLAG .EQ. 0) .AND. (RH .LT. 1.1D0)) GOTO 610
07927 IF (KFLAG .LE. -2) RH = MIN(RH,0.2D0)
07928 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07929 ! If there is a change of order, reset NQ, L, and the coefficients.
07930 ! In any case H is reset according to RH and the YH array is rescaled.
07931 ! Then exit from 690 if the step was OK, or redo the step otherwise.
07932 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07933 IF (NEWQ .EQ. NQ) GOTO 170
07934 630  NQ = NEWQ
07935 L = NQ + 1
07936 IRET = 2
07937 GOTO 150
07938 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07939 ! Control reaches this section if 3 or more failures have occured.
07940 ! If 10 failures have occurred, exit with KFLAG = -1.
07941 ! It is assumed that the derivatives that have accumulated in the
07942 ! YH array have errors of the wrong order.  Hence the first
07943 ! derivative is recomputed, and the order is set to 1.  Then
07944 ! H is reduced by a factor of 10, and the step is retried,
07945 ! until it succeeds or H reaches HMIN.
07946 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07947 640  IF (KFLAG .EQ. -10) GOTO 660
07948 RH = 0.1D0
07949 RH = MAX(HMIN/ABS(H),RH)
07950 H = H*RH
07951 DO 645 I = 1,N
07952 645    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
07953 CALL F (NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF)
07954 NFE = NFE + 1
07955 DO 650 I = 1,N
07956 650    YH(I,2) = H*SAVF(I)
07957 IPUP = MITER
07958 IALTH = 5
07959 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 200
07960 NQ = 1
07961 L = 2
07962 IRET = 3
07963 GOTO 150
07964 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07965 ! All returns are made through this section.  H is saved in HOLD
07966 ! to allow the caller to change H on the next step.
07967 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07968 660  KFLAG = -1
07969 GOTO 720
07970 670  KFLAG = -2
07971 GOTO 720
07972 680  KFLAG = -3
07973 GOTO 720
07974 690  RMAX = 10.0D0
07975 700  R = 1.0D0/TESCO(2,NQU)
07976 DO 710 I = 1,N
07977 710    ACOR(I) = ACOR(I)*R
07978 720  HOLD = H
07979 JSTART = 1
07980 RETURN
07981 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSTOKA ----------------------
07982 END
07983 
07984 SUBROUTINE DSETPK (NEQ, Y, YSV, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, JOK, WM, IWM, F, JAC)
07985 EXTERNAL F, JAC
07986 INTEGER NEQ, JOK, IWM
07987 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YSV, EWT, FTEM, SAVF, WM
07988 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YSV(*), EWT(*), FTEM(*), SAVF(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
07989 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
07990 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
07991 INTEGER JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
07992 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
07993 DOUBLE PRECISION DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN
07994 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
07995 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
07996 COMMON /DLPK01/ DELT, EPCON, SQRTN, RSQRTN, JPRE, JACFLG, LOCWP, LOCIWP, LSAVX, KMP, MAXL, MNEWT, NNI, NLI, NPS, NCFN, NCFL
07997 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
07998 ! DSETPK is called by DSTOKA to interface with the user-supplied
07999 ! routine JAC, to compute and process relevant parts of
08000 ! the matrix P = I - H*EL(1)*J , where J is the Jacobian df/dy,
08001 ! as need for preconditioning matrix operations later.
08002 !
08003 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
08004 ! with DSETPK uses the following:
08005 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
08006 ! YSV   = array containing predicted y, to be saved (YH1 in DSTOKA).
08007 ! FTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTOKA).
08008 ! SAVF  = array containing f evaluated at predicted y.
08009 ! JOK   = input flag showing whether it was judged that Jacobian matrix
08010 !         data need not be recomputed (JOK = 1) or needs to be
08011 !         (JOK = -1).
08012 ! WM    = real work space for matrices.
08013 !         Space for preconditioning data starts at WM(LOCWP).
08014 ! IWM   = integer work space.
08015 !         Space for preconditioning data starts at IWM(LOCIWP).
08016 ! IERPJ = output error flag,  = 0 if no trouble, .gt. 0 if
08017 !         JAC returned an error flag.
08018 ! JCUR  = output flag to indicate whether the matrix data involved
08019 !         is now current (JCUR = 1) or not (JCUR = 0).
08020 ! This routine also uses Common variables EL0, H, TN, IERPJ, JCUR, NJE.
08021 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08022 INTEGER IER
08023 DOUBLE PRECISION HL0
08024 !
08025 IERPJ = 0
08026 JCUR = 0
08027 IF (JOK .EQ. -1) JCUR = 1
08028 HL0 = EL0*H
08029 CALL JAC (F, NEQ, TN, Y, YSV, EWT, SAVF, FTEM, HL0, JOK, WM(LOCWP), IWM(LOCIWP), IER)
08030 NJE = NJE + 1
08031 IF (IER .EQ. 0) RETURN
08032 IERPJ = 1
08033 RETURN
08034 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSETPK ----------------------
08035 END
08036 
08037 SUBROUTINE DSRCKR (RSAV, ISAV, JOB)
08038 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08039 ! This routine saves or restores (depending on JOB) the contents of
08040 ! the Common blocks DLS001, DLS002, DLSR01, DLPK01, which
08041 ! are used internally by the DLSODKR solver.
08042 !
08043 ! RSAV = real array of length 228 or more.
08044 ! ISAV = integer array of length 63 or more.
08045 ! JOB  = flag indicating to save or restore the Common blocks:
08046 !        JOB  = 1 if Common is to be saved (written to RSAV/ISAV)
08047 !        JOB  = 2 if Common is to be restored (read from RSAV/ISAV)
08048 !        A call with JOB = 2 presumes a prior call with JOB = 1.
08049 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08050 INTEGER ISAV, JOB
08051 INTEGER ILS, ILS2, ILSR, ILSP
08052 INTEGER I, IOFF, LENILP, LENRLP, LENILS, LENRLS, LENILR, LENRLR
08053 DOUBLE PRECISION RSAV,   RLS, RLS2, RLSR, RLSP
08054 DIMENSION RSAV(*), ISAV(*)
08055 SAVE LENRLS, LENILS, LENRLP, LENILP, LENRLR, LENILR
08056 COMMON /DLS001/ RLS(218), ILS(37)
08057 COMMON /DLS002/ RLS2, ILS2(4)
08058 COMMON /DLSR01/ RLSR(5), ILSR(9)
08059 COMMON /DLPK01/ RLSP(4), ILSP(13)
08060 DATA LENRLS/218/, LENILS/37/, LENRLP/4/, LENILP/13/
08061 DATA LENRLR/5/, LENILR/9/
08062 !
08063 IF (JOB .EQ. 2) GOTO 100
08064 CALL DCOPY (LENRLS, RLS, 1, RSAV, 1)
08065 RSAV(LENRLS+1) = RLS2
08066 CALL DCOPY (LENRLR, RLSR, 1, RSAV(LENRLS+2), 1)
08067 CALL DCOPY (LENRLP, RLSP, 1, RSAV(LENRLS+LENRLR+2), 1)
08068 DO 20 I = 1,LENILS
08069 20     ISAV(I) = ILS(I)
08070 ISAV(LENILS+1) = ILS2(1)
08071 ISAV(LENILS+2) = ILS2(2)
08072 ISAV(LENILS+3) = ILS2(3)
08073 ISAV(LENILS+4) = ILS2(4)
08074 IOFF = LENILS + 2
08075 DO 30 I = 1,LENILR
08076 30     ISAV(IOFF+I) = ILSR(I)
08077 IOFF = IOFF + LENILR
08078 DO 40 I = 1,LENILP
08079 40     ISAV(IOFF+I) = ILSP(I)
08080 RETURN
08081 !
08082 100  CONTINUE
08083 CALL DCOPY (LENRLS, RSAV, 1, RLS, 1)
08084 RLS2 = RSAV(LENRLS+1)
08085 CALL DCOPY (LENRLR, RSAV(LENRLS+2), 1, RLSR, 1)
08086 CALL DCOPY (LENRLP, RSAV(LENRLS+LENRLR+2), 1, RLSP, 1)
08087 DO 120 I = 1,LENILS
08088 120    ILS(I) = ISAV(I)
08089 ILS2(1) = ISAV(LENILS+1)
08090 ILS2(2) = ISAV(LENILS+2)
08091 ILS2(3) = ISAV(LENILS+3)
08092 ILS2(4) = ISAV(LENILS+4)
08093 IOFF = LENILS + 2
08094 DO 130 I = 1,LENILR
08095 130    ILSR(I) = ISAV(IOFF+I)
08096 IOFF = IOFF + LENILR
08097 DO 140 I = 1,LENILP
08098 140    ILSP(I) = ISAV(IOFF+I)
08099 RETURN
08100 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSRCKR ----------------------
08101 END
08102 
08103 SUBROUTINE DAINVG (RES, ADDA, NEQ, T, Y, YDOT, MITER, ML, MU, PW, IPVT, IER )
08104 EXTERNAL RES, ADDA
08105 INTEGER NEQ, MITER, ML, MU, IPVT, IER
08106 INTEGER I, LENPW, MLP1, NROWPW
08107 DOUBLE PRECISION T, Y, YDOT, PW
08108 DIMENSION Y(*), YDOT(*), PW(*), IPVT(*)
08109 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08110 ! This subroutine computes the initial value
08111 ! of the vector YDOT satisfying
08112 !     A * YDOT = g(t,y)
08113 ! when A is nonsingular.  It is called by DLSODI for
08114 ! initialization only, when ISTATE = 0 .
08115 ! DAINVG returns an error flag IER:
08116 !   IER  =  0  means DAINVG was successful.
08117 !   IER .ge. 2 means RES returned an error flag IRES = IER.
08118 !   IER .lt. 0 means the a-matrix was found to be singular.
08119 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08120 !
08121 IF (MITER .GE. 4)  GOTO 100
08122 !
08123 ! Full matrix case -----------------------------------------------------
08124 !
08125 LENPW = NEQ*NEQ
08126 DO 10  I = 1, LENPW
08127 10    PW(I) = 0.0D0
08128 !
08129 IER = 1
08130 CALL RES ( NEQ, T, Y, PW, YDOT, IER )
08131 IF (IER .GT. 1) RETURN
08132 !
08133 CALL ADDA ( NEQ, T, Y, 0, 0, PW, NEQ )
08134 CALL DGEFA ( PW, NEQ, NEQ, IPVT, IER )
08135 IF (IER .EQ. 0) GOTO 20
08136 IER = -IER
08137 RETURN
08138 20 CALL DGESL ( PW, NEQ, NEQ, IPVT, YDOT, 0 )
08139 RETURN
08140 !
08141 ! Band matrix case -----------------------------------------------------
08142 !
08143 100 CONTINUE
08144 NROWPW = 2*ML + MU + 1
08145 LENPW = NEQ * NROWPW
08146 DO 110  I = 1, LENPW
08147 110    PW(I) = 0.0D0
08148 !
08149 IER = 1
08150 CALL RES ( NEQ, T, Y, PW, YDOT, IER )
08151 IF (IER .GT. 1) RETURN
08152 !
08153 MLP1 = ML + 1
08154 CALL ADDA ( NEQ, T, Y, ML, MU, PW(MLP1), NROWPW )
08155 CALL DGBFA ( PW, NROWPW, NEQ, ML, MU, IPVT, IER )
08156 IF (IER .EQ. 0) GOTO 120
08157 IER = -IER
08158 RETURN
08159 120 CALL DGBSL ( PW, NROWPW, NEQ, ML, MU, IPVT, YDOT, 0 )
08160 RETURN
08161 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DAINVG ----------------------
08162 END
08163 
08164 SUBROUTINE DSTODI (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, SAVR, ACOR, WM, IWM, RES, ADDA, JAC, PJAC, SLVS )
08165 EXTERNAL RES, ADDA, JAC, PJAC, SLVS
08166 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
08167 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, YH1, EWT, SAVF, SAVR, ACOR, WM
08168 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), YH1(*), EWT(*), SAVF(*), SAVR(*), ACOR(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
08169 INTEGER IOWND, IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM
08170 INTEGER LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
08171 DOUBLE PRECISION CONIT, CRATE, EL, ELCO, HOLD, RMAX, TESCO, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
08172 COMMON /DLS001/ CONIT, CRATE, EL(13), ELCO(13,12), HOLD, RMAX, TESCO(3,12), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, &
08173 IOWND(6), IALTH, IPUP, LMAX, MEO, NQNYH, NSLP, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, &
08174 LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
08175 INTEGER I, I1, IREDO, IRES, IRET, J, JB, KGO, M, NCF, NEWQ
08176 DOUBLE PRECISION DCON, DDN, DEL, DELP, DSM, DUP, ELJH, EL1H, EXDN, EXSM, EXUP, R, RH, RHDN, RHSM, RHUP, TOLD, DVNORM
08177 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08178 ! DSTODI performs one step of the integration of an initial value
08179 ! problem for a system of Ordinary Differential Equations.
08180 ! Note: DSTODI is independent of the value of the iteration method
08181 ! indicator MITER, and hence is independent
08182 ! of the type of chord method used, or the Jacobian structure.
08183 ! Communication with DSTODI is done with the following variables:
08184 !
08185 ! NEQ    = integer array containing problem size in NEQ(1), and
08186 !          passed as the NEQ argument in all calls to RES, ADDA,
08187 !          and JAC.
08188 ! Y      = an array of length .ge. N used as the Y argument in
08189 !          all calls to RES, JAC, and ADDA.
08190 ! NEQ    = integer array containing problem size in NEQ(1), and
08191 !          passed as the NEQ argument in all calls tO RES, G, ADDA,
08192 !          and JAC.
08193 ! YH     = an NYH by LMAX array containing the dependent variables
08194 !          and their approximate scaled derivatives, where
08195 !          LMAX = MAXORD + 1.  YH(i,j+1) contains the approximate
08196 !          j-th derivative of y(i), scaled by H**j/factorial(j)
08197 !          (j = 0,1,...,NQ).  On entry for the first step, the first
08198 !          two columns of YH must be set from the initial values.
08199 ! NYH    = a constant integer .ge. N, the first dimension of YH.
08200 ! YH1    = a one-dimensional array occupying the same space as YH.
08201 ! EWT    = an array of length N containing multiplicative weights
08202 !          for local error measurements.  Local errors in y(i) are
08203 !          compared to 1.0/EWT(i) in various error tests.
08204 ! SAVF   = an array of working storage, of length N. also used for
08205 !          input of YH(*,MAXORD+2) when JSTART = -1 and MAXORD is less
08206 !          than the current order NQ.
08207 !          Same as YDOTI in the driver.
08208 ! SAVR   = an array of working storage, of length N.
08209 ! ACOR   = a work array of length N used for the accumulated
08210 !          corrections. On a succesful return, ACOR(i) contains
08211 !          the estimated one-step local error in y(i).
08212 ! WM,IWM = real and integer work arrays associated with matrix
08213 !          operations in chord iteration.
08214 ! PJAC   = name of routine to evaluate and preprocess Jacobian matrix.
08215 ! SLVS   = name of routine to solve linear system in chord iteration.
08216 ! CCMAX  = maximum relative change in H*EL0 before PJAC is called.
08217 ! H      = the step size to be attempted on the next step.
08218 !          H is altered by the error control algorithm during the
08219 !          problem.  H can be either positive or negative, but its
08220 !          sign must remain constant throughout the problem.
08221 ! HMIN   = the minimum absolute value of the step size H to be used.
08222 ! HMXI   = inverse of the maximum absolute value of H to be used.
08223 !          HMXI = 0.0 is allowed and corresponds to an infinite HMAX.
08224 !          HMIN and HMXI may be changed at any time, but will not
08225 !          take effect until the next change of H is considered.
08226 ! TN     = the independent variable. TN is updated on each step taken.
08227 ! JSTART = an integer used for input only, with the following
08228 !          values and meanings:
08229 !               0  perform the first step.
08230 !           .gt.0  take a new step continuing from the last.
08231 !              -1  take the next step with a new value of H, MAXORD,
08232 !                    N, METH, MITER, and/or matrix parameters.
08233 !              -2  take the next step with a new value of H,
08234 !                    but with other inputs unchanged.
08235 !          On return, JSTART is set to 1 to facilitate continuation.
08236 ! KFLAG  = a completion code with the following meanings:
08237 !               0  the step was succesful.
08238 !              -1  the requested error could not be achieved.
08239 !              -2  corrector convergence could not be achieved.
08240 !              -3  RES ordered immediate return.
08241 !              -4  error condition from RES could not be avoided.
08242 !              -5  fatal error in PJAC or SLVS.
08243 !          A return with KFLAG = -1, -2, or -4 means either
08244 !          ABS(H) = HMIN or 10 consecutive failures occurred.
08245 !          On a return with KFLAG negative, the values of TN and
08246 !          the YH array are as of the beginning of the last
08247 !          step, and H is the last step size attempted.
08248 ! MAXORD = the maximum order of integration method to be allowed.
08249 ! MAXCOR = the maximum number of corrector iterations allowed.
08250 ! MSBP   = maximum number of steps between PJAC calls.
08251 ! MXNCF  = maximum number of convergence failures allowed.
08252 ! METH/MITER = the method flags.  See description in driver.
08253 ! N      = the number of first-order differential equations.
08254 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08255 KFLAG = 0
08256 TOLD = TN
08257 NCF = 0
08258 IERPJ = 0
08259 IERSL = 0
08260 JCUR = 0
08261 ICF = 0
08262 DELP = 0.0D0
08263 IF (JSTART .GT. 0) GOTO 200
08264 IF (JSTART .EQ. -1) GOTO 100
08265 IF (JSTART .EQ. -2) GOTO 160
08266 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08267 ! On the first call, the order is set to 1, and other variables are
08268 ! initialized.  RMAX is the maximum ratio by which H can be increased
08269 ! in a single step.  It is initially 1.E4 to compensate for the small
08270 ! initial H, but then is normally equal to 10.  If a failure
08271 ! occurs (in corrector convergence or error test), RMAX is set at 2
08272 ! for the next increase.
08273 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08274 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
08275 NQ = 1
08276 L = 2
08277 IALTH = 2
08278 RMAX = 10000.0D0
08279 RC = 0.0D0
08280 EL0 = 1.0D0
08281 CRATE = 0.7D0
08282 HOLD = H
08283 MEO = METH
08284 NSLP = 0
08285 IPUP = MITER
08286 IRET = 3
08287 GOTO 140
08288 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08289 ! The following block handles preliminaries needed when JSTART = -1.
08290 ! IPUP is set to MITER to force a matrix update.
08291 ! If an order increase is about to be considered (IALTH = 1),
08292 ! IALTH is reset to 2 to postpone consideration one more step.
08293 ! If the caller has changed METH, DCFODE is called to reset
08294 ! the coefficients of the method.
08295 ! If the caller has changed MAXORD to a value less than the current
08296 ! order NQ, NQ is reduced to MAXORD, and a new H chosen accordingly.
08297 ! If H is to be changed, YH must be rescaled.
08298 ! If H or METH is being changed, IALTH is reset to L = NQ + 1
08299 ! to prevent further changes in H for that many steps.
08300 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08301 100  IPUP = MITER
08302 LMAX = MAXORD + 1
08303 IF (IALTH .EQ. 1) IALTH = 2
08304 IF (METH .EQ. MEO) GOTO 110
08305 CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
08306 MEO = METH
08307 IF (NQ .GT. MAXORD) GOTO 120
08308 IALTH = L
08309 IRET = 1
08310 GOTO 150
08311 110  IF (NQ .LE. MAXORD) GOTO 160
08312 120  NQ = MAXORD
08313 L = LMAX
08314 DO 125 I = 1,L
08315 125    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
08316 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
08317 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
08318 EL0 = EL(1)
08319 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
08320 DDN = DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(1,L)
08321 EXDN = 1.0D0/L
08322 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
08323 RH = MIN(RHDN,1.0D0)
08324 IREDO = 3
08325 IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 170
08326 RH = MIN(RH,ABS(H/HOLD))
08327 H = HOLD
08328 GOTO 175
08329 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08330 ! DCFODE is called to get all the integration coefficients for the
08331 ! current METH.  Then the EL vector and related constants are reset
08332 ! whenever the order NQ is changed, or at the start of the problem.
08333 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08334 140  CALL DCFODE (METH, ELCO, TESCO)
08335 150  DO 155 I = 1,L
08336 155    EL(I) = ELCO(I,NQ)
08337 NQNYH = NQ*NYH
08338 RC = RC*EL(1)/EL0
08339 EL0 = EL(1)
08340 CONIT = 0.5D0/(NQ+2)
08341 GOTO (160, 170, 200), IRET
08342 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08343 ! If H is being changed, the H ratio RH is checked against
08344 ! RMAX, HMIN, and HMXI, and the YH array rescaled.  IALTH is set to
08345 ! L = NQ + 1 to prevent a change of H for that many steps, unless
08346 ! forced by a convergence or error test failure.
08347 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08348 160  IF (H .EQ. HOLD) GOTO 200
08349 RH = H/HOLD
08350 H = HOLD
08351 IREDO = 3
08352 GOTO 175
08353 170  RH = MAX(RH,HMIN/ABS(H))
08354 175  RH = MIN(RH,RMAX)
08355 RH = RH/MAX(1.0D0,ABS(H)*HMXI*RH)
08356 R = 1.0D0
08357 DO 180 J = 2,L
08358 R = R*RH
08359 DO 180 I = 1,N
08360 180      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J)*R
08361 H = H*RH
08362 RC = RC*RH
08363 IALTH = L
08364 IF (IREDO .EQ. 0) GOTO 690
08365 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08366 ! This section computes the predicted values by effectively
08367 ! multiplying the YH array by the Pascal triangle matrix.
08368 ! RC is the ratio of new to old values of the coefficient  H*EL(1).
08369 ! When RC differs from 1 by more than CCMAX, IPUP is set to MITER
08370 ! to force PJAC to be called.
08371 ! In any case, PJAC is called at least every MSBP steps.
08372 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08373 200  IF (ABS(RC-1.0D0) .GT. CCMAX) IPUP = MITER
08374 IF (NST .GE. NSLP+MSBP) IPUP = MITER
08375 TN = TN + H
08376 I1 = NQNYH + 1
08377 DO 215 JB = 1,NQ
08378 I1 = I1 - NYH
08379 !DIR$ IVDEP
08380 DO 210 I = I1,NQNYH
08381 210      YH1(I) = YH1(I) + YH1(I+NYH)
08382 215    CONTINUE
08383 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08384 ! Up to MAXCOR corrector iterations are taken.  A convergence test is
08385 ! made on the RMS-norm of each correction, weighted by H and the
08386 ! error weight vector EWT.  The sum of the corrections is accumulated
08387 ! in ACOR(i).  The YH array is not altered in the corrector loop.
08388 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08389 220  M = 0
08390 DO 230 I = 1,N
08391 SAVF(I) = YH(I,2) / H
08392 230    Y(I) = YH(I,1)
08393 IF (IPUP .LE. 0) GOTO 240
08394 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08395 ! If indicated, the matrix P = A - H*EL(1)*dr/dy is reevaluated and
08396 ! preprocessed before starting the corrector iteration.  IPUP is set
08397 ! to 0 as an indicator that this has been done.
08398 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08399 CALL PJAC (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, ACOR, SAVR, SAVF, WM, IWM, RES, JAC, ADDA )
08400 IPUP = 0
08401 RC = 1.0D0
08402 NSLP = NST
08403 CRATE = 0.7D0
08404 IF (IERPJ .EQ. 0) GOTO 250
08405 IF (IERPJ .LT. 0) GOTO 435
08406 IRES = IERPJ
08407 GOTO (430, 435, 430), IRES
08408 ! Get residual at predicted values, if not already done in PJAC. -------
08409 240  IRES = 1
08410 CALL RES ( NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, SAVR, IRES )
08411 NFE = NFE + 1
08412 KGO = ABS(IRES)
08413 GOTO ( 250, 435, 430 ) , KGO
08414 250  DO 260 I = 1,N
08415 260    ACOR(I) = 0.0D0
08416 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08417 ! Solve the linear system with the current residual as
08418 ! right-hand side and P as coefficient matrix.
08419 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08420 270  CONTINUE
08421 CALL SLVS (WM, IWM, SAVR, SAVF)
08422 IF (IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 430
08423 IF (IERSL .GT. 0) GOTO 410
08424 EL1H = EL(1) * H
08425 DEL = DVNORM (N, SAVR, EWT) * ABS(H)
08426 DO 380 I = 1,N
08427 ACOR(I) = ACOR(I) + SAVR(I)
08428 SAVF(I) = ACOR(I) + YH(I,2)/H
08429 380    Y(I) = YH(I,1) + EL1H*ACOR(I)
08430 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08431 ! Test for convergence.  If M .gt. 0, an estimate of the convergence
08432 ! rate constant is stored in CRATE, and this is used in the test.
08433 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08434 IF (M .NE. 0) CRATE = MAX(0.2D0*CRATE,DEL/DELP)
08435 DCON = DEL*MIN(1.0D0,1.5D0*CRATE)/(TESCO(2,NQ)*CONIT)
08436 IF (DCON .LE. 1.0D0) GOTO 460
08437 M = M + 1
08438 IF (M .EQ. MAXCOR) GOTO 410
08439 IF (M .GE. 2 .AND. DEL .GT. 2.0D0*DELP) GOTO 410
08440 DELP = DEL
08441 IRES = 1
08442 CALL RES ( NEQ, TN, Y, SAVF, SAVR, IRES )
08443 NFE = NFE + 1
08444 KGO = ABS(IRES)
08445 GOTO ( 270, 435, 410 ) , KGO
08446 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08447 ! The correctors failed to converge, or RES has returned abnormally.
08448 ! on a convergence failure, if the Jacobian is out of date, PJAC is
08449 ! called for the next try.  Otherwise the YH array is retracted to its
08450 ! values before prediction, and H is reduced, if possible.
08451 ! take an error exit if IRES = 2, or H cannot be reduced, or MXNCF
08452 ! failures have occurred, or a fatal error occurred in PJAC or SLVS.
08453 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08454 410  ICF = 1
08455 IF (JCUR .EQ. 1) GOTO 430
08456 IPUP = MITER
08457 GOTO 220
08458 430  ICF = 2
08459 NCF = NCF + 1
08460 RMAX = 2.0D0
08461 435  TN = TOLD
08462 I1 = NQNYH + 1
08463 DO 445 JB = 1,NQ
08464 I1 = I1 - NYH
08465 !DIR$ IVDEP
08466 DO 440 I = I1,NQNYH
08467 440      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
08468 445    CONTINUE
08469 IF (IRES .EQ. 2) GOTO 680
08470 IF (IERPJ .LT. 0 .OR. IERSL .LT. 0) GOTO 685
08471 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 450
08472 IF (NCF .EQ. MXNCF) GOTO 450
08473 RH = 0.25D0
08474 IPUP = MITER
08475 IREDO = 1
08476 GOTO 170
08477 450  IF (IRES .EQ. 3) GOTO 680
08478 GOTO 670
08479 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08480 ! The corrector has converged.  JCUR is set to 0
08481 ! to signal that the Jacobian involved may need updating later.
08482 ! The local error test is made and control passes to statement 500
08483 ! if it fails.
08484 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08485 460  JCUR = 0
08486 IF (M .EQ. 0) DSM = DEL/TESCO(2,NQ)
08487 IF (M .GT. 0) DSM = ABS(H) * DVNORM (N, ACOR, EWT)/TESCO(2,NQ)
08488 IF (DSM .GT. 1.0D0) GOTO 500
08489 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08490 ! After a successful step, update the YH array.
08491 ! Consider changing H if IALTH = 1.  Otherwise decrease IALTH by 1.
08492 ! If IALTH is then 1 and NQ .lt. MAXORD, then ACOR is saved for
08493 ! use in a possible order increase on the next step.
08494 ! If a change in H is considered, an increase or decrease in order
08495 ! by one is considered also.  A change in H is made only if it is by a
08496 ! factor of at least 1.1.  If not, IALTH is set to 3 to prevent
08497 ! testing for that many steps.
08498 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08499 KFLAG = 0
08500 IREDO = 0
08501 NST = NST + 1
08502 HU = H
08503 NQU = NQ
08504 DO 470 J = 1,L
08505 ELJH = EL(J)*H
08506 DO 470 I = 1,N
08507 470      YH(I,J) = YH(I,J) + ELJH*ACOR(I)
08508 IALTH = IALTH - 1
08509 IF (IALTH .EQ. 0) GOTO 520
08510 IF (IALTH .GT. 1) GOTO 700
08511 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 700
08512 DO 490 I = 1,N
08513 490    YH(I,LMAX) = ACOR(I)
08514 GOTO 700
08515 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08516 ! The error test failed.  KFLAG keeps track of multiple failures.
08517 ! restore TN and the YH array to their previous values, and prepare
08518 ! to try the step again.  Compute the optimum step size for this or
08519 ! one lower order.  After 2 or more failures, H is forced to decrease
08520 ! by a factor of 0.1 or less.
08521 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08522 500  KFLAG = KFLAG - 1
08523 TN = TOLD
08524 I1 = NQNYH + 1
08525 DO 515 JB = 1,NQ
08526 I1 = I1 - NYH
08527 !DIR$ IVDEP
08528 DO 510 I = I1,NQNYH
08529 510      YH1(I) = YH1(I) - YH1(I+NYH)
08530 515    CONTINUE
08531 RMAX = 2.0D0
08532 IF (ABS(H) .LE. HMIN*1.00001D0) GOTO 660
08533 IF (KFLAG .LE. -7) GOTO 660
08534 IREDO = 2
08535 RHUP = 0.0D0
08536 GOTO 540
08537 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08538 ! Regardless of the success or failure of the step, factors
08539 ! RHDN, RHSM, and RHUP are computed, by which H could be multiplied
08540 ! at order NQ - 1, order NQ, or order NQ + 1, respectively.
08541 ! In the case of failure, RHUP = 0.0 to avoid an order increase.
08542 ! The largest of these is determined and the new order chosen
08543 ! accordingly.  If the order is to be increased, we compute one
08544 ! additional scaled derivative.
08545 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08546 520  RHUP = 0.0D0
08547 IF (L .EQ. LMAX) GOTO 540
08548 DO 530 I = 1,N
08549 530    SAVF(I) = ACOR(I) - YH(I,LMAX)
08550 DUP = ABS(H) * DVNORM (N, SAVF, EWT)/TESCO(3,NQ)
08551 EXUP = 1.0D0/(L+1)
08552 RHUP = 1.0D0/(1.4D0*DUP**EXUP + 0.0000014D0)
08553 540  EXSM = 1.0D0/L
08554 RHSM = 1.0D0/(1.2D0*DSM**EXSM + 0.0000012D0)
08555 RHDN = 0.0D0
08556 IF (NQ .EQ. 1) GOTO 560
08557 DDN = DVNORM (N, YH(1,L), EWT)/TESCO(1,NQ)
08558 EXDN = 1.0D0/NQ
08559 RHDN = 1.0D0/(1.3D0*DDN**EXDN + 0.0000013D0)
08560 560  IF (RHSM .GE. RHUP) GOTO 570
08561 IF (RHUP .GT. RHDN) GOTO 590
08562 GOTO 580
08563 570  IF (RHSM .LT. RHDN) GOTO 580
08564 NEWQ = NQ
08565 RH = RHSM
08566 GOTO 620
08567 580  NEWQ = NQ - 1
08568 RH = RHDN
08569 IF (KFLAG .LT. 0 .AND. RH .GT. 1.0D0) RH = 1.0D0
08570 GOTO 620
08571 590  NEWQ = L
08572 RH = RHUP
08573 IF (RH .LT. 1.1D0) GOTO 610
08574 R = H*EL(L)/L
08575 DO 600 I = 1,N
08576 600    YH(I,NEWQ+1) = ACOR(I)*R
08577 GOTO 630
08578 610  IALTH = 3
08579 GOTO 700
08580 620  IF ((KFLAG .EQ. 0) .AND. (RH .LT. 1.1D0)) GOTO 610
08581 IF (KFLAG .LE. -2) RH = MIN(RH,0.1D0)
08582 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08583 ! If there is a change of order, reset NQ, L, and the coefficients.
08584 ! In any case H is reset according to RH and the YH array is rescaled.
08585 ! Then exit from 690 if the step was OK, or redo the step otherwise.
08586 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08587 IF (NEWQ .EQ. NQ) GOTO 170
08588 630  NQ = NEWQ
08589 L = NQ + 1
08590 IRET = 2
08591 GOTO 150
08592 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08593 ! All returns are made through this section.  H is saved in HOLD
08594 ! to allow the caller to change H on the next step.
08595 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08596 660  KFLAG = -1
08597 GOTO 720
08598 670  KFLAG = -2
08599 GOTO 720
08600 680  KFLAG = -1 - IRES
08601 GOTO 720
08602 685  KFLAG = -5
08603 GOTO 720
08604 690  RMAX = 10.0D0
08605 700  R = H/TESCO(2,NQU)
08606 DO 710 I = 1,N
08607 710    ACOR(I) = ACOR(I)*R
08608 720  HOLD = H
08609 JSTART = 1
08610 RETURN
08611 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSTODI ----------------------
08612 END
08613 
08614 SUBROUTINE DPREPJI (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, RTEM, SAVR, S, WM, IWM, RES, JAC, ADDA)
08615 EXTERNAL RES, JAC, ADDA
08616 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
08617 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, EWT, RTEM, SAVR, S, WM
08618 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), EWT(*), RTEM(*), S(*), SAVR(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
08619 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
08620 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
08621 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
08622 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
08623 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
08624 INTEGER I, I1, I2, IER, II, IRES, J, J1, JJ, LENP, MBA, MBAND, MEB1, MEBAND, ML, ML3, MU
08625 DOUBLE PRECISION CON, FAC, HL0, R, SRUR, YI, YJ, YJJ
08626 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08627 ! DPREPJI is called by DSTODI to compute and process the matrix
08628 ! P = A - H*EL(1)*J , where J is an approximation to the Jacobian dr/dy,
08629 ! where r = g(t,y) - A(t,y)*s.  Here J is computed by the user-supplied
08630 ! routine JAC if MITER = 1 or 4, or by finite differencing if MITER =
08631 ! 2 or 5.  J is stored in WM, rescaled, and ADDA is called to generate
08632 ! P. P is then subjected to LU decomposition in preparation
08633 ! for later solution of linear systems with P as coefficient
08634 ! matrix.  This is done by DGEFA if MITER = 1 or 2, and by
08635 ! DGBFA if MITER = 4 or 5.
08636 !
08637 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
08638 ! with DPREPJI uses the following:
08639 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
08640 ! RTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODI).
08641 ! SAVR  = array used for output only.  On output it contains the
08642 !         residual evaluated at current values of t and y.
08643 ! S     = array containing predicted values of dy/dt (SAVF in DSTODI).
08644 ! WM    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains the
08645 !         LU decomposition of P.
08646 !         Storage of matrix elements starts at WM(3).
08647 !         WM also contains the following matrix-related data:
08648 !         WM(1) = SQRT(UROUND), used in numerical Jacobian increments.
08649 ! IWM   = integer work space containing pivot information, starting at
08650 !         IWM(21).  IWM also contains the band parameters
08651 !         ML = IWM(1) and MU = IWM(2) if MITER is 4 or 5.
08652 ! EL0   = el(1) (input).
08653 ! IERPJ = output error flag.
08654 !         = 0 if no trouble occurred,
08655 !         = 1 if the P matrix was found to be singular,
08656 !         = IRES (= 2 or 3) if RES returned IRES = 2 or 3.
08657 ! JCUR  = output flag = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian matrix
08658 !         (or approximation) is now current.
08659 ! This routine also uses the Common variables EL0, H, TN, UROUND,
08660 ! MITER, N, NFE, and NJE.
08661 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08662 NJE = NJE + 1
08663 HL0 = H*EL0
08664 IERPJ = 0
08665 JCUR = 1
08666 GOTO (100, 200, 300, 400, 500), MITER
08667 ! If MITER = 1, call RES, then JAC, and multiply by scalar. ------------
08668 100  IRES = 1
08669 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08670 NFE = NFE + 1
08671 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08672 LENP = N*N
08673 DO 110 I = 1,LENP
08674 110    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
08675 CALL JAC ( NEQ, TN, Y, S, 0, 0, WM(3), N )
08676 CON = -HL0
08677 DO 120 I = 1,LENP
08678 120    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
08679 GOTO 240
08680 ! If MITER = 2, make N + 1 calls to RES to approximate J. --------------
08681 200  CONTINUE
08682 IRES = -1
08683 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08684 NFE = NFE + 1
08685 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08686 SRUR = WM(1)
08687 J1 = 2
08688 DO 230 J = 1,N
08689 YJ = Y(J)
08690 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YJ),0.01D0/EWT(J))
08691 Y(J) = Y(J) + R
08692 FAC = -HL0/R
08693 CALL RES ( NEQ, TN, Y, S, RTEM, IRES )
08694 NFE = NFE + 1
08695 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08696 DO 220 I = 1,N
08697 220      WM(I+J1) = (RTEM(I) - SAVR(I))*FAC
08698 Y(J) = YJ
08699 J1 = J1 + N
08700 230    CONTINUE
08701 IRES = 1
08702 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08703 NFE = NFE + 1
08704 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08705 ! Add matrix A. --------------------------------------------------------
08706 240  CONTINUE
08707 CALL ADDA(NEQ, TN, Y, 0, 0, WM(3), N)
08708 ! Do LU decomposition on P. --------------------------------------------
08709 CALL DGEFA (WM(3), N, N, IWM(21), IER)
08710 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
08711 RETURN
08712 ! Dummy section for MITER = 3
08713 300  RETURN
08714 ! If MITER = 4, call RES, then JAC, and multiply by scalar. ------------
08715 400  IRES = 1
08716 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08717 NFE = NFE + 1
08718 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08719 ML = IWM(1)
08720 MU = IWM(2)
08721 ML3 = ML + 3
08722 MBAND = ML + MU + 1
08723 MEBAND = MBAND + ML
08724 LENP = MEBAND*N
08725 DO 410 I = 1,LENP
08726 410    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
08727 CALL JAC ( NEQ, TN, Y, S, ML, MU, WM(ML3), MEBAND)
08728 CON = -HL0
08729 DO 420 I = 1,LENP
08730 420    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
08731 GOTO 570
08732 ! If MITER = 5, make ML + MU + 2 calls to RES to approximate J. --------
08733 500  CONTINUE
08734 IRES = -1
08735 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08736 NFE = NFE + 1
08737 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08738 ML = IWM(1)
08739 MU = IWM(2)
08740 ML3 = ML + 3
08741 MBAND = ML + MU + 1
08742 MBA = MIN(MBAND,N)
08743 MEBAND = MBAND + ML
08744 MEB1 = MEBAND - 1
08745 SRUR = WM(1)
08746 DO 560 J = 1,MBA
08747 DO 530 I = J,N,MBAND
08748 YI = Y(I)
08749 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YI),0.01D0/EWT(I))
08750 530      Y(I) = Y(I) + R
08751 CALL RES ( NEQ, TN, Y, S, RTEM, IRES)
08752 NFE = NFE + 1
08753 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08754 DO 550 JJ = J,N,MBAND
08755 Y(JJ) = YH(JJ,1)
08756 YJJ = Y(JJ)
08757 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(YJJ),0.01D0/EWT(JJ))
08758 FAC = -HL0/R
08759 I1 = MAX(JJ-MU,1)
08760 I2 = MIN(JJ+ML,N)
08761 II = JJ*MEB1 - ML + 2
08762 DO 540 I = I1,I2
08763 540        WM(II+I) = (RTEM(I) - SAVR(I))*FAC
08764 550      CONTINUE
08765 560    CONTINUE
08766 IRES = 1
08767 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08768 NFE = NFE + 1
08769 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08770 ! Add matrix A. --------------------------------------------------------
08771 570 CONTINUE
08772 CALL ADDA(NEQ, TN, Y, ML, MU, WM(ML3), MEBAND)
08773 ! Do LU decomposition of P. --------------------------------------------
08774 CALL DGBFA (WM(3), MEBAND, N, ML, MU, IWM(21), IER)
08775 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
08776 RETURN
08777 ! Error return for IRES = 2 or IRES = 3 return from RES. ---------------
08778 600  IERPJ = IRES
08779 RETURN
08780 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPREPJI ---------------------
08781 END
08782 
08783 SUBROUTINE DAIGBT (RES, ADDA, NEQ, T, Y, YDOT, MB, NB, PW, IPVT, IER )
08784 EXTERNAL RES, ADDA
08785 INTEGER NEQ, MB, NB, IPVT, IER
08786 INTEGER I, LENPW, LBLOX, LPB, LPC
08787 DOUBLE PRECISION T, Y, YDOT, PW
08788 DIMENSION Y(*), YDOT(*), PW(*), IPVT(*), NEQ(*)
08789 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08790 ! This subroutine computes the initial value
08791 ! of the vector YDOT satisfying
08792 !     A * YDOT = g(t,y)
08793 ! when A is nonsingular.  It is called by DLSOIBT for
08794 ! initialization only, when ISTATE = 0 .
08795 ! DAIGBT returns an error flag IER:
08796 !   IER  =  0  means DAIGBT was successful.
08797 !   IER .ge. 2 means RES returned an error flag IRES = IER.
08798 !   IER .lt. 0 means the A matrix was found to have a singular
08799 !              diagonal block (hence YDOT could not be solved for).
08800 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08801 LBLOX = MB*MB*NB
08802 LPB = 1 + LBLOX
08803 LPC = LPB + LBLOX
08804 LENPW = 3*LBLOX
08805 DO 10 I = 1,LENPW
08806 10     PW(I) = 0.0D0
08807 IER = 1
08808 CALL RES (NEQ, T, Y, PW, YDOT, IER)
08809 IF (IER .GT. 1) RETURN
08810 CALL ADDA (NEQ, T, Y, MB, NB, PW(1), PW(LPB), PW(LPC) )
08811 CALL DDECBT (MB, NB, PW, PW(LPB), PW(LPC), IPVT, IER)
08812 IF (IER .EQ. 0) GOTO 20
08813 IER = -IER
08814 RETURN
08815 20   CALL DSOLBT (MB, NB, PW, PW(LPB), PW(LPC), YDOT, IPVT)
08816 RETURN
08817 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DAIGBT ----------------------
08818 END
08819 
08820 SUBROUTINE DPJIBT (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, RTEM, SAVR, S, WM, IWM, RES, JAC, ADDA)
08821 EXTERNAL RES, JAC, ADDA
08822 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWM
08823 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, EWT, RTEM, SAVR, S, WM
08824 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), EWT(*), RTEM(*), S(*), SAVR(*), WM(*), IWM(*)
08825 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
08826 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
08827 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
08828 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
08829 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
08830 INTEGER I, IER, IIA, IIB, IIC, IPA, IPB, IPC, IRES, J, J1, J2, K, K1, LENP, LBLOX, LPB, LPC, MB, MBSQ, MWID, NB
08831 DOUBLE PRECISION CON, FAC, HL0, R, SRUR
08832 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08833 ! DPJIBT is called by DSTODI to compute and process the matrix
08834 ! P = A - H*EL(1)*J , where J is an approximation to the Jacobian dr/dy,
08835 ! and r = g(t,y) - A(t,y)*s.  Here J is computed by the user-supplied
08836 ! routine JAC if MITER = 1, or by finite differencing if MITER = 2.
08837 ! J is stored in WM, rescaled, and ADDA is called to generate P.
08838 ! P is then subjected to LU decomposition by DDECBT in preparation
08839 ! for later solution of linear systems with P as coefficient matrix.
08840 !
08841 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
08842 ! with DPJIBT uses the following:
08843 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
08844 ! RTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODI).
08845 ! SAVR  = array used for output only.  On output it contains the
08846 !         residual evaluated at current values of t and y.
08847 ! S     = array containing predicted values of dy/dt (SAVF in DSTODI).
08848 ! WM    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains the
08849 !         LU decomposition of P.
08850 !         Storage of matrix elements starts at WM(3).
08851 !         WM also contains the following matrix-related data:
08852 !         WM(1) = SQRT(UROUND), used in numerical Jacobian increments.
08853 ! IWM   = integer work space containing pivot information, starting at
08854 !         IWM(21).  IWM also contains block structure parameters
08855 !         MB = IWM(1) and NB = IWM(2).
08856 ! EL0   = EL(1) (input).
08857 ! IERPJ = output error flag.
08858 !         = 0 if no trouble occurred,
08859 !         = 1 if the P matrix was found to be unfactorable,
08860 !         = IRES (= 2 or 3) if RES returned IRES = 2 or 3.
08861 ! JCUR  = output flag = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian matrix
08862 !         (or approximation) is now current.
08863 ! This routine also uses the Common variables EL0, H, TN, UROUND,
08864 ! MITER, N, NFE, and NJE.
08865 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08866 NJE = NJE + 1
08867 HL0 = H*EL0
08868 IERPJ = 0
08869 JCUR = 1
08870 MB = IWM(1)
08871 NB = IWM(2)
08872 MBSQ = MB*MB
08873 LBLOX = MBSQ*NB
08874 LPB = 3 + LBLOX
08875 LPC = LPB + LBLOX
08876 LENP = 3*LBLOX
08877 GOTO (100, 200), MITER
08878 ! If MITER = 1, call RES, then JAC, and multiply by scalar. ------------
08879 100  IRES = 1
08880 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08881 NFE = NFE + 1
08882 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08883 DO 110 I = 1,LENP
08884 110    WM(I+2) = 0.0D0
08885 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, S, MB, NB, WM(3), WM(LPB), WM(LPC))
08886 CON = -HL0
08887 DO 120 I = 1,LENP
08888 120    WM(I+2) = WM(I+2)*CON
08889 GOTO 260
08890 !
08891 ! If MITER = 2, make 3*MB + 1 calls to RES to approximate J. -----------
08892 200  CONTINUE
08893 IRES = -1
08894 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08895 NFE = NFE + 1
08896 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08897 MWID = 3*MB
08898 SRUR = WM(1)
08899 DO 205 I = 1,LENP
08900 205    WM(2+I) = 0.0D0
08901 DO 250 K = 1,3
08902 DO 240 J = 1,MB
08903 !         Increment Y(I) for group of column indices, and call RES. ----
08904 J1 = J+(K-1)*MB
08905 DO 210 I = J1,N,MWID
08906 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(Y(I)),0.01D0/EWT(I))
08907 Y(I) = Y(I) + R
08908 210      CONTINUE
08909 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, RTEM, IRES)
08910 NFE = NFE + 1
08911 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08912 DO 215 I = 1,N
08913 215        RTEM(I) = RTEM(I) - SAVR(I)
08914 K1 = K
08915 DO 230 I = J1,N,MWID
08916 !           Get Jacobian elements in column I (block-column K1). -------
08917 Y(I) = YH(I,1)
08918 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(Y(I)),0.01D0/EWT(I))
08919 FAC = -HL0/R
08920 !           Compute and load elements PA(*,J,K1). ----------------------
08921 IIA = I - J
08922 IPA = 2 + (J-1)*MB + (K1-1)*MBSQ
08923 DO 221 J2 = 1,MB
08924 221          WM(IPA+J2) = RTEM(IIA+J2)*FAC
08925 IF (K1 .LE. 1) GOTO 223
08926 !           Compute and load elements PB(*,J,K1-1). --------------------
08927 IIB = IIA - MB
08928 IPB = IPA + LBLOX - MBSQ
08929 DO 222 J2 = 1,MB
08930 222          WM(IPB+J2) = RTEM(IIB+J2)*FAC
08931 223        CONTINUE
08932 IF (K1 .GE. NB) GOTO 225
08933 !           Compute and load elements PC(*,J,K1+1). --------------------
08934 IIC = IIA + MB
08935 IPC = IPA + 2*LBLOX + MBSQ
08936 DO 224 J2 = 1,MB
08937 224          WM(IPC+J2) = RTEM(IIC+J2)*FAC
08938 225        CONTINUE
08939 IF (K1 .NE. 3) GOTO 227
08940 !           Compute and load elements PC(*,J,1). -----------------------
08941 IPC = IPA - 2*MBSQ + 2*LBLOX
08942 DO 226 J2 = 1,MB
08943 226          WM(IPC+J2) = RTEM(J2)*FAC
08944 227        CONTINUE
08945 IF (K1 .NE. NB-2) GOTO 229
08946 !           Compute and load elements PB(*,J,NB). ----------------------
08947 IIB = N - MB
08948 IPB = IPA + 2*MBSQ + LBLOX
08949 DO 228 J2 = 1,MB
08950 228          WM(IPB+J2) = RTEM(IIB+J2)*FAC
08951 229      K1 = K1 + 3
08952 230      CONTINUE
08953 240    CONTINUE
08954 250  CONTINUE
08955 ! RES call for first corrector iteration. ------------------------------
08956 IRES = 1
08957 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
08958 NFE = NFE + 1
08959 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
08960 ! Add matrix A. --------------------------------------------------------
08961 260  CONTINUE
08962 CALL ADDA (NEQ, TN, Y, MB, NB, WM(3), WM(LPB), WM(LPC))
08963 ! Do LU decomposition on P. --------------------------------------------
08964 CALL DDECBT (MB, NB, WM(3), WM(LPB), WM(LPC), IWM(21), IER)
08965 IF (IER .NE. 0) IERPJ = 1
08966 RETURN
08967 ! Error return for IRES = 2 or IRES = 3 return from RES. ---------------
08968 600  IERPJ = IRES
08969 RETURN
08970 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPJIBT ----------------------
08971 END
08972 
08973 SUBROUTINE DSLSBT (WM, IWM, X, TEM)
08974 INTEGER IWM
08975 INTEGER LBLOX, LPB, LPC, MB, NB
08976 DOUBLE PRECISION WM, X, TEM
08977 DIMENSION WM(*), IWM(*), X(*), TEM(*)
08978 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08979 ! This routine acts as an interface between the core integrator
08980 ! routine and the DSOLBT routine for the solution of the linear system
08981 ! arising from chord iteration.
08982 ! Communication with DSLSBT uses the following variables:
08983 ! WM    = real work space containing the LU decomposition,
08984 !         starting at WM(3).
08985 ! IWM   = integer work space containing pivot information, starting at
08986 !         IWM(21).  IWM also contains block structure parameters
08987 !         MB = IWM(1) and NB = IWM(2).
08988 ! X     = the right-hand side vector on input, and the solution vector
08989 !         on output, of length N.
08990 ! TEM   = vector of work space of length N, not used in this version.
08991 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
08992 MB = IWM(1)
08993 NB = IWM(2)
08994 LBLOX = MB*MB*NB
08995 LPB = 3 + LBLOX
08996 LPC = LPB + LBLOX
08997 CALL DSOLBT (MB, NB, WM(3), WM(LPB), WM(LPC), X, IWM(21))
08998 RETURN
08999 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSLSBT ----------------------
09000 END
09001 
09002 SUBROUTINE DDECBT (M, N, A, B, C, IP, IER)
09003 INTEGER M, N, IP(M,N), IER
09004 DOUBLE PRECISION A(M,M,N), B(M,M,N), C(M,M,N)
09005 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09006 ! Block-tridiagonal matrix decomposition routine.
09007 ! Written by A. C. Hindmarsh.
09008 ! Latest revision:  November 10, 1983 (ACH)
09009 ! Reference:  UCID-30150
09010 !             Solution of Block-Tridiagonal Systems of Linear
09011 !             Algebraic Equations
09012 !             A.C. Hindmarsh
09013 !             February 1977
09014 ! The input matrix contains three blocks of elements in each block-row,
09015 ! including blocks in the (1,3) and (N,N-2) block positions.
09016 ! DDECBT uses block Gauss elimination and Subroutines DGEFA and DGESL
09017 ! for solution of blocks.  Partial pivoting is done within
09018 ! block-rows only.
09019 !
09020 ! Note: this version uses LINPACK routines DGEFA/DGESL instead of
09021 ! of dec/sol for solution of blocks, and it uses the BLAS routine DDOT
09022 ! for dot product calculations.
09023 !
09024 ! Input:
09025 !     M = order of each block.
09026 !     N = number of blocks in each direction of the matrix.
09027 !         N must be 4 or more.  The complete matrix has order M*N.
09028 !     A = M by M by N array containing diagonal blocks.
09029 !         A(i,j,k) contains the (i,j) element of the k-th block.
09030 !     B = M by M by N array containing the super-diagonal blocks
09031 !         (in B(*,*,k) for k = 1,...,N-1) and the block in the (N,N-2)
09032 !         block position (in B(*,*,N)).
09033 !     C = M by M by N array containing the subdiagonal blocks
09034 !         (in C(*,*,k) for k = 2,3,...,N) and the block in the
09035 !         (1,3) block position (in C(*,*,1)).
09036 !    IP = integer array of length M*N for working storage.
09037 ! Output:
09038 ! A,B,C = M by M by N arrays containing the block-LU decomposition
09039 !         of the input matrix.
09040 !    IP = M by N array of pivot information.  IP(*,k) contains
09041 !         information for the k-th digonal block.
09042 !   IER = 0  if no trouble occurred, or
09043 !       = -1 if the input value of M or N was illegal, or
09044 !       = k  if a singular matrix was found in the k-th diagonal block.
09045 ! Use DSOLBT to solve the associated linear system.
09046 !
09047 ! External routines required: DGEFA and DGESL (from LINPACK) and
09048 ! DDOT (from the BLAS, or Basic Linear Algebra package).
09049 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09050 INTEGER NM1, NM2, KM1, I, J, K
09051 DOUBLE PRECISION DP, DDOT
09052 IF (M .LT. 1 .OR. N .LT. 4) GOTO 210
09053 NM1 = N - 1
09054 NM2 = N - 2
09055 ! Process the first block-row. -----------------------------------------
09056 CALL DGEFA (A, M, M, IP, IER)
09057 K = 1
09058 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 200
09059 DO 10 J = 1,M
09060 CALL DGESL (A, M, M, IP, B(1,J,1), 0)
09061 CALL DGESL (A, M, M, IP, C(1,J,1), 0)
09062 10     CONTINUE
09063 ! Adjust B(*,*,2). -----------------------------------------------------
09064 DO 40 J = 1,M
09065 DO 30 I = 1,M
09066 DP = DDOT (M, C(I,1,2), M, C(1,J,1), 1)
09067 B(I,J,2) = B(I,J,2) - DP
09068 30       CONTINUE
09069 40     CONTINUE
09070 ! Main loop.  Process block-rows 2 to N-1. -----------------------------
09071 DO 100 K = 2,NM1
09072 KM1 = K - 1
09073 DO 70 J = 1,M
09074 DO 60 I = 1,M
09075 DP = DDOT (M, C(I,1,K), M, B(1,J,KM1), 1)
09076 A(I,J,K) = A(I,J,K) - DP
09077 60         CONTINUE
09078 70       CONTINUE
09079 CALL DGEFA (A(1,1,K), M, M, IP(1,K), IER)
09080 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 200
09081 DO 80 J = 1,M
09082 80       CALL DGESL (A(1,1,K), M, M, IP(1,K), B(1,J,K), 0)
09083 100    CONTINUE
09084 ! Process last block-row and return. -----------------------------------
09085 DO 130 J = 1,M
09086 DO 120 I = 1,M
09087 DP = DDOT (M, B(I,1,N), M, B(1,J,NM2), 1)
09088 C(I,J,N) = C(I,J,N) - DP
09089 120      CONTINUE
09090 130    CONTINUE
09091 DO 160 J = 1,M
09092 DO 150 I = 1,M
09093 DP = DDOT (M, C(I,1,N), M, B(1,J,NM1), 1)
09094 A(I,J,N) = A(I,J,N) - DP
09095 150      CONTINUE
09096 160    CONTINUE
09097 CALL DGEFA (A(1,1,N), M, M, IP(1,N), IER)
09098 K = N
09099 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 200
09100 RETURN
09101 ! Error returns. -------------------------------------------------------
09102 200  IER = K
09103 RETURN
09104 210  IER = -1
09105 RETURN
09106 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DDECBT ----------------------
09107 END
09108 
09109 SUBROUTINE DSOLBT (M, N, A, B, C, Y, IP)
09110 INTEGER M, N, IP(M,N)
09111 DOUBLE PRECISION A(M,M,N), B(M,M,N), C(M,M,N), Y(M,N)
09112 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09113 ! Solution of block-tridiagonal linear system.
09114 ! Coefficient matrix must have been previously processed by DDECBT.
09115 ! M, N, A,B,C, and IP  must not have been changed since call to DDECBT.
09116 ! Written by A. C. Hindmarsh.
09117 ! Input:
09118 !     M = order of each block.
09119 !     N = number of blocks in each direction of matrix.
09120 ! A,B,C = M by M by N arrays containing block LU decomposition
09121 !         of coefficient matrix from DDECBT.
09122 !    IP = M by N integer array of pivot information from DDECBT.
09123 !     Y = array of length M*N containg the right-hand side vector
09124 !         (treated as an M by N array here).
09125 ! Output:
09126 !     Y = solution vector, of length M*N.
09127 !
09128 ! External routines required: DGESL (LINPACK) and DDOT (BLAS).
09129 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09130 !
09131 INTEGER NM1, NM2, I, K, KB, KM1, KP1
09132 DOUBLE PRECISION DP, DDOT
09133 NM1 = N - 1
09134 NM2 = N - 2
09135 ! Forward solution sweep. ----------------------------------------------
09136 CALL DGESL (A, M, M, IP, Y, 0)
09137 DO 30 K = 2,NM1
09138 KM1 = K - 1
09139 DO 20 I = 1,M
09140 DP = DDOT (M, C(I,1,K), M, Y(1,KM1), 1)
09141 Y(I,K) = Y(I,K) - DP
09142 20       CONTINUE
09143 CALL DGESL (A(1,1,K), M, M, IP(1,K), Y(1,K), 0)
09144 30     CONTINUE
09145 DO 50 I = 1,M
09146 DP = DDOT (M, C(I,1,N), M, Y(1,NM1), 1) + DDOT (M, B(I,1,N), M, Y(1,NM2), 1)
09147 Y(I,N) = Y(I,N) - DP
09148 50     CONTINUE
09149 CALL DGESL (A(1,1,N), M, M, IP(1,N), Y(1,N), 0)
09150 ! Backward solution sweep. ---------------------------------------------
09151 DO 80 KB = 1,NM1
09152 K = N - KB
09153 KP1 = K + 1
09154 DO 70 I = 1,M
09155 DP = DDOT (M, B(I,1,K), M, Y(1,KP1), 1)
09156 Y(I,K) = Y(I,K) - DP
09157 70       CONTINUE
09158 80     CONTINUE
09159 DO 100 I = 1,M
09160 DP = DDOT (M, C(I,1,1), M, Y(1,3), 1)
09161 Y(I,1) = Y(I,1) - DP
09162 100    CONTINUE
09163 RETURN
09164 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DSOLBT ----------------------
09165 END
09166 
09167 SUBROUTINE DIPREPI (NEQ, Y, S, RWORK, IA, JA, IC, JC, IPFLAG, RES, JAC, ADDA)
09168 EXTERNAL RES, JAC, ADDA
09169 INTEGER NEQ, IA, JA, IC, JC, IPFLAG
09170 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, S, RWORK
09171 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), S(*), RWORK(*), IA(*), JA(*), IC(*), JC(*)
09172 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, 
09173 MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
09174 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
09175 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09176 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
09177 DOUBLE PRECISION RLSS
09178 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
09179 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
09180 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, &
09181 IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09182 INTEGER I, IMAX, LEWTN, LYHD, LYHN
09183 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09184 ! This routine serves as an interface between the driver and
09185 ! Subroutine DPREPI.  Tasks performed here are:
09186 !  * call DPREPI,
09187 !  * reset the required WM segment length LENWK,
09188 !  * move YH back to its final location (following WM in RWORK),
09189 !  * reset pointers for YH, SAVR, EWT, and ACOR, and
09190 !  * move EWT to its new position if ISTATE = 0 or 1.
09191 ! IPFLAG is an output error indication flag.  IPFLAG = 0 if there was
09192 ! no trouble, and IPFLAG is the value of the DPREPI error flag IPPER
09193 ! if there was trouble in Subroutine DPREPI.
09194 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09195 IPFLAG = 0
09196 ! Call DPREPI to do matrix preprocessing operations. -------------------
09197 CALL DPREPI (NEQ, Y, S, RWORK(LYH), RWORK(LSAVF), RWORK(LEWT), RWORK(LACOR), IA, JA, IC, JC, RWORK(LWM), RWORK(LWM), IPFLAG,&
09198 RES, JAC, ADDA)
09199 LENWK = MAX(LREQ,LWMIN)
09200 IF (IPFLAG .LT. 0) RETURN
09201 ! If DPREPI was successful, move YH to end of required space for WM. ---
09202 LYHN = LWM + LENWK
09203 IF (LYHN .GT. LYH) RETURN
09204 LYHD = LYH - LYHN
09205 IF (LYHD .EQ. 0) GOTO 20
09206 IMAX = LYHN - 1 + LENYHM
09207 DO 10 I=LYHN,IMAX
09208 10     RWORK(I) = RWORK(I+LYHD)
09209 LYH = LYHN
09210 ! Reset pointers for SAVR, EWT, and ACOR. ------------------------------
09211 20   LSAVF = LYH + LENYH
09212 LEWTN = LSAVF + N
09213 LACOR = LEWTN + N
09214 IF (ISTATC .EQ. 3) GOTO 40
09215 ! If ISTATE = 1, move EWT (left) to its new position. ------------------
09216 IF (LEWTN .GT. LEWT) RETURN
09217 DO 30 I=1,N
09218 30     RWORK(I+LEWTN-1) = RWORK(I+LEWT-1)
09219 40   LEWT = LEWTN
09220 RETURN
09221 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DIPREPI ---------------------
09222 END
09223 
09224 SUBROUTINE DPREPI (NEQ, Y, S, YH, SAVR, EWT, RTEM, IA, JA, IC, JC, WK, IWK, IPPER, RES, JAC, ADDA)
09225 EXTERNAL RES, JAC, ADDA
09226 INTEGER NEQ, IA, JA, IC, JC, IWK, IPPER
09227 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, S, YH, SAVR, EWT, RTEM, WK
09228 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), S(*), YH(*), SAVR(*), EWT(*), RTEM(*), IA(*), JA(*), IC(*), JC(*), WK(*), IWK(*)
09229 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD
09230 INTEGER MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
09231 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
09232 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09233 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
09234 DOUBLE PRECISION RLSS
09235 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
09236 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
09237 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, &
09238 IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09239 INTEGER I, IBR, IER, IPIL, IPIU, IPTT1, IPTT2, J, K, KNEW, KAMAX, KAMIN, KCMAX, KCMIN, LDIF, LENIGP, LENWK1, LIWK, LJFO
09240 INTEGER MAXG, NP1, NZSUT
09241 DOUBLE PRECISION ERWT, FAC, YJ
09242 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09243 ! This routine performs preprocessing related to the sparse linear
09244 ! systems that must be solved.
09245 ! The operations that are performed here are:
09246 !  * compute sparseness structure of the iteration matrix
09247 !      P = A - con*J  according to MOSS,
09248 !  * compute grouping of column indices (MITER = 2),
09249 !  * compute a new ordering of rows and columns of the matrix,
09250 !  * reorder JA corresponding to the new ordering,
09251 !  * perform a symbolic LU factorization of the matrix, and
09252 !  * set pointers for segments of the IWK/WK array.
09253 ! In addition to variables described previously, DPREPI uses the
09254 ! following for communication:
09255 ! YH     = the history array.  Only the first column, containing the
09256 !          current Y vector, is used.  Used only if MOSS .ne. 0.
09257 ! S      = array of length NEQ, identical to YDOTI in the driver, used
09258 !          only if MOSS .ne. 0.
09259 ! SAVR   = a work array of length NEQ, used only if MOSS .ne. 0.
09260 ! EWT    = array of length NEQ containing (inverted) error weights.
09261 !          Used only if MOSS = 2 or 4 or if ISTATE = MOSS = 1.
09262 ! RTEM   = a work array of length NEQ, identical to ACOR in the driver,
09263 !          used only if MOSS = 2 or 4.
09264 ! WK     = a real work array of length LENWK, identical to WM in
09265 !          the driver.
09266 ! IWK    = integer work array, assumed to occupy the same space as WK.
09267 ! LENWK  = the length of the work arrays WK and IWK.
09268 ! ISTATC = a copy of the driver input argument ISTATE (= 1 on the
09269 !          first call, = 3 on a continuation call).
09270 ! IYS    = flag value from ODRV or CDRV.
09271 ! IPPER  = output error flag , with the following values and meanings:
09272 !        =   0  no error.
09273 !        =  -1  insufficient storage for internal structure pointers.
09274 !        =  -2  insufficient storage for JGROUP.
09275 !        =  -3  insufficient storage for ODRV.
09276 !        =  -4  other error flag from ODRV (should never occur).
09277 !        =  -5  insufficient storage for CDRV.
09278 !        =  -6  other error flag from CDRV.
09279 !        =  -7  if the RES routine returned error flag IRES = IER = 2.
09280 !        =  -8  if the RES routine returned error flag IRES = IER = 3.
09281 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09282 IBIAN = LRAT*2
09283 IPIAN = IBIAN + 1
09284 NP1 = N + 1
09285 IPJAN = IPIAN + NP1
09286 IBJAN = IPJAN - 1
09287 LENWK1 = LENWK - N
09288 LIWK = LENWK*LRAT
09289 IF (MOSS .EQ. 0) LIWK = LIWK - N
09290 IF (MOSS .EQ. 1 .OR. MOSS .EQ. 2) LIWK = LENWK1*LRAT
09291 IF (IPJAN+N-1 .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09292 IF (MOSS .EQ. 0) GOTO 30
09293 !
09294 IF (ISTATC .EQ. 3) GOTO 20
09295 ! ISTATE = 1 and MOSS .ne. 0.  Perturb Y for structure determination.
09296 ! Initialize S with random nonzero elements for structure determination.
09297 DO 10 I=1,N
09298 ERWT = 1.0D0/EWT(I)
09299 FAC = 1.0D0 + 1.0D0/(I + 1.0D0)
09300 Y(I) = Y(I) + FAC*SIGN(ERWT,Y(I))
09301 S(I) = 1.0D0 + FAC*ERWT
09302 10     CONTINUE
09303 GOTO (70, 100, 150, 200), MOSS
09304 !
09305 20   CONTINUE
09306 ! ISTATE = 3 and MOSS .ne. 0. Load Y from YH(*,1) and S from YH(*,2). --
09307 DO 25 I = 1,N
09308 Y(I) = YH(I)
09309 25      S(I) = YH(N+I)
09310 GOTO (70, 100, 150, 200), MOSS
09311 !
09312 ! MOSS = 0. Process user's IA,JA and IC,JC. ----------------------------
09313 30   KNEW = IPJAN
09314 KAMIN = IA(1)
09315 KCMIN = IC(1)
09316 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
09317 DO 60 J = 1,N
09318 DO 35 I = 1,N
09319 35       IWK(LIWK+I) = 0
09320 KAMAX = IA(J+1) - 1
09321 IF (KAMIN .GT. KAMAX) GOTO 45
09322 DO 40 K = KAMIN,KAMAX
09323 I = JA(K)
09324 IWK(LIWK+I) = 1
09325 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09326 IWK(KNEW) = I
09327 KNEW = KNEW + 1
09328 40       CONTINUE
09329 45     KAMIN = KAMAX + 1
09330 KCMAX = IC(J+1) - 1
09331 IF (KCMIN .GT. KCMAX) GOTO 55
09332 DO 50 K = KCMIN,KCMAX
09333 I = JC(K)
09334 IF (IWK(LIWK+I) .NE. 0) GOTO 50
09335 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09336 IWK(KNEW) = I
09337 KNEW = KNEW + 1
09338 50       CONTINUE
09339 55     IWK(IPIAN+J) = KNEW + 1 - IPJAN
09340 KCMIN = KCMAX + 1
09341 60     CONTINUE
09342 GOTO 240
09343 !
09344 ! MOSS = 1. Compute structure from user-supplied Jacobian routine JAC. -
09345 70   CONTINUE
09346 ! A dummy call to RES allows user to create temporaries for use in JAC.
09347 IER = 1
09348 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IER)
09349 IF (IER .GT. 1) GOTO 370
09350 DO 75 I = 1,N
09351 SAVR(I) = 0.0D0
09352 75     WK(LENWK1+I) = 0.0D0
09353 K = IPJAN
09354 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
09355 DO 95 J = 1,N
09356 CALL ADDA (NEQ, TN, Y, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), WK(LENWK1+1))
09357 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, S, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), SAVR)
09358 DO 90 I = 1,N
09359 LJFO = LENWK1 + I
09360 IF (WK(LJFO) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 80
09361 WK(LJFO) = 0.0D0
09362 SAVR(I) = 0.0D0
09363 GOTO 85
09364 80       IF (SAVR(I) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 90
09365 SAVR(I) = 0.0D0
09366 85       IF (K .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09367 IWK(K) = I
09368 K = K+1
09369 90       CONTINUE
09370 IWK(IPIAN+J) = K + 1 - IPJAN
09371 95     CONTINUE
09372 GOTO 240
09373 !
09374 ! MOSS = 2. Compute structure from results of N + 1 calls to RES. ------
09375 100  DO 105 I = 1,N
09376 105    WK(LENWK1+I) = 0.0D0
09377 K = IPJAN
09378 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
09379 IER = -1
09380 IF (MITER .EQ. 1) IER = 1
09381 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IER)
09382 IF (IER .GT. 1) GOTO 370
09383 DO 130 J = 1,N
09384 CALL ADDA (NEQ, TN, Y, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), WK(LENWK1+1))
09385 YJ = Y(J)
09386 ERWT = 1.0D0/EWT(J)
09387 Y(J) = YJ + SIGN(ERWT,YJ)
09388 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, RTEM, IER)
09389 IF (IER .GT. 1) RETURN
09390 Y(J) = YJ
09391 DO 120 I = 1,N
09392 LJFO = LENWK1 + I
09393 IF (WK(LJFO) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 110
09394 WK(LJFO) = 0.0D0
09395 GOTO 115
09396 110      IF (RTEM(I) .EQ. SAVR(I)) GOTO 120
09397 115      IF (K .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09398 IWK(K) = I
09399 K = K + 1
09400 120      CONTINUE
09401 IWK(IPIAN+J) = K + 1 - IPJAN
09402 130    CONTINUE
09403 GOTO 240
09404 !
09405 ! MOSS = 3. Compute structure from the user's IA/JA and JAC routine. ---
09406 150  CONTINUE
09407 ! A dummy call to RES allows user to create temporaries for use in JAC.
09408 IER = 1
09409 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IER)
09410 IF (IER .GT. 1) GOTO 370
09411 DO 155 I = 1,N
09412 155    SAVR(I) = 0.0D0
09413 KNEW = IPJAN
09414 KAMIN = IA(1)
09415 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
09416 DO 190 J = 1,N
09417 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, S, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), SAVR)
09418 KAMAX = IA(J+1) - 1
09419 IF (KAMIN .GT. KAMAX) GOTO 170
09420 DO 160 K = KAMIN,KAMAX
09421 I = JA(K)
09422 SAVR(I) = 0.0D0
09423 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09424 IWK(KNEW) = I
09425 KNEW = KNEW + 1
09426 160      CONTINUE
09427 170    KAMIN = KAMAX + 1
09428 DO 180 I = 1,N
09429 IF (SAVR(I) .EQ. 0.0D0) GOTO 180
09430 SAVR(I) = 0.0D0
09431 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09432 IWK(KNEW) = I
09433 KNEW = KNEW + 1
09434 180      CONTINUE
09435 IWK(IPIAN+J) = KNEW + 1 - IPJAN
09436 190    CONTINUE
09437 GOTO 240
09438 !
09439 ! MOSS = 4. Compute structure from user's IA/JA and N + 1 RES calls. ---
09440 200  KNEW = IPJAN
09441 KAMIN = IA(1)
09442 IWK(IPIAN) = 1
09443 IER = -1
09444 IF (MITER .EQ. 1) IER = 1
09445 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IER)
09446 IF (IER .GT. 1) GOTO 370
09447 DO 235 J = 1,N
09448 YJ = Y(J)
09449 ERWT = 1.0D0/EWT(J)
09450 Y(J) = YJ + SIGN(ERWT,YJ)
09451 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, RTEM, IER)
09452 IF (IER .GT. 1) RETURN
09453 Y(J) = YJ
09454 KAMAX = IA(J+1) - 1
09455 IF (KAMIN .GT. KAMAX) GOTO 225
09456 DO 220 K = KAMIN,KAMAX
09457 I = JA(K)
09458 RTEM(I) = SAVR(I)
09459 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09460 IWK(KNEW) = I
09461 KNEW = KNEW + 1
09462 220      CONTINUE
09463 225    KAMIN = KAMAX + 1
09464 DO 230 I = 1,N
09465 IF (RTEM(I) .EQ. SAVR(I)) GOTO 230
09466 IF (KNEW .GT. LIWK) GOTO 310
09467 IWK(KNEW) = I
09468 KNEW = KNEW + 1
09469 230      CONTINUE
09470 IWK(IPIAN+J) = KNEW + 1 - IPJAN
09471 235    CONTINUE
09472 !
09473 240  CONTINUE
09474 IF (MOSS .EQ. 0 .OR. ISTATC .EQ. 3) GOTO 250
09475 ! If ISTATE = 0 or 1 and MOSS .ne. 0, restore Y from YH. ---------------
09476 DO 245 I = 1,N
09477 245    Y(I) = YH(I)
09478 250  NNZ = IWK(IPIAN+N) - 1
09479 IPPER = 0
09480 NGP = 0
09481 LENIGP = 0
09482 IPIGP = IPJAN + NNZ
09483 IF (MITER .NE. 2) GOTO 260
09484 !
09485 ! Compute grouping of column indices (MITER = 2). ----------------------
09486 !
09487 MAXG = NP1
09488 IPJGP = IPJAN + NNZ
09489 IBJGP = IPJGP - 1
09490 IPIGP = IPJGP + N
09491 IPTT1 = IPIGP + NP1
09492 IPTT2 = IPTT1 + N
09493 LREQ = IPTT2 + N - 1
09494 IF (LREQ .GT. LIWK) GOTO 320
09495 CALL JGROUP (N, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), MAXG, NGP, IWK(IPIGP), IWK(IPJGP), IWK(IPTT1), IWK(IPTT2), IER)
09496 IF (IER .NE. 0) GOTO 320
09497 LENIGP = NGP + 1
09498 !
09499 ! Compute new ordering of rows/columns of Jacobian. --------------------
09500 260  IPR = IPIGP + LENIGP
09501 IPC = IPR
09502 IPIC = IPC + N
09503 IPISP = IPIC + N
09504 IPRSP = (IPISP-2)/LRAT + 2
09505 IESP = LENWK + 1 - IPRSP
09506 IF (IESP .LT. 0) GOTO 330
09507 IBR = IPR - 1
09508 DO 270 I = 1,N
09509 270    IWK(IBR+I) = I
09510 NSP = LIWK + 1 - IPISP
09511 CALL ODRV(N, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), WK, IWK(IPR), IWK(IPIC), NSP, IWK(IPISP), 1, IYS)
09512 IF (IYS .EQ. 11*N+1) GOTO 340
09513 IF (IYS .NE. 0) GOTO 330
09514 !
09515 ! Reorder JAN and do symbolic LU factorization of matrix. --------------
09516 IPA = LENWK + 1 - NNZ
09517 NSP = IPA - IPRSP
09518 LREQ = MAX(12*N/LRAT, 6*N/LRAT+2*N+NNZ) + 3
09519 LREQ = LREQ + IPRSP - 1 + NNZ
09520 IF (LREQ .GT. LENWK) GOTO 350
09521 IBA = IPA - 1
09522 DO 280 I = 1,NNZ
09523 280    WK(IBA+I) = 0.0D0
09524 IPISP = LRAT*(IPRSP - 1) + 1
09525 CALL CDRV(N,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN), WK(IPA),WK(IPA),WK(IPA),NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,5,IYS)
09526 LREQ = LENWK - IESP
09527 IF (IYS .EQ. 10*N+1) GOTO 350
09528 IF (IYS .NE. 0) GOTO 360
09529 IPIL = IPISP
09530 IPIU = IPIL + 2*N + 1
09531 NZU = IWK(IPIL+N) - IWK(IPIL)
09532 NZL = IWK(IPIU+N) - IWK(IPIU)
09533 IF (LRAT .GT. 1) GOTO 290
09534 CALL ADJLR (N, IWK(IPISP), LDIF)
09535 LREQ = LREQ + LDIF
09536 290  CONTINUE
09537 IF (LRAT .EQ. 2 .AND. NNZ .EQ. N) LREQ = LREQ + 1
09538 NSP = NSP + LREQ - LENWK
09539 IPA = LREQ + 1 - NNZ
09540 IBA = IPA - 1
09541 IPPER = 0
09542 RETURN
09543 !
09544 310  IPPER = -1
09545 LREQ = 2 + (2*N + 1)/LRAT
09546 LREQ = MAX(LENWK+1,LREQ)
09547 RETURN
09548 !
09549 320  IPPER = -2
09550 LREQ = (LREQ - 1)/LRAT + 1
09551 RETURN
09552 !
09553 330  IPPER = -3
09554 CALL CNTNZU (N, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), NZSUT)
09555 LREQ = LENWK - IESP + (3*N + 4*NZSUT - 1)/LRAT + 1
09556 RETURN
09557 !
09558 340  IPPER = -4
09559 RETURN
09560 !
09561 350  IPPER =  -5
09562 RETURN
09563 !
09564 360  IPPER = -6
09565 LREQ = LENWK
09566 RETURN
09567 !
09568 370  IPPER = -IER - 5
09569 LREQ = 2 + (2*N + 1)/LRAT
09570 RETURN
09571 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPREPI ----------------------
09572 END
09573 
09574 SUBROUTINE DAINVGS (NEQ, T, Y, WK, IWK, TEM, YDOT, IER, RES, ADDA)
09575 EXTERNAL RES, ADDA
09576 INTEGER NEQ, IWK, IER
09577 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP, IPA
