09578 INTEGER LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09579 INTEGER I, IMUL, J, K, KMIN, KMAX
09580 DOUBLE PRECISION T, Y, WK, TEM, YDOT
09581 DOUBLE PRECISION RLSS
09582 DIMENSION Y(*), WK(*), IWK(*), TEM(*), YDOT(*)
09583 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, &
09584 IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09585 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09586 ! This subroutine computes the initial value of the vector YDOT
09587 ! satisfying
09588 !     A * YDOT = g(t,y)
09589 ! when A is nonsingular.  It is called by DLSODIS for initialization
09590 ! only, when ISTATE = 0.  The matrix A is subjected to LU
09591 ! decomposition in CDRV.  Then the system A*YDOT = g(t,y) is solved
09592 ! in CDRV.
09593 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
09594 ! with DAINVGS uses the following:
09595 ! Y     = array of initial values.
09596 ! WK    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains A and
09597 !         its LU decomposition.  The LU decomposition is not entirely
09598 !         sparse unless the structure of the matrix A is identical to
09599 !         the structure of the Jacobian matrix dr/dy.
09600 !         Storage of matrix elements starts at WK(3).
09601 !         WK(1) = SQRT(UROUND), not used here.
09602 ! IWK   = integer work space for matrix-related data, assumed to
09603 !         be equivalenced to WK.  In addition, WK(IPRSP) and WK(IPISP)
09604 !         are assumed to have identical locations.
09605 ! TEM   = vector of work space of length N (ACOR in DSTODI).
09606 ! YDOT  = output vector containing the initial dy/dt. YDOT(i) contains
09607 !         dy(i)/dt when the matrix A is non-singular.
09608 ! IER   = output error flag with the following values and meanings:
09609 !       = 0  if DAINVGS was successful.
09610 !       = 1  if the A-matrix was found to be singular.
09611 !       = 2  if RES returned an error flag IRES = IER = 2.
09612 !       = 3  if RES returned an error flag IRES = IER = 3.
09613 !       = 4  if insufficient storage for CDRV (should not occur here).
09614 !       = 5  if other error found in CDRV (should not occur here).
09615 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09616 !
09617 DO 10 I = 1,NNZ
09618 10     WK(IBA+I) = 0.0D0
09619 !
09620 IER = 1
09621 CALL RES (NEQ, T, Y, WK(IPA), YDOT, IER)
09622 IF (IER .GT. 1) RETURN
09623 !
09624 KMIN = IWK(IPIAN)
09625 DO 30 J = 1,NEQ
09626 KMAX = IWK(IPIAN+J) - 1
09627 DO 15 K = KMIN,KMAX
09628 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
09629 15       TEM(I) = 0.0D0
09630 CALL ADDA (NEQ, T, Y, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), TEM)
09631 DO 20 K = KMIN,KMAX
09632 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
09633 20       WK(IBA+K) = TEM(I)
09634 KMIN = KMAX + 1
09635 30   CONTINUE
09636 NLU = NLU + 1
09637 IER = 0
09638 DO 40 I = 1,NEQ
09639 40     TEM(I) = 0.0D0
09640 !
09641 ! Numerical factorization of matrix A. ---------------------------------
09642 CALL CDRV (NEQ,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN), WK(IPA),TEM,TEM,NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,2,IYS)
09643 IF (IYS .EQ. 0) GOTO 50
09644 IMUL = (IYS - 1)/NEQ
09645 IER = 5
09646 IF (IMUL .EQ. 8) IER = 1
09647 IF (IMUL .EQ. 10) IER = 4
09648 RETURN
09649 !
09650 ! Solution of the linear system. ---------------------------------------
09651 50   CALL CDRV (NEQ,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN), WK(IPA),YDOT,YDOT,NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,4,IYS)
09652 IF (IYS .NE. 0) IER = 5
09653 RETURN
09654 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DAINVGS ---------------------
09655 END
09656 
09657 SUBROUTINE DPRJIS (NEQ, Y, YH, NYH, EWT, RTEM, SAVR, S, WK, IWK, RES, JAC, ADDA)
09658 EXTERNAL RES, JAC, ADDA
09659 INTEGER NEQ, NYH, IWK
09660 DOUBLE PRECISION Y, YH, EWT, RTEM, SAVR, S, WK
09661 DIMENSION NEQ(*), Y(*), YH(NYH,*), EWT(*), RTEM(*), S(*), SAVR(*), WK(*), IWK(*)
09662 INTEGER IOWND, IOWNS, ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM
09663 INTEGER LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
09664 INTEGER IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, IPISP, IPRSP
09665 INTEGER IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09666 DOUBLE PRECISION ROWNS, CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND
09667 DOUBLE PRECISION RLSS
09668 COMMON /DLS001/ ROWNS(209), CCMAX, EL0, H, HMIN, HMXI, HU, RC, TN, UROUND, IOWND(6), IOWNS(6), ICF, IERPJ, IERSL, JCUR, &
09669 JSTART, KFLAG, L, LYH, LEWT, LACOR, LSAVF, LWM, LIWM, METH, MITER, MAXORD, MAXCOR, MSBP, MXNCF, N, NQ, NST, NFE, NJE, NQU
09670 COMMON /DLSS01/ RLSS(6), IPLOST, IESP, ISTATC, IYS, IBA, IBIAN, IBJAN, IBJGP, IPIAN, IPJAN, IPJGP, IPIGP, IPR, IPC, IPIC, &
09671 IPISP, IPRSP, IPA, LENYH, LENYHM, LENWK, LREQ, LRAT, LREST, LWMIN, MOSS, MSBJ, NSLJ, NGP, NLU, NNZ, NSP, NZL, NZU
09672 INTEGER I, IMUL, IRES, J, JJ, JMAX, JMIN, K, KMAX, KMIN, NG
09673 DOUBLE PRECISION CON, FAC, HL0, R, SRUR
09674 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09675 ! DPRJIS is called to compute and process the matrix
09676 ! P = A - H*EL(1)*J, where J is an approximation to the Jacobian dr/dy,
09677 ! where r = g(t,y) - A(t,y)*s.  J is computed by columns, either by
09678 ! the user-supplied routine JAC if MITER = 1, or by finite differencing
09679 ! if MITER = 2.  J is stored in WK, rescaled, and ADDA is called to
09680 ! generate P.  The matrix P is subjected to LU decomposition in CDRV.
09681 ! P and its LU decomposition are stored separately in WK.
09682 !
09683 ! In addition to variables described previously, communication
09684 ! with DPRJIS uses the following:
09685 ! Y     = array containing predicted values on entry.
09686 ! RTEM  = work array of length N (ACOR in DSTODI).
09687 ! SAVR  = array containing r evaluated at predicted y. On output it
09688 !         contains the residual evaluated at current values of t and y.
09689 ! S     = array containing predicted values of dy/dt (SAVF in DSTODI).
09690 ! WK    = real work space for matrices.  On output it contains P and
09691 !         its sparse LU decomposition.  Storage of matrix elements
09692 !         starts at WK(3).
09693 !         WK also contains the following matrix-related data.
09694 !         WK(1) = SQRT(UROUND), used in numerical Jacobian increments.
09695 ! IWK   = integer work space for matrix-related data, assumed to be
09696 !         equivalenced to WK.  In addition,  WK(IPRSP) and IWK(IPISP)
09697 !         are assumed to have identical locations.
09698 ! EL0   = EL(1) (input).
09699 ! IERPJ = output error flag (in COMMON).
09700 !         =  0 if no error.
09701 !         =  1 if zero pivot found in CDRV.
09702 !         = IRES (= 2 or 3) if RES returned IRES = 2 or 3.
09703 !         = -1 if insufficient storage for CDRV (should not occur).
09704 !         = -2 if other error found in CDRV (should not occur here).
09705 ! JCUR  = output flag = 1 to indicate that the Jacobian matrix
09706 !         (or approximation) is now current.
09707 ! This routine also uses other variables in Common.
09708 !-----------------------------------------------------------------------
09709 HL0 = H*EL0
09710 CON = -HL0
09711 JCUR = 1
09712 NJE = NJE + 1
09713 GOTO (100, 200), MITER
09714 !
09715 ! If MITER = 1, call RES, then call JAC and ADDA for each column. ------
09716 100  IRES = 1
09717 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
09718 NFE = NFE + 1
09719 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
09720 KMIN = IWK(IPIAN)
09721 DO 130 J = 1,N
09722 KMAX = IWK(IPIAN+J)-1
09723 DO 110 I = 1,N
09724 110      RTEM(I) = 0.0D0
09725 CALL JAC (NEQ, TN, Y, S, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), RTEM)
09726 DO 120 I = 1,N
09727 120      RTEM(I) = RTEM(I)*CON
09728 CALL ADDA (NEQ, TN, Y, J, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), RTEM)
09729 DO 125 K = KMIN,KMAX
09730 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
09731 WK(IBA+K) = RTEM(I)
09732 125      CONTINUE
09733 KMIN = KMAX + 1
09734 130    CONTINUE
09735 GOTO 290
09736 !
09737 ! If MITER = 2, make NGP + 1 calls to RES to approximate J and P. ------
09738 200  CONTINUE
09739 IRES = -1
09740 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
09741 NFE = NFE + 1
09742 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
09743 SRUR = WK(1)
09744 JMIN = IWK(IPIGP)
09745 DO 240 NG = 1,NGP
09746 JMAX = IWK(IPIGP+NG) - 1
09747 DO 210 J = JMIN,JMAX
09748 JJ = IWK(IBJGP+J)
09749 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(Y(JJ)),0.01D0/EWT(JJ))
09750 210      Y(JJ) = Y(JJ) + R
09751 CALL RES (NEQ,TN,Y,S,RTEM,IRES)
09752 NFE = NFE + 1
09753 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
09754 DO 230 J = JMIN,JMAX
09755 JJ = IWK(IBJGP+J)
09756 Y(JJ) = YH(JJ,1)
09757 R = MAX(SRUR*ABS(Y(JJ)),0.01D0/EWT(JJ))
09758 FAC = -HL0/R
09759 KMIN = IWK(IBIAN+JJ)
09760 KMAX = IWK(IBIAN+JJ+1) - 1
09761 DO 220 K = KMIN,KMAX
09762 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
09763 RTEM(I) = (RTEM(I) - SAVR(I))*FAC
09764 220        CONTINUE
09765 CALL ADDA (NEQ, TN, Y, JJ, IWK(IPIAN), IWK(IPJAN), RTEM)
09766 DO 225 K = KMIN,KMAX
09767 I = IWK(IBJAN+K)
09768 WK(IBA+K) = RTEM(I)
09769 225      CONTINUE
09770 230      CONTINUE
09771 JMIN = JMAX + 1
09772 240    CONTINUE
09773 IRES = 1
09774 CALL RES (NEQ, TN, Y, S, SAVR, IRES)
09775 NFE = NFE + 1
09776 IF (IRES .GT. 1) GOTO 600
09777 !
09778 ! Do numerical factorization of P matrix. ------------------------------
09779 290  NLU = NLU + 1
09780 IERPJ = 0
09781 DO 295 I = 1,N
09782 295    RTEM(I) = 0.0D0
09783 CALL CDRV (N,IWK(IPR),IWK(IPC),IWK(IPIC),IWK(IPIAN),IWK(IPJAN), WK(IPA),RTEM,RTEM,NSP,IWK(IPISP),WK(IPRSP),IESP,2,IYS)
09784 IF (IYS .EQ. 0) RETURN
09785 IMUL = (IYS - 1)/N
09786 IERPJ = -2
09787 IF (IMUL .EQ. 8) IERPJ = 1
09788 IF (IMUL .EQ. 10) IERPJ = -1
09789 RETURN
09790 ! Error return for IRES = 2 or IRES = 3 return from RES. ---------------
09791 600  IERPJ = IRES
09792 RETURN
09793 !----------------------- End of Subroutine DPRJIS ----------------------
09794 END
